    '（可选）AWS IAM Role ARN，格式 arn:aws:iam::账号ID:role/角色名。\n新版 SP-API 不再需要。',
  // 状态列（自定义 key）
  col_preview_status:
    'Amazon 预览结果。\n✅ 通过 = 可以提交\n❌ 失败 = 有字段不符合 Amazon 要求\n⚪ 未运行 = 点「5 预览验证」先跑一次',
  col_submit_status:
    '正式提交结果。\n• 提交中 = 已发出，等 Amazon 处理\n• 成功 = 已生成 ASIN\n• 失败 = 被 Amazon 拒绝，看错误原因',
  col_submission_id:
    'Amazon 给这次提交的回执号。\n出问题让客服查这个号最快定位。',
  col_route:
    '上架路径：\n• putListingsItem = 逐条上架（小批量）\n• JSON_LISTINGS_FEED = 批量 Feed（>1500 条自动切换）',
  col_final_status:
    'Amazon 后台最终的商品状态：\n• ACCEPTED = 已接收\n• DISCOVERABLE = 可被搜到\n• SUPPRESSED = 被压制（需修复）',
  col_listing_issues:
    'Amazon 后台报出的问题数。\n>0 说明上架后还有合规/字段问题需要修。',
};

function tipFor(key) {
  if (!FIELD_TOOLTIPS_ZH || !FIELD_TOOLTIPS_ZH[key]) return '';
  return ` <span class="term-help" data-tip="${key}" tabindex="0" role="button" aria-label="术语解释">?</span>`;
}

(function setupTermTooltips() {
  let tipEl = null;
  let activeTrigger = null;

  function ensureEl() {
    if (!tipEl) {
      tipEl = document.createElement('div');
      tipEl.className = 'term-help-pop';
      tipEl.setAttribute('role', 'tooltip');
      document.body.appendChild(tipEl);
    }
    return tipEl;
  }

  function show(trigger) {
    const key = trigger.getAttribute('data-tip');
    const text = FIELD_TOOLTIPS_ZH[key];
    if (!text) return;
    const el = ensureEl();
    el.textContent = text;
    el.style.display = 'block';
    el.style.visibility = 'hidden';
    el.classList.remove('show');
    const r = trigger.getBoundingClientRect();
    const tw = el.offsetWidth;
    const th = el.offsetHeight;
    let left = r.left + r.width / 2 - tw / 2;
    if (left < 8) left = 8;
    if (left + tw > window.innerWidth - 8) left = window.innerWidth - 8 - tw;
    let top = r.top - th - 8;
    if (top < 8) top = r.bottom + 8;
    el.style.left = left + 'px';
    el.style.top = top + 'px';
    el.style.visibility = 'visible';
    el.classList.add('show');
    activeTrigger = trigger;
  }

  function hide() {
    if (tipEl) {
      tipEl.classList.remove('show');
      tipEl.style.display = 'none';
    }
    activeTrigger = null;
  }

  document.addEventListener('mouseover', e => {
    const t = e.target.closest && e.target.closest('.term-help');
    if (t && t !== activeTrigger) show(t);
  });
  document.addEventListener('mouseout', e => {
    const t = e.target.closest && e.target.closest('.term-help');
    if (!t) return;
    if (e.relatedTarget && t.contains(e.relatedTarget)) return;
    hide();
  });
  document.addEventListener('focusin', e => {
    if (e.target.classList && e.target.classList.contains('term-help')) show(e.target);
  });
  document.addEventListener('focusout', e => {
    if (e.target.classList && e.target.classList.contains('term-help')) hide();
  });
  document.addEventListener('keydown', e => { if (e.key === 'Escape') hide(); });
  document.addEventListener('scroll', hide, true);
  window.addEventListener('resize', hide);
})();

// ===== 3. i18n Functions =====
function t(key) { return (i18n[lang] && i18n[lang][key]) || key; }
function setLanguage(nextLang) {
  lang = nextLang === 'en' ? 'en' : 'zh';
  document.getElementById('langText').textContent = lang === 'zh' ? '中文' : 'EN';
  applyLang();
}
function applyLang() {
  document.querySelectorAll('[data-t]').forEach(el => {
    const k = el.getAttribute('data-t');
    if (i18n[lang][k]) el.textContent = i18n[lang][k];
  });
  document.querySelectorAll('[data-t-placeholder]').forEach(el => {
    const k = el.getAttribute('data-t-placeholder');
    if (i18n[lang][k]) el.placeholder = i18n[lang][k];
  });
  updateTaskCenterCollapseUi();
}
function toggleLang() {
  setLanguage(lang === 'zh' ? 'en' : 'zh');
}

function updateTaskCenterCollapseUi() {
  const grid = document.getElementById('taskCenterGrid');
  const toggleBtn = document.getElementById('taskCenterToggleBtn');
  if (grid) grid.classList.toggle('collapsed', taskCenterCollapsed);
  if (toggleBtn) toggleBtn.textContent = taskCenterCollapsed
    ? (lang === 'zh' ? '展开' : 'Expand')
    : (lang === 'zh' ? '收起' : 'Collapse');
}

function setTaskCenterCollapsed(nextState) {
  taskCenterCollapsed = !!nextState;
  updateTaskCenterCollapseUi();
}

function toggleTaskCenter() {
  setTaskCenterCollapsed(!taskCenterCollapsed);
}

function formatSubmissionRoute(route) {
  if (route === 'existing_asin') return '匹配已有 ASIN';
  if (route === 'new_listing') return '新建目录';
  return '待判定';
}

function formatSubmitStatusLabel(status) {
  const text = String(status || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  if (!text || text === 'PENDING') return '未提交';
  if (text === 'ACCEPTED') return '已接受';
  if (text === 'PREVIEW_BLOCKED') return '预览阻断';
  if (text === 'VALID') return '预览通过';
  if (text === 'INVALID') return '预览失败';
  if (text === 'ERROR') return '提交异常';
  return text;
}

function compactMiddle(value, left = 8, right = 6) {
  const text = String(value || '').trim();
  if (!text || text.length <= left + right + 3) return text;
  return `${text.slice(0, left)}...${text.slice(-right)}`;
}

function getAccountMeta(accountId = '') {
  const account = amazonAccounts.find(item => item && item.seller_id === accountId)
    || amazonAccounts.find(item => item && item.is_default)
    || amazonAccounts[0]
    || null;
  if (!account) return null;
  return {
    id: account.seller_id || '',
    name: account.name || account.seller_id || '',
    site: account.marketplace_name || account.marketplace_id || '-',
  };
}

function formatExecutionModeLabel(mode) {
  if (mode === 'submit') return '正式提交';
  if (mode === 'preview') return '预览验证';
  if (mode === 'validate') return '批量校验';
  if (mode === 'rewrite') return '批量AI文案';
  if (mode === 'image') return '批量AI生图';
  if (mode === 'export') return '导出';
  return '批量处理';
}

function formatFinalListingStatus(status) {
  const map = {
    discoverable: '已可发现',
    suppressed: '已抑制',
    asin_linked: '已关联 ASIN',
    processing: '处理中',
    pending: '待回写',
  };
  return map[status] || '待判定';
}

// ===== 4. Navigation =====
function showPage(page) {
  closeDrawer();
  document.querySelectorAll('.page').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.s-item').forEach(s => s.classList.remove('active'));
  const pageEl = document.getElementById('page-' + page);
  const navEl = document.querySelector(`[data-page="${page}"]`);
  if (pageEl) pageEl.classList.add('active');
  if (navEl) navEl.classList.add('active');
  document.getElementById('pageTitle').textContent = t(page);
  if (page === 'settings') {
    showSettingsSection(settingsActiveSection || 'ai');
    loadConfig();
    loadAccounts();
    refreshSetupStatus({ showFirstRun: false });
  }
  closeMobileSidebar();
}

function showSettingsSection(section) {
  const allowed = ['ai', 'amazon', 'self_check', 'advanced'];
  const next = allowed.includes(section) ? section : 'ai';
  settingsActiveSection = next;
  localStorage.setItem('amazon28_settingsSection', next);
  document.querySelectorAll('[data-settings-section]').forEach(card => {
    card.classList.toggle('is-hidden', card.getAttribute('data-settings-section') !== next);
  });
  document.querySelectorAll('[data-settings-tab]').forEach(tab => {
    tab.classList.toggle('active', tab.getAttribute('data-settings-tab') === next);
  });
}

function isMobileViewport() {
  return window.innerWidth <= 768;
}
function toggleSidebar() {
  const sidebar = document.getElementById('sidebar');
  const backdrop = document.getElementById('sidebarBackdrop');
  if (isMobileViewport()) {
    const willOpen = !sidebar.classList.contains('mobile-open');
    sidebar.classList.remove('collapsed');
    sidebar.classList.toggle('mobile-open', willOpen);
    if (backdrop) backdrop.classList.toggle('show', willOpen);
    return;
  }
  sidebar.classList.toggle('collapsed');
}
function closeMobileSidebar() {
  const sidebar = document.getElementById('sidebar');
  const backdrop = document.getElementById('sidebarBackdrop');
  if (sidebar) sidebar.classList.remove('mobile-open');
  if (backdrop) backdrop.classList.remove('show');
}

// ===== 5. Utility =====
function escHtml(s) {
  if (!s) return '';
  const d = document.createElement('div');
  d.textContent = String(s);
  return d.innerHTML;
}

function setupStatusLabel(status) {
  const map = {
    done: ['已完成', 'done'],
    todo: ['待完成', 'todo'],
    blocked: ['需处理', 'blocked'],
  };
  return map[status] || ['待完成', 'todo'];
}

function renderSetupStepCard(step, options = {}) {
  const [label, tone] = setupStatusLabel(step.status);
  const action = step.action ? ` setupAction="${escHtml(step.action)}"` : '';
  const button = step.button && !options.readonly
    ? `<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="runSetupAction('${escHtml(step.action || '')}')">${escHtml(step.button)}</button>`
    : '';
  return `<div class="setup-step-card ${tone}"${action}>
    <div class="setup-step-top">
      <div class="setup-step-title">${escHtml(step.title || '')}</div>
      <span class="setup-step-badge ${tone}">${label}</span>
    </div>
    <div class="setup-step-message">${escHtml(step.message || '')}</div>
    ${button}
  </div>`;
}

function renderSetupStatus(data) {
  setupStatus = data || null;
  setupNextAction = data?.next_step?.action || '';

  const guide = document.getElementById('setupGuideCard');
  const guideSteps = document.getElementById('setupGuideSteps');
  const guideSummary = document.getElementById('setupGuideSummary');
  const primary = document.getElementById('setupPrimaryAction');
  const panel = document.getElementById('setupStatusGrid');
  const steps = data?.steps || [];

  if (panel) {
    panel.innerHTML = steps.map(step => renderSetupStepCard(step)).join('');
  }

  if (guide && guideSteps && guideSummary) {
    const hiddenForSession = sessionStorage.getItem('amazon28_setup_hidden') === '1';
    if (!data || data.ready || hiddenForSession) {
      guide.style.display = 'none';
    } else {
      guide.style.display = '';
      guideSummary.textContent = data.next_step
        ? `下一步：${data.next_step.title}。${data.next_step.message || ''}`
        : '基础配置已完成，可以开始处理商品。';
      guideSteps.innerHTML = steps.map(step => renderSetupStepCard(step, { readonly: true })).join('');
      if (primary) primary.textContent = data.next_step?.button || '继续下一步';
    }
  }
  renderCustomerFlow();
  enableToolbar(products.length > 0);
}

async function refreshSetupStatus(options = {}) {
  try {
    const response = await fetch('/api/setup-status');
    const data = await response.json();
    if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
    renderSetupStatus(data);
    if (options.manual) showToast(data.ready ? 'success' : 'info', data.ready ? '配置已就绪' : '已刷新配置状态，请按提示继续');
    if (options.showFirstRun !== false) maybeShowFirstRunModal(data);
    return data;
  } catch (e) {
    if (options.manual) showToast('error', '读取配置状态失败: ' + e.message);
    return null;
  }
}

function maybeShowFirstRunModal(data) {
  if (!data || data.ready || !data.needs_setup) return;
  if (sessionStorage.getItem('amazon28_first_run_seen') === '1') return;
  sessionStorage.setItem('amazon28_first_run_seen', '1');
  const steps = data.steps || [];
  showModal('第一次使用：先完成 3 件事', `
    <div class="customer-quick-start">
      <div class="quick-start-step">
        <strong>1. 先填 AI 接口</strong>
        <p>不填 AI Key，批量文案和生图会失败。Base URL 固定填 https://api.kk666.best；填完后点“测试连接”。</p>
      </div>
      <div class="quick-start-step">
        <strong>2. 再填 Amazon 账号</strong>
        <p>不填 Seller ID / LWA / Refresh Token，就不能做 Amazon 预览和正式提交。</p>
      </div>
      <div class="quick-start-step">
        <strong>3. 最后导入 Excel 或生成官方模板</strong>
        <p>导入后系统会自动检查字段，能做的按钮才继续往下走。</p>
      </div>
      <div class="setup-status-grid">${steps.map(step => renderSetupStepCard(step, { readonly: true })).join('')}</div>
    </div>
  `);
  document.getElementById('modalFooter').innerHTML = `
    <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="closeModal(); runSetupPrimaryAction()">按提示继续</button>
    <button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="closeModal(); openCustomerQuickStart()">看详细说明</button>
    <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="closeModal()">稍后再说</button>`;
}

function dismissSetupGuide() {
  sessionStorage.setItem('amazon28_setup_hidden', '1');
  const guide = document.getElementById('setupGuideCard');
  if (guide) guide.style.display = 'none';
}

function runSetupPrimaryAction() {
  runSetupAction(setupNextAction || setupStatus?.next_step?.action || 'settings_ai');
}

function scrollToElementLater(selector) {
  setTimeout(() => {
    const el = document.querySelector(selector);
    if (el) el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
  }, 160);
}

function runSetupAction(action) {
  if (action === 'settings_ai') {
    showPage('settings');
    showSettingsSection('ai');
    scrollToElementLater('#cfgTextApiKey');
    setTimeout(() => document.getElementById('cfgTextApiKey')?.focus(), 220);
    return;
  }
  if (action === 'settings_account') {
    showPage('settings');
    showSettingsSection('amazon');
    scrollToElementLater('#accountTable');
    return;
  }
  if (action === 'add_account') {
    showPage('settings');
    showSettingsSection('amazon');
    setTimeout(showAddAccount, 180);
    return;
  }
  if (action === 'upload') {
    document.getElementById('fileInput')?.click();
    return;
  }
  if (action === 'self_check') {
    showPage('settings');
    showSettingsSection('self_check');
    scrollToElementLater('#selfCheckResults');
    setTimeout(runSelfCheck, 220);
    return;
  }
  showPage('settings');
}

function openCustomerQuickStart() {
  showModal('客户版操作说明', `
    <div class="customer-quick-start">
      <div class="quick-start-step">
        <strong>只双击一个启动文件</strong>
        <p>Windows 双击“启动亚马逊2.8.bat”，Mac 双击“启动亚马逊2.8.command”。不要直接点 exe，不要在压缩包里运行。</p>
      </div>
      <div class="quick-start-step">
        <strong>打开后先去“设置”</strong>
        <p>先点“一键恢复推荐”，Base URL 固定用 https://api.kk666.best，再粘贴文字/图片 Key，最后添加 Amazon 账号。</p>
      </div>
      <div class="quick-start-step">
        <strong>处理顺序固定</strong>
        <p>导入 Excel -> AI 文案/生图 -> 校验/缺项诊断 -> Amazon 预览 -> 正式提交。不要跳过预览直接提交。</p>
      </div>
      <div class="quick-start-step">
        <strong>出问题先点一键自检</strong>
        <p>自检会告诉你是 AI、Amazon 账号、输出目录还是文件格式问题，直接把结果截图发给技术支持即可。</p>
      </div>
    </div>
  `);
  document.getElementById('modalFooter').innerHTML = `
    <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="closeModal(); runSetupPrimaryAction()">回到下一步</button>
    <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="closeModal()">关闭</button>`;
}

function getCustomerFlowSnapshot() {
  const realProducts = products.filter(product => product.parentage_level !== 'parent' && !isRowDisabled(product));
  const total = realProducts.length;
  const processed = realProducts.filter(product => ['completed', 'done'].includes(String(product.ai_status || '').toLowerCase())).length;
  const previewPassed = realProducts.filter(product => isPreviewValidForSelectedAccount(product)).length;
  const submitted = realProducts.filter(product => isAlreadySubmittedProduct(product)).length;
  const blocking = realProducts.filter(product => {
    const hasLocalErrors = Array.isArray(product._validErrors) && product._validErrors.length > 0;
    return hasLocalErrors || hasTemplateBlockingIssues(product);
  }).length;
  return {
    aiReady: !!setupStatus?.ai?.ready,
    amazonReady: !!setupStatus?.amazon?.ready,
    hasFile: !!currentFile && total > 0,
    total,
    processed,
    previewPassed,
    submitted,
    blocking,
  };
}

function resolveCustomerFlow(snapshot = getCustomerFlowSnapshot()) {
  const steps = [
    {
      id: 'setup',
      name: '先配置',
      desc: snapshot.aiReady && snapshot.amazonReady ? 'AI 和账号已就绪' : '先去设置页填 Key 和账号',
      action: snapshot.aiReady ? 'add_account' : 'settings_ai',
      done: snapshot.aiReady && snapshot.amazonReady,
    },
    {
      id: 'import',
      name: '导入表格',
      desc: snapshot.hasFile ? `已载入 ${snapshot.total} 个商品` : '导入 Excel 或生成官方模板',
      action: 'upload',
      done: snapshot.hasFile,
    },
    {
      id: 'ai',
      name: '跑 AI',
      desc: snapshot.hasFile ? `${snapshot.processed}/${snapshot.total} 已处理` : '先导入商品表',
      action: 'batch_ai',
      done: snapshot.hasFile && snapshot.total > 0 && snapshot.processed >= snapshot.total,
    },
    {
      id: 'check',
      name: '检查问题',
      desc: snapshot.hasFile ? (snapshot.blocking ? `还有 ${snapshot.blocking} 个问题` : '校验/诊断无阻断') : '先导入商品表',
      action: 'check',
      done: snapshot.hasFile && snapshot.total > 0 && snapshot.blocking === 0,
    },
    {
      id: 'preview',
      name: '先预览',
      desc: snapshot.hasFile ? `${snapshot.previewPassed}/${snapshot.total} 预览通过` : '提交前必须预览',
      action: 'preview',
      done: snapshot.hasFile && snapshot.total > 0 && snapshot.previewPassed >= snapshot.total,
    },
    {
      id: 'submit',
      name: '再提交',
      desc: snapshot.submitted ? `已提交 ${snapshot.submitted} 个` : '最后一步，不要提前点',
      action: 'submit',
      done: snapshot.hasFile && snapshot.total > 0 && snapshot.submitted >= snapshot.total,
    },
  ];

  let activeIndex = steps.findIndex(step => !step.done);
  if (activeIndex < 0) activeIndex = steps.length - 1;
  steps.forEach((step, index) => {
    step.state = step.done ? 'done' : (index === activeIndex ? 'active' : 'locked');
  });
  const active = steps[activeIndex];
  return { steps, active };
}

function renderCustomerFlow() {
  const container = document.getElementById('customerFlowCard');
  const stepsEl = document.getElementById('customerFlowSteps');
  const titleEl = document.getElementById('customerFlowTitle');
  const hintEl = document.getElementById('customerFlowHint');
  const btn = document.getElementById('customerFlowPrimaryBtn');
  const heroTitle = document.getElementById('customerNextStepTitle');
  const heroDesc = document.getElementById('customerNextStepDesc');
  const heroBtn = document.getElementById('customerFlowHeroBtn');
  if (!container || !stepsEl) return;

  const snapshot = getCustomerFlowSnapshot();
  const flow = resolveCustomerFlow(snapshot);
  customerFlowNextAction = flow.active?.action || '';
  stepsEl.innerHTML = flow.steps.map((step, idx) => `<div class="customer-flow-step ${step.state}">
    <div class="customer-flow-number">${step.state === 'done' ? '✓' : idx + 1}</div>
    <div class="customer-flow-name">${escHtml(step.name)}</div>
    <div class="customer-flow-desc">${escHtml(step.desc)}</div>
  </div>`).join('');

  const titleMap = {
    setup: '先别处理商品，先把配置填完整',
    import: '下一步：导入客户 Excel',
    ai: '下一步：批量跑 AI 文案/图片',
    check: '下一步：检查并修掉阻断项',
    preview: '下一步：先做 Amazon 预览',
    submit: '下一步：确认预览通过后再正式提交',
  };
  const buttonMap = {
    setup: snapshot.aiReady ? '添加 Amazon 账号' : '去设置 AI',
    import: '导入 Excel',
    ai: '开始批量 AI',
    check: '开始校验',
    preview: '先跑预览',
    submit: '正式提交',
  };
  const descMap = {
    setup: snapshot.aiReady
      ? 'AI 已经可以用了，现在只差 Amazon 账号。点按钮后填 Seller ID、LWA Client ID/Secret、Refresh Token。'
      : '先把 AI Key 填好。点按钮后直接进入 AI 设置页，客户只需要点“一键恢复推荐”再粘贴 Key。',
    import: '配置完成后先导入 Excel。没有真实表也可以先生成示例 Excel，确认软件能正常跑通。',
    ai: '表格已导入，先让系统批量生成/改写文案。不要先提交，未处理内容更容易被 Amazon 拒绝。',
    check: 'AI 处理后先跑校验/缺项诊断，把红色阻断项修掉，再进入 Amazon 预览。',
    preview: '正式提交前必须先预览。预览会发现 Amazon 后台字段/权限问题，但不会真正上架。',
    submit: '只有最近同账号同站点预览通过的 SKU 才能提交。提交前还会再弹一次确认。',
  };
  if (titleEl) titleEl.textContent = titleMap[flow.active?.id] || '按顺序做，不要跳步';
  if (hintEl) hintEl.textContent = flow.active?.desc || '系统会根据当前状态告诉你下一步该点什么。';
  if (btn) btn.textContent = buttonMap[flow.active?.id] || '按推荐执行';
  if (heroTitle) heroTitle.textContent = titleMap[flow.active?.id] || '按推荐执行下一步';
  if (heroDesc) heroDesc.textContent = descMap[flow.active?.id] || '不要跳步，系统会一直把最安全的下一步放在这里。';
  if (heroBtn) heroBtn.textContent = buttonMap[flow.active?.id] || '按推荐执行';
}

function runCustomerFlowPrimary() {
  runCustomerFlowAction(customerFlowNextAction || resolveCustomerFlow().active?.action || 'settings_ai');
}

function runCustomerFlowAction(action) {
  if (action === 'settings_ai' || action === 'add_account' || action === 'upload' || action === 'self_check') {
    return runSetupAction(action);
  }
  if (action === 'batch_ai') return batchProcess('rewrite', 'all');
  if (action === 'check') return batchValidate();
  if (action === 'preview') return submitToAmazon('preview');
  if (action === 'submit') return submitToAmazon('submit');
  return runSetupPrimaryAction();
}

function showCustomerBlock(title, message, action, buttonText = '去处理') {
  showModal(title, `<div class="customer-quick-start">
    <div class="quick-start-step">
      <strong>${escHtml(title)}</strong>
      <p>${escHtml(message)}</p>
    </div>
    <ul class="customer-block-list">
      <li>系统已经帮你挡住这一步，避免客户点错造成失败。</li>
      <li>按推荐按钮处理完，再回来继续当前操作。</li>
    </ul>
  </div>`);
  document.getElementById('modalFooter').innerHTML = `
    <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="closeModal(); runCustomerFlowAction('${escHtml(action)}')">${escHtml(buttonText)}</button>
    <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="closeModal()">关闭</button>`;
}

async function ensureCustomerPrerequisite(kind, options = {}) {
  if (!setupStatus) await refreshSetupStatus({ showFirstRun: false });
  const snapshot = getCustomerFlowSnapshot();
  if (kind === 'file' && !snapshot.hasFile) {
    showCustomerBlock('还没有商品表', '先导入 Excel，系统才知道要处理哪些商品。', 'upload', '导入 Excel');
    return false;
  }
  if (kind === 'ai' && !snapshot.aiReady) {
    showCustomerBlock('AI 还没配置好', '先去设置页点“一键恢复推荐”，Base URL 固定用 https://api.kk666.best，然后粘贴文字 AI 和图片 AI 的 Key。否则批量文案和生图一定会失败。', 'settings_ai', '去设置 AI');
    return false;
  }
  if (kind === 'amazon' && !snapshot.amazonReady) {
    showCustomerBlock('Amazon 账号还没配置好', '先添加 Seller ID、LWA Client ID、LWA Client Secret 和 Refresh Token。否则无法预览或正式提交。', 'add_account', '添加账号');
    return false;
  }
  if (kind === 'preview_before_submit') {
    const targetSet = new Set((options.skus || []).map(item => String(item || '').trim()).filter(Boolean));
    const realProducts = products.filter(product => {
      if (product.parentage_level === 'parent' || isRowDisabled(product)) return false;
      return targetSet.size === 0 || targetSet.has(product.sku);
    });
    const notPreviewed = realProducts.filter(product => !isPreviewValidForSelectedAccount(product));
    if (notPreviewed.length > 0) {
      showCustomerBlock('先预览，别直接提交', `还有 ${notPreviewed.length} 个 SKU 没有用当前账号完成 Amazon 预览。客户模式下先跑预览，预览通过后才允许正式提交。`, 'preview', '先跑预览');
      return false;
    }
  }
  return true;
}

function formatOfficialFieldLabel(key, zhLabel = '', enLabel = '') {
  const official = String(key || '').trim();
  const zh = String(zhLabel || COMMON_FIELD_LABELS_ZH[official] || '').trim();
  const en = String(enLabel || '').trim();
  if (!official) return zh || en || '';
  const translated = zh || (lang === 'zh' ? en : en);
  if (!translated || translated.toLowerCase() === official.toLowerCase()) return official;
  return `${official}（${translated}）`;
}

function findSchemaFieldMeta(schema, key) {
  const target = String(key || '').trim();
  if (!schema || !target) return null;
  for (const section of schema.sections || []) {
    for (const field of section.fields || []) {
      const aliases = [field.key, field.source_attribute].map(item => String(item || '').trim()).filter(Boolean);
      if (aliases.includes(target)) return field;
      for (const child of field.children || []) {
        const childAliases = [child.key, child.source_attribute].map(item => String(item || '').trim()).filter(Boolean);
        if (childAliases.includes(target)) return child;
      }
    }
  }
  return null;
}

function formatSchemaFieldReference(product, key, fallbackTitle = '') {
  const schema = product ? formSchemaCache.get(getFormSchemaKey(product)) : null;
  const meta = findSchemaFieldMeta(schema, key);
  return formatOfficialFieldLabel(
    key,
    meta?.label_zh || fallbackTitle || '',
    meta?.label_en || fallbackTitle || key
  );
}

function formatTemplateFieldText(text, product = null) {
  const raw = String(text || '').trim();
  const key = extractFieldKeyFromSummaryText(raw);
  if (!key) return raw;
  const title = raw.replace(/\(([^()]+)\)\s*$/, '').trim();
  const display = product
    ? formatSchemaFieldReference(product, key, title)
    : formatOfficialFieldLabel(key, title, title || key);
  return raw.replace(/^(.*?)(\s*\([^()]+\)\s*)$/, display);
}

function formatIssueMessageWithFields(product, issue, fallbackText = '') {
  const base = formatTemplateFieldText(String(issue?.message || fallbackText || '').trim(), product);
  const attrs = (issue?.attributeNames || []).map(item => String(item || '').trim()).filter(Boolean);
  if (!attrs.length) return base;
  if (attrs.some(name => base.includes(name))) return base;
  const fieldInfo = attrs.map(name => formatSchemaFieldReference(product, name, name)).join('、');
  if (!fieldInfo) return base;
  return `${base}${base ? ' ' : ''}字段：${fieldInfo}`;
}

function explainIssueForMerchant(product, issue, fallbackText = '') {
  const rawMessage = String(issue?.message || fallbackText || '').trim();
  const code = String(issue?.code || '').trim();
  const attrs = (issue?.attributeNames || []).map(item => String(item || '').trim()).filter(Boolean);
  const fieldsText = attrs.length > 0
    ? attrs.map(name => formatSchemaFieldReference(product, name, name)).join('、')
    : '';
  const appendFields = text => fieldsText ? `${text} 关联字段：${fieldsText}` : text;

  if (/merchant suggested asin/i.test(rawMessage) || /merchant_suggested_asin/i.test(rawMessage)) {
    return appendFields('系统没拿到可直接匹配的 ASIN。先确认这是新建商品还是已有商品跟卖；如果是已有商品，请补 ASIN。');
  }
  if (/externally assigned product identifier/i.test(rawMessage) || /external product id/i.test(rawMessage) || code === '8560') {
    return appendFields('当前商品身份信息不足。你需要补真实条码，或者确认这个商品是否符合免码条件。');
  }
  if (/submission_id/i.test(rawMessage)) {
    return appendFields('这是系统运行字段，不应该影响商家填写。当前更值得先看商品身份和类目结构问题。');
  }
  if (/you submitted an attribute .* does not belong/i.test(rawMessage) || code === '90000900') {
    return appendFields('这个字段对当前类目不是必需的，或者当前类目不接受这个字段。通常先不用优先处理，先看真正阻塞上架的问题。');
  }
  if (/bottoms size/i.test(rawMessage) || /size_system/i.test(rawMessage) || /size_class/i.test(rawMessage)) {
    return appendFields('当前裤装尺码结构不符合亚马逊要求。不是只填 M/L/XL 就行，还要按裤装尺码结构填写。');
  }
  if (/unit count/i.test(rawMessage)) {
    return appendFields('当前缺少单位数量，或者单位数量格式不对。一般可以先检查数量是不是数字、单位是不是 Count。');
  }
  if (/import designation/i.test(rawMessage)) {
    return appendFields('当前缺少进口标识信息。先确认商品是进口还是本地生产，再补这个字段。');
  }
  if (/target gender/i.test(rawMessage)) {
    return appendFields('当前缺少目标性别信息。服饰类目通常需要明确是 male、female 还是 unisex。');
  }
  if (/model name/i.test(rawMessage)) {
    return appendFields('当前缺少型号名称。可以理解成这个款式或型号在亚马逊要怎么被识别。');
  }
  if (/list price/i.test(rawMessage)) {
    return appendFields('当前缺少建议零售价。先确认这个类目是否真的需要该字段，以及是否要填写划线价。');
  }
  if (/closure type/i.test(rawMessage) || /\bclosure\b/i.test(rawMessage)) {
    return appendFields('当前缺少裤子/服饰类目的闭合方式信息，比如拉链、抽绳、纽扣等。');
  }
  if (/rise style/i.test(rawMessage) || /\brise\b/i.test(rawMessage)) {
    return appendFields('当前缺少裤腰高度信息，比如 High Rise / Mid Rise / Low Rise。');
  }
  if (/dangerous goods regulations/i.test(rawMessage) || /supplier_declared_dg_hz_regulation/i.test(rawMessage)) {
    return appendFields('这是危化品相关的兼容性提示。通常不是当前最主要阻塞，可以先处理身份或结构问题。');
  }
  if (/unable to retrieve media content/i.test(rawMessage) || /image file type isn't supported/i.test(rawMessage)) {
    return appendFields('亚马逊无法读取你的图片。先检查图片链接能否直接打开、图片格式是否正确，以及是否会 404。');
  }
  if (/discoverable/i.test(rawMessage)) {
    return appendFields('这是上架后的结果状态信息，说明系统正在跟踪商品是否已经可被亚马逊前台发现。');
  }
  if (/required but missing/i.test(rawMessage)) {
    return appendFields('这是缺少必填字段的提示。先补齐这里提到的字段，再重新预览。');
  }
  if (/not a valid value/i.test(rawMessage) || /invalid value/i.test(rawMessage)) {
    return appendFields('这个字段目前填写了，但值不符合亚马逊类目规则。建议按该字段的可选值重新选择。');
  }
  if (!rawMessage) return '';
  return appendFields(formatIssueMessageWithFields(product, issue, rawMessage));
}

function buildMerchantIssueView(product, issue, fallbackText = '') {
  const raw = formatIssueMessageWithFields(product, issue, fallbackText);
  const explained = explainIssueForMerchant(product, issue, fallbackText);
  if (!explained) return { primary: raw, secondary: '' };
  if (!raw || explained === raw) return { primary: explained, secondary: '' };
  return { primary: explained, secondary: raw };
}

function formatShortMerchantIssue(product, issue, fallbackText = '') {
  const view = buildMerchantIssueView(product, issue, fallbackText);
  return view.primary || view.secondary || fallbackText || '';
}

function summarizeTechnicalIssue(issue, fallbackText = '') {
  const code = String(issue?.code || '').trim();
  const severity = String(issue?.severity || issue?.level || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  const raw = String(issue?.message || fallbackText || '').trim();
  const parts = [];
  if (severity) parts.push(severity);
  if (code) parts.push(code);
  const head = parts.length > 0 ? `[${parts.join(' / ')}] ` : '';
  return `${head}${raw}`.trim();
}

function hasHttpUrl(value) {
  return /^https?:\/\//i.test(String(value || '').trim());
}

function hasMediaLocator(value) {
  return /^(https?:\/\/|s3:\/\/)/i.test(String(value || '').trim());
}

function parsePriceAmount(value) {
  const text = String(value ?? '').trim().replace(/[$,¥￥€£\s]/g, '');
  if (!text) return null;
  const amount = Number(text);
  return Number.isFinite(amount) ? amount : NaN;
}

function getPriceBlockingReason(value) {
  const raw = String(value ?? '').trim();
  if (!raw) return '缺少价格';
  const amount = parsePriceAmount(raw);
  if (Number.isNaN(amount)) return `价格格式错误：${raw}`;
  if (amount <= 0) return `价格必须大于 0：${raw}`;
  if (amount > MAX_SUBMISSION_PRICE) return `价格疑似小数点/单位填错：${raw}`;
  return '';
}

function getProductAsin(product) {
  const raw = product?._raw || {};
  return String(
    product?.asin || product?.merchant_suggested_asin || product?.source_asin ||
    raw.asin || raw.ASIN || raw.merchant_suggested_asin || raw.source_asin || ''
  ).trim().toUpperCase();
}

function getDuplicateAsinMap() {
  const grouped = new Map();
  products.forEach(product => {
    const asin = getProductAsin(product);
    if (!asin) return;
    if (!grouped.has(asin)) grouped.set(asin, []);
    grouped.get(asin).push(product.sku || '-');
  });
  const duplicated = new Map();
  grouped.forEach((skus, asin) => {
    const uniqueSkus = Array.from(new Set(skus.filter(Boolean)));
    if (uniqueSkus.length > 1) uniqueSkus.forEach(sku => duplicated.set(sku, { asin, skus: uniqueSkus }));
  });
  return duplicated;
}

function getIncompleteFamilyMessageForSkus(skus) {
  const selected = new Set((skus || []).map(item => String(item || '').trim()).filter(Boolean));
  for (const sku of selected) {
    const product = products.find(item => item.sku === sku);
    if (!product) continue;
    const level = String(product.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase();
    const parentSku = level === 'parent' ? product.sku : String(product.parent_sku || '').trim();
    if (!parentSku) continue;
    const children = products.filter(item => String(item.parent_sku || '').trim() === parentSku && String(item.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase() === 'child');
    if (level === 'parent' && children.length === 0) return `父体 ${parentSku} 没有子体，不能单独提交`;
    const missing = children.filter(child => !selected.has(child.sku)).map(child => child.sku).filter(Boolean);
    if (missing.length > 0) return `变体家族 ${parentSku} 必须整组处理，还缺子 SKU：${missing.slice(0, 8).join('、')}`;
  }
  return '';
}

function isAlreadySubmittedProduct(product) {
  const status = String(product?.submit_status || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  return ['ACCEPTED', 'ACCEPTED_WITH_WARNINGS'].includes(status);
}

function getAccountById(accountId) {
  const id = String(accountId || '').trim();
  return amazonAccounts.find(account => String(account.seller_id || '').trim() === id) || null;
}

function isPreviewValidForSelectedAccount(product) {
  if (String(product?.preview_status || '').trim().toUpperCase() !== 'VALID') return false;
  if (!selectedAccountId) return true;
  const account = getAccountById(selectedAccountId);
  const previewAccountId = String(product.preview_account_id || '').trim();
  const previewAccountName = String(product.preview_account || '').trim();
  if (previewAccountId && previewAccountId !== selectedAccountId) return false;
  if (!previewAccountId) {
    const currentAccountName = String(account?.name || '').trim();
    if (!previewAccountName) return false;
    if (![selectedAccountId, currentAccountName].filter(Boolean).includes(previewAccountName)) return false;
  }
  const previewMarketplace = String(product.preview_marketplace_id || '').trim();
  if (!previewMarketplace) return false;
  if (account && previewMarketplace && previewMarketplace !== String(account.marketplace_id || '').trim()) return false;
  return true;
}

function getPreviewDisplayStatus(product) {
  const status = String(product?.preview_status || '').trim();
  if (status.toUpperCase() === 'VALID' && !isPreviewValidForSelectedAccount(product)) return '需重新预览';
  return status;
}

function refreshPreviewAccountHints(options = {}) {
  let staleCount = 0;
  products.forEach(product => {
    product._previewStaleForAccount = String(product.preview_status || '').trim().toUpperCase() === 'VALID'
      && !isPreviewValidForSelectedAccount(product);
    if (product._previewStaleForAccount) staleCount += 1;
  });
  if (options.toast && staleCount > 0) {
    showToast('warning', `已切换 Amazon 账号，${staleCount} 个 SKU 需要用当前账号重新预览`);
  }
  return staleCount;
}

function setSelectedAmazonAccount(accountId, options = {}) {
  const next = String(accountId || '').trim();
  const changed = next !== selectedAccountId;
  selectedAccountId = next;
  refreshPreviewAccountHints({ toast: changed && options.toast });
  if (options.refreshUi) {
    renderTable();
    updateStats();
    refreshTemplateFlowUi();
  }
}

function getProductImageCandidates(product) {
  const urls = [];
  const pushUnique = (value) => {
    const text = String(value || '').trim();
    if (hasHttpUrl(text) && !urls.includes(text)) urls.push(text);
  };
  pushUnique(product.main_image_url);
  for (let i = 2; i <= 9; i++) {
    pushUnique(product['image_' + i]);
    pushUnique(product['other_image_url_' + (i - 1)]);
  }
  return urls;
}

function getRawSkuValue(product) {
  const raw = product && product._raw ? product._raw : {};
  return String(raw.SKU || raw.sku || raw.seller_sku || '').trim();
}

function isRowDisabled(product) {
  const candidates = [
    product.enabled,
    product.is_active,
    product.active,
    product.status,
    product.row_status,
    product.listing_status,
    product.action,
    product.update_delete,
    product._raw && product._raw.enabled,
    product._raw && product._raw.status,
    product._raw && product._raw.action,
  ];
  return candidates.some(value => {
    const text = String(value == null ? '' : value).trim().toLowerCase();
    return ['false', '0', 'disabled', 'disable', 'inactive', 'off', '停用', '禁用', '暂停', '删除'].includes(text);
  });
}

function splitIssueText(text) {
  return String(text || '').split(/[;|]/).map(item => item.trim()).filter(Boolean);
}

function getTemplateBlockingReasons(product) {
  const reasons = [];
  splitIssueText(product.template_blocking_issues || '').forEach(reason => reasons.push(reason));
  splitIssueText(product.template_required_missing_fields || '').forEach(reason => reasons.push(`模板必填缺失：${reason}`));
  if (String(product.listing_check_status || '').toLowerCase() === 'fail') {
    if (product.listing_check_summary) reasons.push(`缺项诊断未通过：${product.listing_check_summary}`);
    else reasons.push('缺项诊断未通过');
  }
  return Array.from(new Set(reasons));
}

function hasTemplateBlockingIssues(product) {
  if (!product) return false;
  if (Number(product.template_required_missing_count || 0) > 0) return true;
  if (String(product.template_ready_to_submit || '').toLowerCase() === 'no') return true;
  if (String(product.listing_check_status || '').toLowerCase() === 'fail') return true;
  return getTemplateBlockingReasons(product).length > 0;
}

function getSubmitEligibleSkus() {
  return products
    .filter(p => p.parentage_level !== 'parent' && !isRowDisabled(p))
    .filter(p => !hasTemplateBlockingIssues(p))
    .filter(p => !isAlreadySubmittedProduct(p))
    .filter(p => !!(p.title || p.item_name || '').trim())
    .filter(p => !getPriceBlockingReason(p.price || p.standard_price || ''))
    .filter(p => hasMediaLocator(p.main_image_url || ''))
    .map(p => p.sku)
    .filter(Boolean);
}

function updateSubmitAvailability() {
  const btn = document.getElementById('btnSubmit');
  if (!btn) return;
  const reason = products.length === 0
    ? '先导入 Excel'
    : (!setupStatus?.amazon?.ready ? 'Amazon 账号还没配置好：先添加账号' : (getSubmitEligibleSkus().length === 0 ? '没有可预览/提交的 SKU，请先修复阻断项' : ''));
  btn.disabled = !!reason;
  btn.title = reason || '';
  btn.classList.toggle('toolbar-locked', !!reason);
}

function getSelectedActionableSkus() {
  const actionableSet = new Set(
    products
      .filter(p => p.parentage_level !== 'parent' && !isRowDisabled(p) && !hasTemplateBlockingIssues(p))
      .map(p => p.sku)
      .filter(Boolean)
  );
  return Array.from(selectedSkus).filter(sku => actionableSet.has(sku));
}

function getFilteredActionableSkus() {
  return products
    .filter(p => p.parentage_level !== 'parent' && !isRowDisabled(p))
    .filter(p => matchFilter(p) && matchSearch(p))
    .map(p => p.sku)
    .filter(Boolean);
}

function getWorkspaceActionableProducts() {
  return products.filter(product => product.parentage_level !== 'parent' && !isRowDisabled(product));
}

function setTemplatePanelCollapsed(nextState) {
  templatePanelCollapsed = !!nextState;
  refreshTemplateFlowUi();
}

function toggleTemplatePanel() {
  setTemplatePanelCollapsed(!templatePanelCollapsed);
}

function syncSelectionState() {
  const validSkus = new Set(
    products
      .filter(p => p.parentage_level !== 'parent' && !isRowDisabled(p))
      .map(p => p.sku)
      .filter(Boolean)
  );
  selectedSkus.forEach(sku => {
    if (!validSkus.has(sku)) selectedSkus.delete(sku);
  });
  updateBatchBar();
  const filteredSkus = getFilteredActionableSkus();
  const selectAllCb = document.getElementById('selectAllCb');
  if (selectAllCb) {
    selectAllCb.checked = filteredSkus.length > 0 && filteredSkus.every(sku => selectedSkus.has(sku));
    selectAllCb.indeterminate = filteredSkus.some(sku => selectedSkus.has(sku)) && !selectAllCb.checked;
  }
  updateToolbarRecommendation();
}

function renderFileHealth() {
  const banner = document.getElementById('fileHealthBanner');
  const text = document.getElementById('fileHealthText');
  const fileInfo = document.getElementById('fileInfo');
  if (!banner || !text || !fileInfo) return;

  const warningText = currentFileMeta.warning || (currentFileMeta.type === 'xls'
    ? '当前文件是 `.xls`，建议尽快另存为 `.xlsx`；复杂样式保留依赖本机 Excel/WPS。'
    : '');

  if (currentFileMeta.type === 'xls' && warningText) {
    banner.classList.add('show');
    text.textContent = warningText;
    fileInfo.textContent = `${fileInfo.textContent || ''} · XLS兼容模式`.trim();
  } else {
    banner.classList.remove('show');
    text.textContent = '';
  }
}

function collectActionPlan(action, scope) {
  const selectedOnly = selectedSkus.size > 0;
  const requestedProducts = selectedOnly
    ? products.filter(p => selectedSkus.has(p.sku))
    : products.filter(p => p.parentage_level !== 'parent');

  const actionableSkus = [];
  const skipped = [];
  const attention = [];
  const seen = new Set();
  const requestedSkuSet = new Set(requestedProducts.map(product => product.sku).filter(Boolean));
  const duplicateAsins = getDuplicateAsinMap();

  const addSkipped = (product, reason) => {
    skipped.push({ sku: product.sku || '-', reason });
  };

  const ensureVariantParentQueued = product => {
    if (!['submit', 'preview'].includes(action)) return true;
    if (String(product.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase() !== 'child') return true;
    const parentSku = String(product.parent_sku || '').trim();
    if (!parentSku) {
      addSkipped(product, '子体缺少 parent_sku，无法进行父子变体提交');
      return false;
    }
    const parent = products.find(p => p.sku === parentSku && String(p.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase() === 'parent');
    if (!parent) {
      addSkipped(product, `缺少父体行 ${parentSku}，无法进行父子变体提交`);
      return false;
    }
    const rawParentSku = getRawSkuValue(parent);
    if (!rawParentSku || rawParentSku !== parentSku) {
      addSkipped(product, `父体 ${parentSku} 只存在于前端分组展示中，Excel 里缺少真实父体行`);
      return false;
    }
    if (isRowDisabled(parent)) {
      addSkipped(product, `父体 ${parentSku} 当前被停用，无法提交变体家族`);
      return false;
    }
    if (hasTemplateBlockingIssues(parent)) {
      const reasons = getTemplateBlockingReasons(parent);
      addSkipped(product, reasons[0] ? `父体未就绪：${reasons[0]}` : `父体 ${parentSku} 未就绪`);
      return false;
    }
    const familyChildren = products.filter(p => String(p.parent_sku || '').trim() === parentSku && String(p.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase() === 'child');
    const missingChildren = familyChildren.filter(child => !requestedSkuSet.has(child.sku)).map(child => child.sku).filter(Boolean);
    if (missingChildren.length > 0) {
      addSkipped(product, `变体家族必须整组提交，还缺子 SKU：${missingChildren.slice(0, 8).join('、')}`);
      return false;
    }
    if (!seen.has(parentSku)) {
      seen.add(parentSku);
      actionableSkus.push(parentSku);
    }
    return true;
  };

  requestedProducts.forEach(product => {
    const sku = product.sku || '';
    if (seen.has(sku)) return;
    seen.add(sku);

    if (product.parentage_level === 'parent') {
      addSkipped(product, '父体行仅用于分组展示，请处理子 SKU');
      return;
    }
    if (!sku) {
      addSkipped(product, '缺少 SKU');
      return;
    }
    if (isRowDisabled(product)) {
      addSkipped(product, '该行处于停用/禁用状态');
      return;
    }
    if ((action === 'submit' || action === 'preview') && duplicateAsins.has(sku)) {
      const info = duplicateAsins.get(sku);
      addSkipped(product, `ASIN ${info.asin} 在表内重复：${info.skus.join('、')}`);
      return;
    }

    const title = product.title || product.item_name || '';
    const price = product.price || product.standard_price || '';
    const mainImage = product.main_image_url || '';
    const allImages = getProductImageCandidates(product);

    if (action === 'rewrite') {
      if (!title) {
        addSkipped(product, '缺少标题，无法稳定生成文案');
        return;
      }
    }

    if (action === 'image') {
      if (scope === 'all') {
        if (allImages.length === 0) {
          addSkipped(product, '缺少可用图片 URL');
          return;
        }
      } else if (!hasHttpUrl(mainImage)) {
        addSkipped(product, '缺少主图 URL');
        return;
      }
    }

    if (action === 'submit' || action === 'preview') {
      if (!ensureVariantParentQueued(product)) return;
      if (action === 'submit' && isAlreadySubmittedProduct(product)) {
        addSkipped(product, `已上架成功${product.asin ? ` ASIN ${product.asin}` : ''}，不要重复提交`);
        return;
      }
      const missing = [];
      if (!title) missing.push('缺少标题');
      const priceReason = getPriceBlockingReason(price);
      if (priceReason) missing.push(priceReason);
      if (!hasMediaLocator(mainImage)) missing.push('缺少主图');
      if (missing.length > 0) {
        addSkipped(product, missing.join('、'));
        return;
      }
      if (hasTemplateBlockingIssues(product)) {
        const reasons = getTemplateBlockingReasons(product);
        addSkipped(product, reasons[0] || '模板阻断项未修复');
        return;
      }
      if (action === 'submit' && !isPreviewValidForSelectedAccount(product)) {
        addSkipped(product, '当前账号未重新预览通过');
        return;
      }
    }

    if (action === 'validate') {
      const warnings = [];
      if (!title) warnings.push('缺少标题');
      const priceReason = getPriceBlockingReason(price);
      if (priceReason) warnings.push(priceReason);
      if (!hasMediaLocator(mainImage)) warnings.push('缺少主图');
      if (warnings.length > 0) {
        attention.push({ sku, reason: warnings.join('、') });
      }
    }

    actionableSkus.push(sku);
  });

  let finalActionableSkus = actionableSkus;
  if (action === 'submit' || action === 'preview') {
    const childSkusInPlan = new Set(actionableSkus.filter(sku => {
      const product = products.find(item => item.sku === sku);
      return product && String(product.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase() !== 'parent';
    }));
    finalActionableSkus = actionableSkus.filter(sku => {
      const product = products.find(item => item.sku === sku);
      if (!product || String(product.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase() !== 'parent') return true;
      return products.some(child => String(child.parent_sku || '').trim() === sku && childSkusInPlan.has(child.sku));
    });
  }

  const reasonCounts = {};
  skipped.forEach(item => { reasonCounts[item.reason] = (reasonCounts[item.reason] || 0) + 1; });
  const attentionCounts = {};
  attention.forEach(item => { attentionCounts[item.reason] = (attentionCounts[item.reason] || 0) + 1; });

  return {
    action,
    scope,
    selectedOnly,
    requestedCount: requestedProducts.length,
    actionableSkus: finalActionableSkus,
    skipped,
    attention,
    reasonCounts,
    attentionCounts,
  };
}

function getPlanTitle(action, scope) {
  if (action === 'rewrite') {
    if (scope === 'title') return '批量AI文案（标题）';
    if (scope === 'bullets') return '批量AI文案（卖点）';
    return '批量AI文案';
  }
  if (action === 'image') return scope === 'all' ? '批量AI生图（全部图片）' : '批量AI生图（主图）';
  if (action === 'validate') return '批量校验';
  if (action === 'submit') return '正式提交';
  if (action === 'preview') return '预览验证';
  if (action === 'export') return '导出';
  return '批量处理';
}

function renderReasonSummary(mapObj, toneClass) {
  const entries = Object.entries(mapObj || {});
  if (entries.length === 0) return '<div class="preflight-empty">无</div>';
  return `<div class="preflight-tags">${entries.map(([reason, count]) =>
    `<span class="preflight-tag ${toneClass}">${escHtml(reason)} × ${count}</span>`
  ).join('')}</div>`;
}

function renderSkippedSkuDetails(skipped) {
  const items = (skipped || []).slice(0, 20);
  if (items.length === 0) return '';
  return `<div class="preflight-block">
    <div class="preflight-title">逐 SKU 跳过原因</div>
    <div class="preflight-sku-list">${items.map(item => `<div class="preflight-sku-row"><strong>${escHtml(item.sku || '-')}</strong><span>${escHtml(item.reason || '-')}</span></div>`).join('')}</div>
    ${(skipped || []).length > items.length ? `<div class="preflight-empty">还有 ${(skipped || []).length - items.length} 个 SKU 未展开显示</div>` : ''}
  </div>`;
}

function showActionPreflight(plan, onConfirm, context = {}) {
  const title = getPlanTitle(plan.action, plan.scope);
  const skippedHtml = renderReasonSummary(plan.reasonCounts, 'warn');
  const attentionHtml = renderReasonSummary(plan.attentionCounts, 'info');
  const accountMeta = context.account || null;
  const executionTags = [
    context.mode ? `<span class="preflight-tag info">模式：${escHtml(formatExecutionModeLabel(context.mode))}</span>` : '',
    accountMeta ? `<span class="preflight-tag info">目标账号：${escHtml(accountMeta.name)}</span>` : '',
    accountMeta ? `<span class="preflight-tag info">目标站点：${escHtml(accountMeta.site)}</span>` : '',
    `<span class="preflight-tag info">SKU 数量：${plan.actionableSkus.length}</span>`,
  ].filter(Boolean).join('');
  showModal(title + ' - 执行摘要', `
    <div class="preflight-panel">
      <div class="preflight-stat-grid">
        <div class="preflight-stat"><span>候选商品</span><strong>${plan.requestedCount}</strong></div>
        <div class="preflight-stat"><span>实际处理</span><strong>${plan.actionableSkus.length}</strong></div>
        <div class="preflight-stat"><span>自动跳过</span><strong>${plan.skipped.length}</strong></div>
        <div class="preflight-stat"><span>风险提醒</span><strong>${plan.attention.length}</strong></div>
      </div>
      <div class="preflight-block">
        <div class="preflight-title">本次执行</div>
        ${executionTags ? `<div class="preflight-tags">${executionTags}</div>` : '<div class="preflight-empty">无</div>'}
      </div>
      <div class="preflight-block">
        <div class="preflight-title">自动跳过原因</div>
        ${skippedHtml}
      </div>
      ${renderSkippedSkuDetails(plan.skipped)}
      <div class="preflight-block">
        <div class="preflight-title">执行前提醒</div>
        ${attentionHtml}
      </div>
      ${plan.skipped.length > 0 ? `<div class="preflight-note">系统将只处理可执行 SKU，避免把父体行、无图行或明显不完整的商品带入流程。</div>` : ''}
    </div>
  `);
  document.getElementById('modalFooter').innerHTML = `
    <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="closeModal()">取消</button>
    <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" id="preflightConfirmBtn">继续处理 ${plan.actionableSkus.length} 个 SKU</button>`;
  document.getElementById('preflightConfirmBtn').onclick = () => {
    closeModal();
    onConfirm();
  };
}

function normalizeProductForValidation(p) {
  return {
    sku: p.sku || '',
    title: p.title || p.item_name || '',
    brand: p.brand || p.brand_name || '',
    description: p.description || p.product_description || '',
    keywords: p.keywords || p.generic_keywords || '',
    price: p.price || p.standard_price || '',
    currency: p.currency || 'USD',
    quantity: p.quantity || '',
    condition_type: p.condition_type || '',
    fulfillment_channel: p.fulfillment_channel || '',
    product_type: p.product_type || '',
    upc: p.upc || p.ean || p.product_id || '',
    external_product_id_type: p.external_product_id_type || '',
    product_identity_mode: p.product_identity_mode || '',
    item_type_keyword: p.item_type_keyword || '',
    main_image_url: p.main_image_url || '',
    bullet_point_1: p.bullet_point_1 || '',
    bullet_point_2: p.bullet_point_2 || '',
    bullet_point_3: p.bullet_point_3 || '',
    bullet_point_4: p.bullet_point_4 || '',
    bullet_point_5: p.bullet_point_5 || '',
    color: p.color || '',
    size: p.size || '',
    material: p.material || '',
    manufacturer: p.manufacturer || '',
    model_number: p.model_number || '',
    country_of_origin: p.country_of_origin || '',
    list_price: p.list_price || '',
    unit_count: p.unit_count || '',
    number_of_items: p.number_of_items || '',
    included_components: p.included_components || '',
    care_instructions: p.care_instructions || '',
    special_feature: p.special_feature || '',
    item_weight: p.item_weight || '',
    item_weight_unit: p.item_weight_unit || '',
    item_length: p.item_length || '',
    item_width: p.item_width || '',
    item_height: p.item_height || '',
    dimension_unit: p.dimension_unit || '',
    package_weight: p.package_weight || '',
    package_weight_unit: p.package_weight_unit || '',
    package_length: p.package_length || '',
    package_width: p.package_width || '',
    package_height: p.package_height || '',
    batteries_required: p.batteries_required || '',
    batteries_included: p.batteries_included || '',
    battery_type: p.battery_type || '',
    number_of_batteries: p.number_of_batteries || '',
    battery_cell_composition: p.battery_cell_composition || '',
    lithium_battery_packaging: p.lithium_battery_packaging || '',
    lithium_battery_energy_content: p.lithium_battery_energy_content || '',
    lithium_battery_weight: p.lithium_battery_weight || '',
    hazmat_declaration: p.hazmat_declaration || '',
    parent_sku: p.parent_sku || '',
    parentage_level: p.parentage_level || '',
    variation_theme: p.variation_theme || '',
  };
}

function applyValidationResult(product, result) {
  const issues = result.issues || [];
  const errors = issues.filter(issue => issue.level === 'error').map(issue => issue.message);
  const warnings = issues.filter(issue => issue.level === 'warning').map(issue => issue.message);
  product._validPass = errors.length === 0;
  product._validErrors = errors;
  product._validWarnings = warnings;
  product._validationIssues = issues;
  product._schemaRequiredMissing = result.schema_required_missing || [];
}

function applyListingCheckResult(product, result) {
  product._listingCheck = result || null;
  product._previewIssuePayload = {
    status: result?.preview?.status || product.preview_status || '',
    valid: String(result?.preview?.status || '').toUpperCase() === 'VALID',
    issues: result?.preview?.issues || [],
  };
  product.listing_check_status = result?.status || '';
  product.listing_check_summary = result?.summary_text || '';
  product.listing_check_time = result?.checked_at || '';
  product.listing_check_account = result?.account_name || product.listing_check_account || '';
  product.listing_check_missing_fields = (result?.missing_fields || [])
    .map(item => `${item.title || item.name} (${item.name})`)
    .join('; ');
  const issueMessages = [];
  (result?.preview?.issues || []).forEach(issue => {
    const text = formatShortMerchantIssue(product, issue, issue.message || '');
    if (text) issueMessages.push(text);
  });
  (result?.listing?.issues || []).forEach(issue => {
    const text = formatShortMerchantIssue(product, issue, issue.message || '');
    if (text) issueMessages.push(text);
  });
  (result?.media?.checks || []).forEach(item => {
    if (!item.ok && item.message) issueMessages.push(`${item.field}: ${item.message}`);
  });
  product.listing_check_issues = issueMessages.join(' | ');
}

function applyPreviewResult(product, result) {
  if (!product || !result) return;
  const status = result.status || (result.valid ? 'VALID' : 'INVALID');
  product.preview_status = status;
  product._previewIssuePayload = {
    status,
    valid: !!result.valid,
    issues: result.issues || [],
  };
  if (result.account_id) product.preview_account_id = result.account_id;
  if (result.marketplace_id) product.preview_marketplace_id = result.marketplace_id;
  if (result.account || result.account_name) product.preview_account = result.account || result.account_name;
  const messages = [];
  (result.errors || []).forEach(message => {
    if (message) messages.push(`[ERROR] ${formatTemplateFieldText(message, product)}`);
  });
  (result.warnings || []).forEach(message => {
    if (message) messages.push(`[WARN] ${formatTemplateFieldText(message, product)}`);
  });
  product.preview_message = messages.join('; ');
}

function showValidationIssues(sku) {
  const product = products.find(p => p.sku === sku);
  if (!product) return;

  const errors = product._validErrors || [];
  const warnings = product._validWarnings || [];
  const schemaMissing = product._schemaRequiredMissing || [];
  const lines = [];

  if (errors.length) {
    lines.push(`<div style="margin-bottom:12px"><strong style="color:#cf1322">错误</strong><ul style="margin:8px 0 0 18px">${errors.map(msg => `<li>${escHtml(msg)}</li>`).join('')}</ul></div>`);
  }
  if (warnings.length) {
    lines.push(`<div style="margin-bottom:12px"><strong style="color:#d48806">警告</strong><ul style="margin:8px 0 0 18px">${warnings.map(msg => `<li>${escHtml(msg)}</li>`).join('')}</ul></div>`);
  }
  if (schemaMissing.length) {
    lines.push(`<div><strong>类目必填缺失</strong><ul style="margin:8px 0 0 18px">${schemaMissing.map(item => `<li>${escHtml(formatSchemaFieldReference(product, item.name || '', item.title || item.name || ''))}</li>`).join('')}</ul></div>`);
  }
  const templateBlocking = getTemplateBlockingReasons(product);
  if (templateBlocking.length) {
    lines.push(`<div style="margin-bottom:12px"><strong style="color:#cf1322">模板阻断项</strong><ul style="margin:8px 0 0 18px">${templateBlocking.map(msg => `<li>${escHtml(formatTemplateFieldText(msg, product))}</li>`).join('')}</ul></div>`);
  }

  if (lines.length === 0) {
    lines.push('<p>当前无校验问题。</p>');
  }

  const bucketKey = inferPrimaryIssueBucketForProduct(product);
  if (bucketKey) {
    const labels = {
      identity: '去补身份字段',
      structure: '去补结构字段',
      content: '去补内容字段',
      media: '去看图片问题',
    };
    lines.unshift(`<div style="margin-bottom:12px;padding:10px 12px;border:1px solid var(--border-light);border-radius:12px;background:#f8fbff;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;gap:12px;">
      <div style="font-size:12px;line-height:1.6;color:var(--text-secondary);">系统已经帮你判断出当前最该先处理的问题类型。你不用自己猜，直接跳过去修就行。</div>
      <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="closeModal(); openPrimaryIssueNavigator('${escHtml(sku)}','${bucketKey}')">${labels[bucketKey] || '去修字段'}</button>
    </div>`);
  }

  showModal(`校验结果 - ${sku}`, lines.join(''));
}

async function fetchAccounts(force = false) {
  if (!force && amazonAccounts.length > 0) return amazonAccounts;
  const response = await fetch('/api/accounts');
  const data = await response.json();
  if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
  amazonAccounts = (data.accounts || []).filter(account => account.enabled !== false);
  if (data.current && data.current.account && data.current.kind === 'submit') {
    const currentAccount = amazonAccounts.find(account => (account.name || account.seller_id) === data.current.account || account.seller_id === data.current.account);
    if (currentAccount) setSelectedAmazonAccount(currentAccount.seller_id);
  }
  if (amazonAccounts.length === 0) {
    setSelectedAmazonAccount('');
    return amazonAccounts;
  }
  if (!selectedAccountId || !amazonAccounts.some(account => account.seller_id === selectedAccountId)) {
    const defaultAccount = amazonAccounts.find(account => account.is_default) || amazonAccounts[0];
    setSelectedAmazonAccount(defaultAccount ? defaultAccount.seller_id : '');
  }
  return amazonAccounts;
}


function rememberRecentSubmitResult(task, options = {}) {
  if (!task || task.kind !== 'submit') return;
  const result = task && typeof task.result === 'object' ? task.result : {};
  const rows = Array.isArray(result.results) ? result.results : [];
  const acceptedRows = rows.filter(item => String(item.status || '').trim().toUpperCase() === 'ACCEPTED');
  if (acceptedRows.length === 0) return;
  recentSubmitHighlights = new Set(acceptedRows.map(item => item.sku).filter(Boolean));
  const shouldToast = options.toast === true && task.id && !recentSubmitToastTaskIds.has(task.id);
  if (shouldToast) {
    recentSubmitToastTaskIds.add(task.id);
    acceptedRows.forEach(item => showSubmitSuccessToast({ ...item, account: result.account || '', marketplace_name: result.marketplace || '' }));
  }
}

function getActionableSkus() {
  const actionableProducts = products.filter(p => p.parentage_level !== 'parent' && !isRowDisabled(p));
  if (selectedSkus.size === 0) {
    return actionableProducts.map(p => p.sku).filter(Boolean);
  }
  const actionableSkuSet = new Set(actionableProducts.map(p => p.sku).filter(Boolean));
  return Array.from(selectedSkus).filter(sku => actionableSkuSet.has(sku));
}

function computeTemplateFlowState() {
  const actionableProducts = getWorkspaceActionableProducts();
  const templateInput = (document.getElementById('templateProductTypeInput')?.value || selectedTemplateType || workspaceTemplateSummary?.product_type || '').trim();
  const templateReady = !!(workspaceTemplateSummary && workspaceTemplateSummary.template_id);
  const fileLoaded = !!currentFile;
  const diagnosticsReady = actionableProducts.length > 0 && actionableProducts.some(product =>
    String(product.listing_check_status || '').trim()
    || Number(product.template_required_total || 0) > 0
    || splitIssueText(product.template_blocking_issues || '').length > 0
    || splitIssueText(product.template_required_missing_fields || '').length > 0
    || splitIssueText(product.template_recommended_missing_fields || '').length > 0
  );
  const previewPassCount = actionableProducts.filter(product => isPreviewValidForSelectedAccount(product)).length;
  const submitDoneCount = actionableProducts.filter(product => {
    return isAlreadySubmittedProduct(product);
  }).length;
  const previewReady = actionableProducts.length > 0 && previewPassCount === actionableProducts.length;
  const submitReady = actionableProducts.length > 0 && submitDoneCount === actionableProducts.length;
  const directFlow = fileLoaded && !templateInput && !templateReady;
  const directDiagnoseDone = actionableProducts.length > 0 && (diagnosticsReady || previewPassCount > 0 || submitDoneCount > 0);

  const steps = directFlow
    ? [
        { key: 'upload', label: '导入商品', done: fileLoaded },
        { key: 'diagnose', label: '缺项诊断', done: directDiagnoseDone },
        { key: 'preview', label: '预览通过', done: previewReady },
        { key: 'submit', label: '正式提交', done: submitReady },
      ]
    : [
        { key: 'choose', label: '选择模板', done: !!templateInput },
        { key: 'download', label: '下载模板', done: templateReady },
        { key: 'upload', label: '上传采集结果', done: fileLoaded },
        { key: 'diagnose', label: '自动诊断', done: diagnosticsReady },
        { key: 'preview', label: '预览通过', done: previewReady },
        { key: 'submit', label: '正式提交', done: submitReady },
      ];

  const activeIndex = steps.findIndex(step => !step.done);
  return {
    steps,
    activeIndex,
    nextLabel: activeIndex >= 0 ? steps[activeIndex].label : '流程已完成',
    fileLoaded,
    actionableCount: actionableProducts.length,
    previewPassCount,
    submitDoneCount,
    directFlow,
  };
}

function renderTemplateStepper() {
  const el = document.getElementById('templateStepper');
  if (!el) return;
  const state = computeTemplateFlowState();
  el.innerHTML = state.steps.map((step, index) => {
    let statusClass = 'pending';
    if (step.done) statusClass = 'done';
    else if (state.activeIndex === index) statusClass = 'active';
    return `<div class="template-step ${statusClass}">
      <span class="template-step-index">${index + 1}</span>
      <span>${escHtml(step.label)}</span>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

function renderTemplateCompactSummary() {
  const el = document.getElementById('templateCompactSummary');
  const card = document.getElementById('templateFlowCard');
  const toggleBtn = document.getElementById('templatePanelToggleBtn');
  if (!el || !card || !toggleBtn) return;

  const state = computeTemplateFlowState();
  const fileName = document.getElementById('fileInfo')?.dataset.baseName || '';
  const templateName = workspaceTemplateSummary?.template_id || workspaceTemplateSummary?.product_type || '未使用';
  const summaryBits = [
    fileName ? `文件 ${fileName}` : '',
    `模板 ${templateName}`,
    state.actionableCount > 0 ? `SKU ${state.actionableCount}` : '',
    state.previewPassCount > 0 ? `预览通过 ${state.previewPassCount}` : '',
    state.submitDoneCount > 0 ? `已提交 ${state.submitDoneCount}` : '',
  ].filter(Boolean);

  const collapsed = templatePanelCollapsed && state.fileLoaded && !activeTemplateTaskId;
  card.classList.toggle('collapsed', collapsed);
  toggleBtn.textContent = collapsed ? '展开模板区' : '收起模板区';

  if (!collapsed) {
    el.innerHTML = '';
    return;
  }

  el.innerHTML = `<div class="template-compact-card">
    <div class="template-compact-main">
      <strong>${state.directFlow ? '直接提交流程' : '维护模式'}</strong>
      <span>${escHtml(summaryBits.join(' · ') || '已进入商品维护流程')}</span>
    </div>
    <div class="template-compact-next">${escHtml(state.directFlow ? `无需先选模板，下一步：${state.nextLabel}` : `下一步：${state.nextLabel}`)}</div>
  </div>`;
}

function refreshTemplateFlowUi() {
  const currentProductType = ((document.getElementById('templateProductTypeInput') || {}).value || selectedTemplateType || '').trim();
  const currentVariation = ((document.getElementById('templateVariationMode') || {}).value || 'single').trim();
  if (templateSelectionValidation && (
    String(templateSelectionValidation.product_type || '').trim() !== currentProductType
    || String(templateSelectionValidation.variation_mode || '').trim() !== currentVariation
  )) {
    templateSelectionValidation = null;
  }
  renderTemplateStepper();
  renderTemplateCompactSummary();
  renderTemplateSelectionStatus();
}

function renderTemplateCandidateList(containerId, candidates, mode = 'auto') {
  const container = document.getElementById(containerId);
  if (!container) return;
  if (!candidates || candidates.length === 0) {
    container.innerHTML = '';
    return;
  }
  container.innerHTML = candidates.map(item => {
    const productType = item.product_type || '';
    const active = productType === selectedTemplateType ? 'active' : '';
    const score = item.score ? ` · ${(Number(item.score) * 100).toFixed(0)}%` : '';
    const sourceTag = mode === 'manual'
      ? `<span class="template-candidate-source">手动搜索</span>`
      : `<span class="template-candidate-source">自动推荐</span>`;
    return `<button class="template-candidate-chip ${active}" onclick="chooseTemplateCandidate('${escHtml(productType)}')">
      <strong>${escHtml(item.display_name || productType)}</strong>
      <span>${escHtml(productType)}${escHtml(score)}</span>
      ${sourceTag}
    </button>`;
  }).join('');
}

function renderTemplateCandidates() {
  renderTemplateCandidateList('templateCandidates', templateCandidates, 'auto');
  renderTemplateCandidateList('templateManualCandidates', templateManualCandidates, 'manual');
}

function renderTemplateRecommendationSummary() {
  const el = document.getElementById('templateRecommendationSummary');
  if (!el) return;
  const state = templateRecommendationState;
  if (!state) {
    el.innerHTML = '';
    return;
  }
  const tone = state.candidates && state.candidates.length > 0
    ? (state.confidence === 'high' ? 'success' : 'warn')
    : 'danger';
  const sourceLabel = {
    keyword: '关键词',
    title: '标题',
    url_title: '页面标题',
    url_slug: '链接关键词',
    manual_search: '手动搜索',
    heuristic: '兜底猜测',
    empty: '未识别',
  }[state.source] || state.source || '未识别';
  const headline = state.candidates && state.candidates.length > 0
    ? `系统已找到 ${state.candidates.length} 个 Amazon 官方候选模板`
    : '系统还没拿到可靠模板，请改用手动搜索官方类目';
  const bodyParts = [];
  if (state.title) bodyParts.push(`识别到的标题：${state.title}`);
  if (state.query) bodyParts.push(`用于搜索的关键词：${state.query}`);
  bodyParts.push(`推荐来源：${sourceLabel}`);
  if (state.warning) bodyParts.push(state.warning);
  el.innerHTML = `<div class="template-hint-card ${tone}">
    <div class="template-hint-title">${escHtml(headline)}</div>
    <div class="template-hint-body">${bodyParts.map(part => `<div>${escHtml(part)}</div>`).join('')}</div>
  </div>`;
}

function renderTemplateSelectionStatus() {
  const el = document.getElementById('templateSelectionStatus');
  if (!el) return;
  const productType = ((document.getElementById('templateProductTypeInput') || {}).value || selectedTemplateType || '').trim();
  if (!productType && !templateSelectionValidation) {
    el.innerHTML = '';
    return;
  }
  const validation = templateSelectionValidation;
  const tone = !productType ? 'warn' : (validation?.usable ? 'success' : (validation ? 'danger' : 'warn'));
  const title = !productType
    ? '还没有确认最终模板'
    : (validation?.usable ? '当前模板可直接生成' : (validation ? '当前模板还不能直接用' : '当前模板待检查'));
  const body = [];
  if (productType) body.push(`当前 product_type：${productType}`);
  if (validation?.variation_mode) body.push(`模板结构：${validation.variation_mode}`);
  if (validation?.required_total !== undefined) body.push(`必填字段数：${validation.required_total}`);
  if (validation?.message) body.push(validation.message);
  else if (productType) body.push('建议先点击“检查当前模板”，确认这是可直接生成的 Amazon 官方模板。');
  el.innerHTML = `<div class="template-selection-card ${tone}">
    <div class="template-selection-title">${escHtml(title)}</div>
    <div class="template-selection-body">
      ${body.map(part => `<div>${escHtml(part)}</div>`).join('')}
      ${validation?.usable ? `<div class="template-selection-grid">
        <div class="template-selection-item"><span class="template-selection-label">Marketplace</span><strong class="template-selection-value">${escHtml(validation.marketplace || 'US')}</strong></div>
        <div class="template-selection-item"><span class="template-selection-label">Variation</span><strong class="template-selection-value">${escHtml(validation.variation_mode || 'single')}</strong></div>
        <div class="template-selection-item"><span class="template-selection-label">Template ID</span><strong class="template-selection-value">${escHtml(validation.template_id || '-')}</strong></div>
      </div>` : ''}
    </div>
  </div>`;
}

function resetTemplateRecommendationState() {
  templateRecommendationState = null;
  templateCandidates = [];
  templateManualCandidates = [];
  selectedTemplateType = '';
  templateSelectionValidation = null;
  const input = document.getElementById('templateProductTypeInput');
  if (input) input.value = '';
  renderTemplateRecommendationSummary();
  renderTemplateCandidates();
  renderTemplateSelectionStatus();
  refreshTemplateFlowUi();
}

function chooseTemplateCandidate(productType) {
  selectedTemplateType = productType || '';
  const input = document.getElementById('templateProductTypeInput');
  if (input) input.value = selectedTemplateType;
  templateSelectionValidation = null;
  renderTemplateCandidates();
  renderTemplateSelectionStatus();
  refreshTemplateFlowUi();
}

function renderTemplateTaskStatus(task) {
  const el = document.getElementById('templateTaskStatus');
  if (!el) return;
  if (!task) {
    el.innerHTML = '';
    refreshTemplateFlowUi();
    return;
  }
  const total = Number(task.total || 0);
  const progress = Number(task.progress || 0);
  const percent = total > 0 ? Math.max(0, Math.min(100, Math.round((progress / total) * 100))) : 20;
  const detail = task.current_item || task.message || '';
  const statusText = task.stage_name || task.status || '处理中';
  el.innerHTML = `<div class="template-task-card">
    <div class="template-task-stage">${escHtml(statusText)}</div>
    <div class="template-task-meta">${escHtml(detail)}</div>
    <div class="template-progress-bar"><span style="width:${percent}%"></span></div>
    <div class="template-task-meta" style="margin-top:8px;">${escHtml(String(progress || 0))}/${escHtml(String(total || 0 || 1))}</div>
  </div>`;
  refreshTemplateFlowUi();
}

function renderTemplateResult(result) {
  const el = document.getElementById('templateResultBox');
  if (!el) return;
  if (!result) {
    el.innerHTML = '';
    refreshTemplateFlowUi();
    return;
  }
  if (result.results) {
    workspaceTemplateSummary = result.template || workspaceTemplateSummary;
    el.innerHTML = `<div class="template-result-card">
      <div class="template-task-stage">模板自动诊断完成</div>
      <div class="template-result-grid">
        <div class="template-result-item"><span class="template-result-label">总 SKU</span><strong class="template-result-value">${escHtml(String(result.total || 0))}</strong></div>
        <div class="template-result-item"><span class="template-result-label">通过</span><strong class="template-result-value">${escHtml(String(result.pass || 0))}</strong></div>
        <div class="template-result-item"><span class="template-result-label">警告</span><strong class="template-result-value">${escHtml(String(result.warn || 0))}</strong></div>
        <div class="template-result-item"><span class="template-result-label">失败</span><strong class="template-result-value">${escHtml(String(result.fail || 0))}</strong></div>
      </div>
      ${(result.template && result.template.template_id) ? `<div class="template-task-meta">模板：${escHtml(result.template.product_type || '')} · ${escHtml(result.template.variation_mode || 'single')}</div>` : ''}
      ${(result.column_issues && result.column_issues.length) ? `<div class="template-task-meta">模板列问题：${escHtml(result.column_issues.map(item => item.message).join('；'))}</div>` : ''}
    </div>`;
    refreshTemplateFlowUi();
    return;
  }

  workspaceTemplateSummary = {
    ...(workspaceTemplateSummary || {}),
    template_id: result.template_id || workspaceTemplateSummary?.template_id || '',
    product_type: result.product_type || workspaceTemplateSummary?.product_type || '',
    variation_mode: result.variation_mode || workspaceTemplateSummary?.variation_mode || 'single',
    required_total: result.required_total || workspaceTemplateSummary?.required_total || 0,
    column_count: result.column_count || workspaceTemplateSummary?.column_count || 0,
  };
  el.innerHTML = `<div class="template-result-card">
    <div class="template-task-stage">官方模板已生成</div>
    <div class="template-result-grid">
      <div class="template-result-item"><span class="template-result-label">产品类型</span><strong class="template-result-value">${escHtml(result.product_type || '')}</strong></div>
      <div class="template-result-item"><span class="template-result-label">模板结构</span><strong class="template-result-value">${escHtml(result.variation_mode || 'single')}</strong></div>
      <div class="template-result-item"><span class="template-result-label">必填字段</span><strong class="template-result-value">${escHtml(String(result.required_total || 0))}</strong></div>
      <div class="template-result-item"><span class="template-result-label">总列数</span><strong class="template-result-value">${escHtml(String(result.column_count || 0))}</strong></div>
    </div>
    ${result.download_url ? `<div class="template-task-meta" style="margin-top:12px;"><a class="btn-link" href="${escHtml(result.download_url)}">下载模板 Excel</a></div>` : ''}
  </div>`;
  refreshTemplateFlowUi();
}

async function pollTaskDetail(taskId, onComplete) {
  if (!taskId) return;
  activeTemplateTaskId = taskId;
  try {
    const response = await fetch('/api/tasks/' + encodeURIComponent(taskId));
    const task = await response.json();
    if (task.error) throw new Error(task.error);
    renderTemplateTaskStatus(task);
    loadTaskCenter();
    if (task.status === 'completed') {
      activeTemplateTaskId = '';
      renderTemplateTaskStatus(null);
      renderTemplateResult(task.result || {});
      if (typeof onComplete === 'function') onComplete(task.result || {});
      return;
    }
    if (task.status === 'failed') {
      activeTemplateTaskId = '';
      showToast('error', task.error || task.message || '任务失败');
      return;
    }
    setTimeout(() => pollTaskDetail(taskId, onComplete), 1200);
  } catch (e) {
    activeTemplateTaskId = '';
    showToast('error', '任务查询失败: ' + e.message);
  }
}

async function recommendTemplate() {
  const source = (document.getElementById('templateSourceInput') || {}).value || '';
  const keyword = (document.getElementById('templateKeywordInput') || {}).value || '';
  if (!source && !keyword) return showToast('warning', '请先输入商品链接、标题或关键词');
  try {
    templateCandidates = [];
    templateManualCandidates = [];
    selectedTemplateType = '';
    templateSelectionValidation = null;
    const response = await fetch('/api/templates/recommend', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        source_url: source,
        title: source && !/^https?:\/\//i.test(source) ? source : '',
        keyword
      })
    });
    const data = await response.json();
    if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
    templateRecommendationState = data;
    templateCandidates = data.candidates || [];
    templateManualCandidates = [];
    renderTemplateRecommendationSummary();
    if (templateCandidates.length > 0) {
      chooseTemplateCandidate(templateCandidates[0].product_type || '');
      if (data.warning) showToast('warning', data.warning);
      await validateSelectedTemplate({ silentSuccess: true });
    } else {
      const input = document.getElementById('templateProductTypeInput');
      if (input) input.value = '';
      renderTemplateCandidates();
      renderTemplateSelectionStatus();
      showToast('warning', data.warning || '未找到官方候选类目，请手动搜索或填写 product_type');
    }
  } catch (e) {
    showToast('error', '类目推荐失败: ' + e.message);
  }
}

async function searchOfficialTemplate() {
  const keyword = (document.getElementById('templateManualSearchInput') || {}).value || '';
  if (!keyword.trim()) return showToast('warning', '请先输入官方类目关键词');
  try {
    const response = await fetch('/api/templates/manual-search', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ keyword })
    });
    const data = await response.json();
    if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
    templateManualCandidates = data.candidates || [];
    templateRecommendationState = data;
    renderTemplateRecommendationSummary();
    renderTemplateCandidates();
    if (templateManualCandidates.length === 0) {
      showToast('warning', data.warning || '没有找到匹配的官方类目，请换个关键词');
    } else {
      chooseTemplateCandidate(templateManualCandidates[0].product_type || '');
      await validateSelectedTemplate({ silentSuccess: true });
      showToast('success', `已找到 ${templateManualCandidates.length} 个官方类目候选`);
    }
  } catch (e) {
    showToast('error', '官方类目搜索失败: ' + e.message);
  }
}

async function validateSelectedTemplate(options = {}) {
  const input = document.getElementById('templateProductTypeInput');
  const variationInput = document.getElementById('templateVariationMode');
  const productType = ((input && input.value) || selectedTemplateType || '').trim();
  const variationMode = ((variationInput && variationInput.value) || 'single').trim();
  if (!productType) {
    templateSelectionValidation = null;
    renderTemplateSelectionStatus();
    return showToast('warning', '请先选择或填写 product_type');
  }
  try {
    const response = await fetch('/api/templates/validate', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ product_type: productType, variation_mode: variationMode, marketplace: 'US' })
    });
    const data = await response.json();
    if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
    templateSelectionValidation = data;
    renderTemplateSelectionStatus();
    if (!options.silentSuccess || !data.usable) {
      showToast(data.usable ? 'success' : 'warning', data.message || (data.usable ? '模板可用' : '模板不可用'));
    }
    return data;
  } catch (e) {
    templateSelectionValidation = { usable: false, message: e.message, product_type: productType, variation_mode: variationMode, marketplace: 'US' };
    renderTemplateSelectionStatus();
    showToast('error', '模板检查失败: ' + e.message);
    return templateSelectionValidation;
  }
}

async function generateTemplateTask() {
  const input = document.getElementById('templateProductTypeInput');
  const variationInput = document.getElementById('templateVariationMode');
  const productType = ((input && input.value) || selectedTemplateType || '').trim();
  const variationMode = ((variationInput && variationInput.value) || 'single').trim();
  if (!productType) return showToast('warning', '请先选择或填写 product_type');
  try {
    const validation = await validateSelectedTemplate({ silentSuccess: true });
    if (!validation || !validation.usable) {
      return showToast('warning', validation?.message || '当前模板还不可用，请先确认类目');
    }
    setTemplatePanelCollapsed(false);
    renderTemplateResult(null);
    const response = await fetch('/api/templates/generate', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ product_type: productType, variation_mode: variationMode })
    });
    const data = await response.json();
    if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
    showToast('info', '正在生成官方模板...');
    pollTaskDetail(data.task_id, (result) => {
