      if (result && result.download_url) showToast('success', '模板生成完成，可直接下载');
    });
  } catch (e) {
    showToast('error', '模板生成失败: ' + e.message);
  }
}

function uploadTemplateFile(file) {
  if (!file) return;
  setTemplatePanelCollapsed(true);
  const fd = new FormData();
  fd.append('file', file);
  if (selectedAccountId) fd.append('account_id', selectedAccountId);
  fetch('/api/template-upload', { method: 'POST', body: fd })
    .then(r => r.json())
    .then(d => {
      if (d.error) throw new Error(d.error);
      currentFile = d.filepath || d.filename || file.name;
      localStorage.setItem('amazon28_currentFile', currentFile);
      workspaceTemplateSummary = d.template || null;
      currentFileMeta = { type: (d.filename || '').toLowerCase().endsWith('.xls') ? 'xls' : 'xlsx', warning: '', xlsPreserveSupported: true };
      const fileInfo = document.getElementById('fileInfo');
      if (fileInfo) {
        fileInfo.dataset.baseName = d.filename || file.name;
        fileInfo.textContent = d.filename || file.name;
      }
      const uploadInfo = document.getElementById('templateUploadInfo');
      if (uploadInfo) uploadInfo.textContent = (d.template && d.template.template_id) ? `模板 ${d.template.product_type || ''} 已识别，正在自动诊断...` : '已上传，正在自动诊断...';
      showToast('info', '模板文件已上传，正在自动诊断');
      loadProducts();
      pollTaskDetail(d.task_id, () => {
        loadProducts();
        showToast('success', '模板诊断完成，请查看缺项诊断与预览状态');
      });
    })
    .catch(e => showToast('error', '模板上传失败: ' + e.message));
  const input = document.getElementById('templateUploadInput');
  if (input) input.value = '';
}

// ===== 6. Excel Upload =====
function workspaceHasProtectedProgress() {
  if (!currentFile) return false;
  if (products.length === 0) return true;
  return products.some(product => {
    const hasAi = ['ai_title', 'ai_description', 'ai_keywords', 'ai_main_image', 'ai_image_url'].some(key => String(product[key] || '').trim());
    const hasWorkflow = ['preview_status', 'submit_status', 'asin', 'listing_check_status', 'validation_status'].some(key => String(product[key] || '').trim() && String(product[key] || '').trim() !== 'PENDING');
    return hasAi || hasWorkflow;
  });
}

function confirmPendingExcelUpload() {
  const file = pendingExcelUploadFile;
  pendingExcelUploadFile = null;
  closeModal();
  if (file) uploadExcel(file, { confirmed: true });
}

function cancelPendingExcelUpload() {
  pendingExcelUploadFile = null;
  const input = document.getElementById('fileInput');
  if (input) input.value = '';
  closeModal();
}

function uploadExcel(file, options = {}) {
  if (!file) return;
  if (!options.confirmed && workspaceHasProtectedProgress()) {
    pendingExcelUploadFile = file;
    const currentName = (document.getElementById('fileInfo')?.dataset.baseName || currentFile.split(/[\\/]/).pop() || currentFile);
    showModal('确认切换商品表', `<div class="customer-quick-start">
      <div class="quick-start-step">
        <strong>你已经有正在处理的商品表</strong>
        <p>当前表：${escHtml(currentName)}。新导入 ${escHtml(file.name)} 会切换工作区，不会自动合并旧表里的 AI 结果、预览结果和提交结果。</p>
      </div>
      <ul class="customer-block-list">
        <li>如果只是想继续刚才的工作，请点“取消”，不要重复导入同一个 Excel。</li>
        <li>如果确定要换一张新表，请点“确认导入”。旧文件仍在输入目录中，不会被物理覆盖。</li>
      </ul>
    </div>`);
    document.getElementById('modalFooter').innerHTML = `
      <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="confirmPendingExcelUpload()">确认导入新表</button>
      <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="cancelPendingExcelUpload()">取消</button>`;
    return;
  }
  setTemplatePanelCollapsed(true);
  const fd = new FormData();
  fd.append('file', file);
  showToast('info', '正在上传: ' + file.name);
  fetch('/api/upload', { method: 'POST', body: fd })
    .then(r => { if (!r.ok) throw new Error('HTTP ' + r.status); return r.json(); })
    .then(d => {
      if (d.error) return showToast('error', d.error);
      currentFile = d.filepath || d.filename || file.name;
      currentFileVersion = Number(d.file_version || 0);
      localStorage.setItem('amazon28_currentFile', currentFile);
      currentFileMeta = {
        type: d.file_type || '',
        warning: d.warning || '',
        xlsPreserveSupported: !!d.xls_preserve_supported,
      };
      workspaceTemplateSummary = null;
      selectedSkus.clear();
      expandedParents.clear();
      document.getElementById('fileInfo').dataset.baseName = d.filename || file.name;
      document.getElementById('fileInfo').textContent = d.filename || file.name;
      renderFileHealth();
      showToast('success', '上传成功');
      if (d.warning) showToast('warning', d.warning);
      loadProducts();
      loadTaskCenter();
      refreshSetupStatus({ showFirstRun: false });
    })
    .catch(e => showToast('error', '上传失败: ' + e.message));
  document.getElementById('fileInput').value = '';
}

// ===== 7. Load Products =====
function loadProducts() {
  if (!currentFile) return;
  // Preserve validation states before reload
  const validationMap = new Map();
  products.forEach(p => {
    if (p._validPass !== undefined || (p._validErrors && p._validErrors.length > 0) || (p._validWarnings && p._validWarnings.length > 0)) {
      validationMap.set(p.sku, {
        _validPass: p._validPass,
        _validErrors: p._validErrors,
        _validWarnings: p._validWarnings,
      });
    }
  });
  // Clear search box
  const searchInput = document.getElementById('searchInput');
  if (searchInput) searchInput.value = '';
  searchQuery = '';

  // Show loading spinner
  const loadingEl = document.getElementById('tableLoading');
  const tableWrap = document.getElementById('tableWrap');
  if (loadingEl) loadingEl.style.display = 'flex';
  if (tableWrap) tableWrap.style.display = 'none';

  fetch('/api/products?file=' + encodeURIComponent(currentFile))
    .then(r => { if (!r.ok) throw new Error('HTTP ' + r.status); return r.json(); })
    .then(d => {
      if (loadingEl) loadingEl.style.display = 'none';
      if (tableWrap) tableWrap.style.display = '';
      if (d.error) return showToast('error', d.error);
      currentFileVersion = Number(d.file_version || 0);
      products = flattenProducts(d.products || []);
      workspaceTemplateSummary = d.template || null;
      mergeListingStatusIntoProducts();
      refreshPreviewAccountHints();
      if (!document.getElementById('fileInfo').dataset.baseName) {
        document.getElementById('fileInfo').dataset.baseName = currentFile.split(/[\\/]/).pop() || currentFile;
      }
      document.getElementById('fileInfo').textContent = document.getElementById('fileInfo').dataset.baseName || '';
      // Restore validation states: first from server data, then from memory
      products.forEach(p => {
        hydratePersistedDiagnosticData(p);
        // Server-persisted validation
        const persistedErrors = (p.validation_errors || '').split('; ').filter(Boolean);
        const persistedWarnings = (p.validation_warnings || '').split('; ').filter(Boolean);
        if (p.validation_status === 'pass') {
          p._validPass = true;
          p._validErrors = [];
          p._validWarnings = [];
        } else if (p.validation_status === 'warn') {
          p._validPass = true;
          p._validErrors = [];
          p._validWarnings = persistedWarnings;
        } else if (p.validation_status === 'fail') {
          p._validPass = false;
          p._validErrors = persistedErrors;
          p._validWarnings = persistedWarnings;
        }
        // Memory-cached validation takes precedence
        const saved = validationMap.get(p.sku);
        if (saved) {
          p._validPass = saved._validPass;
          p._validErrors = saved._validErrors;
          p._validWarnings = saved._validWarnings || [];
        }
      });
      refreshPreviewAccountHints();
      syncSelectionState();
      applyFilter();
      updateStats();
      updateWorkspaceContext(d.template || {});
      enableToolbar(products.length > 0);
      if (!activeTemplateTaskId && d.template && d.template.template_id) {
        renderTemplateResult(d.template);
      } else {
        refreshTemplateFlowUi();
      }
      renderFileHealth();
      loadTaskCenter();
      if (drawerProduct) {
        const refreshed = products.find(item => item.sku === drawerProduct.sku);
        if (refreshed) {
          drawerProduct = refreshed;
          renderDrawerContent();
        }
      }
      const trackedSkus = products
        .filter(p => p.parentage_level !== 'parent' && ((p.submit_status && p.submit_status !== 'PENDING') || p.asin))
        .map(p => p.sku);
      if (trackedSkus.length > 0) refreshListingStatuses(trackedSkus, { rounds: 1, intervalMs: 1500 });
    })
    .catch(e => {
      if (loadingEl) loadingEl.style.display = 'none';
      if (tableWrap) tableWrap.style.display = '';
      showToast('error', '加载失败: ' + e.message);
    });
}

function flattenProducts(groups) {
  const flat = [];
  // Build a set of parent_sku values from "parent" type groups
  // so we can skip standalone rows that are actually parent rows
  const parentSkuSet = new Set();
  groups.forEach(g => {
    if (g.type === 'parent') parentSkuSet.add(g.parent_sku);
  });

  groups.forEach(g => {
    const skus = g.skus || [];

    // Skip standalone rows whose SKU matches a parent group
    // (these are parent rows in Excel that got separated)
    if (g.type === 'standalone' && skus.length === 1 && parentSkuSet.has(skus[0].sku)) {
      return;
    }

    if (g.type === 'parent' && skus.length >= 1) {
      // Find matching standalone parent row for title/brand
      const parentRow = groups.find(og =>
        og.type === 'standalone' && og.skus && og.skus[0] && og.skus[0].sku === g.parent_sku
      );
      const parentSource = (parentRow && parentRow.skus && parentRow.skus[0]) || skus[0] || {};
      const parentTitle = (parentRow && parentRow.title) || g.title || skus[0].title || '';
      const parentBrand = (parentRow && parentRow.brand) || g.brand || '';

      // Parent row
      flat.push({
        ...parentSource,
        sku: g.parent_sku,
        title: parentTitle,
        item_name: parentTitle,
        brand: parentBrand,
        parentage_level: 'parent',
        parent_sku: '',
        variation_theme: g.variation_theme || '',
        main_image_url: parentSource.main_image_url || skus[0].main_image_url || '',
        price: '',
        quantity: '',
        ai_status: parentSource.ai_status || '',
        submit_status: parentSource.submit_status || '',
        _raw: parentSource._raw || {},
      });
      // Child rows
      skus.forEach(s => {
        flat.push({
          ...s,
          parentage_level: 'child',
          parent_sku: g.parent_sku,
          brand: parentBrand || s.brand || '',
          variation_theme: g.variation_theme || '',
        });
      });
    } else {
      // Standalone product (single SKU, no parent group)
      const s = skus[0] || {};
      flat.push({
        ...s,
        brand: g.brand || s.brand || '',
        variation_theme: g.variation_theme || '',
        parentage_level: '',
        parent_sku: '',
      });
    }
  });
  return flat;
}

function mergeListingStatusIntoProducts() {
  products.forEach(p => {
    const live = listingStatusMap.get(p.sku);
    if (!live) return;
    p.live_asin = live.asin || p.asin || '';
    p.submission_route = live.route || p.submission_route || 'unknown';
    p.final_listing_status = live.final_status || '';
    p.discoverable = !!live.discoverable;
    p.listing_issue_count = Number(live.issue_count || 0);
    p.offer_count = Number(live.offer_count || 0);
    p.fulfillment_count = Number(live.fulfillment_count || 0);
    p.listing_status_values = live.status || [];
    p.listing_live_issues = live.issues || [];
  });
}

function applyRecentSubmitHighlights() {
  if (!recentSubmitHighlights || recentSubmitHighlights.size === 0) return;
  let firstRow = null;
  recentSubmitHighlights.forEach(sku => {
    const row = document.querySelector(`tr[data-sku="${sku}"]`);
    if (!row) return;
    row.classList.add('selected');
    row.classList.add('recent-submit-row');
    if (!firstRow) firstRow = row;
  });
  if (recentSubmitScrollPending && firstRow) {
    firstRow.scrollIntoView({ block: 'center', behavior: 'smooth' });
    recentSubmitScrollPending = false;
  }
}

function updateWorkspaceContext(summary) {
  if (summary !== undefined) {
    workspaceTemplateSummary = (summary && Object.keys(summary).length > 0) ? summary : null;
  }
  const fileEl = document.getElementById('ctxFile');
  const accountEl = document.getElementById('ctxAccount');
  const templateEl = document.getElementById('ctxTemplate');
  const typeEl = document.getElementById('ctxProductType');
  if (fileEl) fileEl.textContent = (document.getElementById('fileInfo')?.dataset.baseName) || '未加载';
  const account = amazonAccounts.find(account => account.seller_id === selectedAccountId)
    || amazonAccounts.find(account => account.is_default)
    || amazonAccounts[0];
  if (accountEl) accountEl.textContent = account ? (account.name || account.seller_id) : '未选择';
  if (templateEl) templateEl.textContent = (summary && summary.template_id) || '未使用';
  if (typeEl) typeEl.textContent = (summary && summary.product_type) || '-';
  refreshTemplateFlowUi();
}

async function fetchListingStatusFor(file, sku, accountId = '') {
  const params = new URLSearchParams({
    file,
    sku,
    account_id: accountId || '',
  });
  const response = await fetch('/api/listing-status?' + params.toString());
  const data = await response.json();
  if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
  return data.listing || {};
}

async function fetchListingStatus(sku) {
  return fetchListingStatusFor(currentFile, sku, selectedAccountId || '');
}

async function refreshListingStatuses(skus, options = {}) {
  const targets = (skus || []).filter(Boolean);
  if (!currentFile || targets.length === 0) return;
  const rounds = options.rounds || 1;
  const intervalMs = options.intervalMs || 2500;
  for (let round = 0; round < rounds; round++) {
    for (const sku of targets) {
      try {
        const listing = await fetchListingStatus(sku);
        listingStatusMap.set(sku, listing);
      } catch (e) {
        console.warn('listing status fetch failed', sku, e);
      }
    }
    mergeListingStatusIntoProducts();
    updateStats();
    renderTable();
    if (round < rounds - 1) await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, intervalMs));
  }
}

function enableToolbar(enabled) {
  const aiReady = !!setupStatus?.ai?.ready;
  const amazonReady = !!setupStatus?.amazon?.ready;
  const locks = {
    btnBatchCopy: enabled && aiReady ? '' : (enabled ? 'AI 还没配置好：去设置页填 Key 并保存' : '先导入 Excel'),
    btnBatchImg: enabled && aiReady ? '' : (enabled ? 'AI 还没配置好：去设置页填 Key 并保存' : '先导入 Excel'),
    btnValidate: enabled ? '' : '先导入 Excel',
    btnListingCheck: enabled && amazonReady ? '' : (enabled ? 'Amazon 账号还没配置好：先添加账号' : '先导入 Excel'),
    btnExport: enabled ? '' : '先导入 Excel',
    btnComparison: enabled ? '' : '先导入 Excel',
  };
  Object.entries(locks).forEach(([id, reason]) => {
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (!el) return;
    el.disabled = !!reason;
    el.title = reason || '';
    el.classList.toggle('toolbar-locked', !!reason);
  });
  updateSubmitAvailability();
  const submitBtn = document.getElementById('btnSubmit');
  if (submitBtn && enabled && !amazonReady) {
    submitBtn.disabled = true;
    submitBtn.title = 'Amazon 账号还没配置好：先添加账号';
    submitBtn.classList.add('toolbar-locked');
  } else if (submitBtn && !submitBtn.disabled) {
    submitBtn.title = '';
    submitBtn.classList.remove('toolbar-locked');
  }
}

// ===== 8. Stats =====
function updateStats() {
  let total = 0, processed = 0, pending = 0, errors = 0, previewPass = 0, previewFail = 0;
  let submitted = 0, asinCount = 0, discoverableCount = 0;
  products.forEach(p => {
    if (p.parentage_level === 'parent') return;
    total++;
    const st = p.ai_status || '';
    const previewStatus = String(p.preview_status || '').toUpperCase();
    if (st === 'completed' || st === 'done') processed++;
    else pending++;
    if ((p._validErrors && p._validErrors.length > 0) || hasTemplateBlockingIssues(p)) errors++;
    if (previewStatus === 'VALID') previewPass++;
    else if (previewStatus) previewFail++;
    if (p.submit_status && p.submit_status !== 'PENDING') submitted++;
    if ((p.live_asin || p.asin)) asinCount++;
    if (p.discoverable || p.final_listing_status === 'discoverable') discoverableCount++;
  });
  document.getElementById('statTotal').textContent = total;
  document.getElementById('statProcessed').textContent = processed;
  document.getElementById('statPending').textContent = pending;
  document.getElementById('statErrors').textContent = errors;
  const submittedEl = document.getElementById('statSubmitted');
  const asinEl = document.getElementById('statAsin');
  const discoverableEl = document.getElementById('statDiscoverable');
  if (submittedEl) submittedEl.textContent = submitted;
  if (asinEl) asinEl.textContent = asinCount;
  if (discoverableEl) discoverableEl.textContent = discoverableCount;
  // Filter counts
  document.getElementById('filterCountAll').textContent = total;
  document.getElementById('filterCountPending').textContent = pending;
  document.getElementById('filterCountProcessed').textContent = processed;
  const validCount = products.filter(p => p.parentage_level !== 'parent' && p._validPass).length;
  document.getElementById('filterCountValid').textContent = validCount;
  document.getElementById('filterCountError').textContent = errors;
  const previewPassEl = document.getElementById('filterCountPreviewPass');
  const previewFailEl = document.getElementById('filterCountPreviewFail');
  if (previewPassEl) previewPassEl.textContent = previewPass;
  if (previewFailEl) previewFailEl.textContent = previewFail;
  updateSubmitAvailability();
  updateToolbarRecommendation();
  renderCustomerFlow();
}

// ===== 9. Filter & Search =====
function filterByStatus(status) {
  currentFilter = status;
  currentPage = 1;
  document.querySelectorAll('.filter-tab').forEach(t => {
    t.classList.toggle('active', t.getAttribute('data-filter') === status);
  });
  applyFilter();
}

function filterTable(query) {
  searchQuery = query.toLowerCase().trim();
  currentPage = 1;
  applyFilter();
}

function applyFilter() {
  filteredProducts = [];
  const parentMap = {};
  // Build parent map
  products.forEach(p => {
    if (p.parentage_level === 'parent') parentMap[p.sku] = [];
  });
  products.forEach(p => {
    if (p.parentage_level === 'child' && p.parent_sku && parentMap[p.parent_sku]) {
      parentMap[p.parent_sku].push(p);
    }
  });

  products.forEach(p => {
    // Skip children (they will be added under their parent)
    if (p.parentage_level === 'child' && p.parent_sku && parentMap[p.parent_sku]) return;

    if (p.parentage_level === 'parent') {
      const children = parentMap[p.sku] || [];
      const matchingChildren = children.filter(c => matchFilter(c) && matchSearch(c));
      if (matchingChildren.length > 0 || matchSearch(p)) {
        filteredProducts.push(p);
        const expanded = expandedParents.has(p.sku);
        if (expanded) {
          matchingChildren.forEach(c => filteredProducts.push(c));
        }
      }
    } else {
      // Independent product
      if (matchFilter(p) && matchSearch(p)) filteredProducts.push(p);
    }
  });
  syncSelectionState();
  renderTable();
}

function matchFilter(p) {
  if (currentFilter === 'all') return true;
  const st = p.ai_status || '';
  const previewStatus = String(p.preview_status || '').toUpperCase();
  if (currentFilter === 'pending') return st !== 'completed' && st !== 'done';
  if (currentFilter === 'processed') return st === 'completed' || st === 'done';
  if (currentFilter === 'valid') return p._validPass === true;
  if (currentFilter === 'error') return (p._validErrors && p._validErrors.length > 0) || hasTemplateBlockingIssues(p);
  if (currentFilter === 'previewPass') return isPreviewValidForSelectedAccount(p);
  if (currentFilter === 'previewFail') return previewStatus && !isPreviewValidForSelectedAccount(p);
  return true;
}

function matchSearch(p) {
  if (!searchQuery) return true;
  const sku = (p.sku || '').toLowerCase();
  const title = (p.title || p.item_name || '').toLowerCase();
  return sku.includes(searchQuery) || title.includes(searchQuery);
}

function renderInlineSubmissionSummary(p) {
  const submitStatus = String(p.submit_status || '').trim();
  const previewStatus = getPreviewDisplayStatus(p);
  const submissionId = String(p.submission_id || '').trim();
  const route = String(p.submission_route || '').trim();
  const pills = [];

  if (submitStatus && submitStatus.toUpperCase() !== 'PENDING') {
    pills.push(`<span class="table-meta-pill status">${escHtml(formatSubmitStatusLabel(submitStatus))}</span>`);
  } else if (previewStatus) {
    pills.push(`<span class="table-meta-pill preview">${escHtml(`预览 ${previewStatus}`)}</span>`);
  }
  if (submissionId) {
    pills.push(`<span class="table-meta-pill id">提交ID ${escHtml(compactMiddle(submissionId, 10, 8))}</span>`);
  }
  if (route && route !== 'unknown') {
    pills.push(`<span class="table-meta-pill route">${escHtml(formatSubmissionRoute(route))}</span>`);
  }

  if (pills.length === 0) return '';
  return `<div class="table-row-status">${pills.join('')}</div>`;
}

function renderWorkspaceEmptyState() {
  const empty = document.getElementById('emptyState');
  if (!empty) return;
  const titleEl = empty.querySelector('.empty-title');
  const descEl = empty.querySelector('.empty-desc');
  const actionsEl = document.getElementById('emptyActions');
  const snapshot = getCustomerFlowSnapshot();
  let title = '暂无商品数据';
  let desc = '导入 Excel 文件或生成示例 Excel 开始铺货。';
  let actions = [
    `<button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="document.getElementById('fileInput').click()">导入 Excel</button>`,
    `<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="createSampleExcel()">生成示例 Excel</button>`,
  ];

  if (!snapshot.aiReady) {
    title = '第一步：先配置 AI，不要直接导入';
    desc = '客户只需要点“一键恢复推荐”，Base URL 固定用 https://api.kk666.best，然后粘贴文字 Key 和图片 Key。';
    actions = [
      `<button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="runSetupAction('settings_ai')">去设置 AI</button>`,
      `<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="resetRecommendedAiConfig()">一键恢复推荐</button>`,
    ];
  } else if (!snapshot.amazonReady) {
    title = '第二步：添加 Amazon 账号';
    desc = '还没有可用 Seller ID、LWA Client ID/Secret、Refresh Token。没有账号就不能做 Amazon 预览和正式提交。';
    actions = [
      `<button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="runSetupAction('add_account')">添加 Amazon 账号</button>`,
      `<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="runSetupAction('self_check')">先跑一键自检</button>`,
    ];
  } else if (!currentFile) {
    title = '第三步：导入商品 Excel';
    desc = 'AI 和 Amazon 账号都准备好了。现在导入客户表格；不确定格式时先生成示例 Excel 测试。';
  } else if (products.length > 0 && filteredProducts.length === 0) {
    title = '当前筛选没有匹配商品';
    desc = '数据已经导入，但当前筛选条件下没有行。切回“全部”或清空搜索关键词即可看到商品。';
    actions = [
      `<button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="filterByStatus('all')">查看全部商品</button>`,
      `<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="document.getElementById('searchInput').value=''; searchQuery=''; applyFilter();">清空搜索</button>`,
    ];
  }

  if (titleEl) titleEl.textContent = title;
  if (descEl) descEl.textContent = desc;
  if (actionsEl) actionsEl.innerHTML = actions.join('');
}

// ===== 10. Table Rendering =====
function renderTable() {
  const tbody = document.getElementById('tableBody');
  const empty = document.getElementById('emptyState');
  const pag = document.getElementById('pagination');

  if (filteredProducts.length === 0) {
    tbody.innerHTML = '';
    renderWorkspaceEmptyState();
    empty.style.display = 'flex';
    pag.style.display = 'none';
    return;
  }
  empty.style.display = 'none';

  // Pagination
  const totalPages = Math.ceil(filteredProducts.length / pageSize);
  if (currentPage > totalPages) currentPage = totalPages;
  const start = (currentPage - 1) * pageSize;
  const pageItems = filteredProducts.slice(start, start + pageSize);

  pag.style.display = filteredProducts.length > pageSize ? 'flex' : 'none';
  document.getElementById('pageInfo').textContent =
    `共 ${filteredProducts.length} 条`;
  document.getElementById('pageNum').textContent =
    `${currentPage} / ${totalPages}`;
  document.getElementById('btnPrev').disabled = currentPage <= 1;
  document.getElementById('btnNext').disabled = currentPage >= totalPages;

  let rowNum = 0;
  let html = '';
  pageItems.forEach((p, idx) => {
    const sku = p.sku || '';
    const title = p.title || p.item_name || '';
    const imgUrl = resolveProductMainPreview(p) || p.ai_main_image || '';
    const price = p.price || p.standard_price || '';
    const stock = p.quantity || '';
    const isParent = p.parentage_level === 'parent';
    const isChild = p.parentage_level === 'child';
    const checked = !isParent && selectedSkus.has(sku);
    const rowClass = isChild ? 'row-child' : (checked ? 'selected' : '');
    const variantIssueSummary = getVariantIssueSummary(p);
    const family = getVariantFamilyMembers(p);
    const familyTheme = String((family.parent && family.parent.variation_theme) || p.variation_theme || '').trim();
    const childCount = family.children.length;

    if (!isChild) rowNum++;

    // AI status badge
    const aiSt = p.ai_status || '';
    let aiBadge;
    if (aiSt === 'completed' || aiSt === 'done') aiBadge = `<span class="badge badge-success">${t('ai_processed')}</span>`;
    else if (aiSt === 'processing') aiBadge = `<span class="badge badge-processing">处理中</span>`;
    else if (aiSt === 'failed') aiBadge = `<span class="badge badge-danger">失败</span>`;
    else aiBadge = `<span class="badge badge-default">${t('pending')}</span>`;

    // Validation
    let validCell;
    const templateBlockingReasons = getTemplateBlockingReasons(p);
    if (templateBlockingReasons.length > 0) validCell = `<span class="valid-fail" onclick="showValidationIssues('${escHtml(sku)}')" title="${escHtml(templateBlockingReasons.join('; '))}">&#10007;</span>`;
    else if (p._validErrors && p._validErrors.length > 0) validCell = `<span class="valid-fail" onclick="showValidationIssues('${escHtml(sku)}')" title="${escHtml(p._validErrors.join('; '))}">&#10007;</span>`;
    else if (p._validWarnings && p._validWarnings.length > 0) validCell = `<span class="valid-warn" onclick="showValidationIssues('${escHtml(sku)}')" title="${escHtml(p._validWarnings.join('; '))}">&#9888;</span>`;
    else if (p._validPass === true) validCell = '<span class="valid-pass">&#10003;</span>';
    else validCell = '<span class="valid-none">-</span>';

    // SKU cell
    let skuCell;
    if (isParent) {
      const exp = expandedParents.has(sku);
      skuCell = `<div class="sku-cell sku-cell-parent">
        <span class="sku-toggle ${exp?'expanded':''}" onclick="toggleParent('${escHtml(sku)}')">&#9654;</span>
        <span class="sku-text">${escHtml(sku)}</span>
        <span class="sku-type-badge sku-badge-parent">Parent</span>
        ${familyTheme ? `<span class="variant-inline-chip">${escHtml(familyTheme)}</span>` : ''}
        ${childCount > 0 ? `<span class="variant-inline-chip subtle">${childCount} 子体</span>` : ''}
        ${variantIssueSummary.count > 0 ? `<span class="variant-inline-chip danger">${variantIssueSummary.count} 问题</span>` : ''}
      </div>`;
    } else if (isChild) {
      const isLast = (idx === pageItems.length - 1) || (pageItems[idx+1] && pageItems[idx+1].parentage_level !== 'child');
      const line = isLast ? '&#9492;' : '&#9500;';
      skuCell = `<div class="sku-cell sku-child-indent">
        <span class="sku-tree-line">${line}</span>
        <span class="sku-child-text">${escHtml(sku)}</span>
        ${p.color ? `<span class="variant-inline-chip subtle">${escHtml(p.color)}</span>` : ''}
        ${p.size ? `<span class="variant-inline-chip subtle">${escHtml(p.size)}</span>` : ''}
        ${variantIssueSummary.count > 0 ? `<span class="variant-inline-chip danger">${variantIssueSummary.count} 问题</span>` : ''}
      </div>`;
    } else {
      skuCell = `<div class="sku-cell"><span class="sku-text">${escHtml(sku)}</span></div>`;
    }

    // Image cell
    const imgCell = imgUrl
      ? `<img class="img-thumb" src="${escHtml(imgUrl)}" alt="" onerror="this.style.display='none';this.nextElementSibling.style.display='flex'" onmouseenter="showImgPreview(event,'${escHtml(imgUrl)}')" onmouseleave="hideImgPreview()"><div class="img-placeholder" style="display:none">-</div>`
      : '<div class="img-placeholder">-</div>';

    // Price cell (inline edit)
    const priceDisplay = price ? `$${parseFloat(price).toFixed(2)}` : '-';
    const priceCell = isParent ? '-' : `<span class="inline-edit" ondblclick="inlineEdit(this,'price','${escHtml(sku)}')">${priceDisplay}</span>`;

    // Stock cell
    const stockDisplay = stock || '-';
    const stockCell = isParent ? '-' : `<span class="inline-edit" ondblclick="inlineEdit(this,'quantity','${escHtml(sku)}')">${stockDisplay}</span>`;

    // Optional columns
    const optCols = buildOptionalCols(p);

    // Action links
    const actions = `<div class="action-links">
      <button class="btn-link" onclick="openDrawer('${escHtml(sku)}')">${t('edit')}</button>
      <span class="action-sep">|</span>
      <button class="btn-link" onclick="processSingle('${escHtml(sku)}')">${t('ai_process')}</button>
    </div>`;

    html += `<tr class="${rowClass}" data-sku="${escHtml(sku)}">
      <td class="col-cb col-fixed-left"><input type="checkbox" ${checked?'checked':''} ${isParent ? 'disabled title="父体行不可直接处理"' : ''} onchange="toggleSelect('${escHtml(sku)}',this.checked)"></td>
      <td class="col-num col-fixed-left">${isChild ? '' : rowNum}</td>
      <td class="col-sku col-fixed-left">${skuCell}</td>
      <td class="col-title" title="${escHtml(title)}">
        <div class="title-cell">${escHtml(title)}</div>
        ${renderInlineSubmissionSummary(p)}
        ${isParent ? renderFamilyTableSummary(p) : ''}
        ${variantIssueSummary.count > 0 ? `<button type="button" class="row-issue-summary" title="${escHtml(variantIssueSummary.issues.join('；'))}" onclick="openPrimaryIssueNavigator('${escHtml(sku)}')">${escHtml(variantIssueSummary.issues[0])}</button>` : ''}
      </td>
      <td class="col-img">${imgCell}</td>
      <td class="col-price">${priceCell}</td>
      <td class="col-stock">${stockCell}</td>
      ${optCols}
      <td class="col-ai">${aiBadge}</td>
      <td class="col-valid">${validCell}</td>
      <td class="col-actions col-fixed-right">${actions}</td>
    </tr>`;
  });

  tbody.innerHTML = html;
  applyRecentSubmitHighlights();
}

function buildOptionalCols(p) {
  const cols = ['brand','productType','variantType','upc','color','size','fulfillment','previewStatus','submitStatus','submissionId','asin','route','finalStatus','listingIssues'];
  return cols.map(col => {
    const visible = visibleCols[col];
    const style = visible ? '' : 'style="display:none"';
    let val = '';
    switch(col) {
      case 'brand': val = p.brand || p.brand_name || ''; break;
      case 'productType': val = p.product_type || ''; break;
      case 'variantType': val = p.parentage_level || ''; break;
      case 'upc': val = p.upc || p.ean || p.product_id || ''; break;
      case 'color': val = p.color || p.color_name || ''; break;
      case 'size': val = p.size || p.size_name || ''; break;
      case 'fulfillment': val = p.fulfillment_channel || ''; break;
      case 'previewStatus': val = getPreviewDisplayStatus(p) || ''; break;
      case 'submitStatus': val = formatSubmitStatusLabel(p.submit_status || ''); break;
      case 'submissionId': val = compactMiddle(p.submission_id || '', 10, 8); break;
      case 'asin': val = p.live_asin || p.asin || ''; break;
      case 'route': val = formatSubmissionRoute(p.submission_route || 'unknown'); break;
      case 'finalStatus': val = formatFinalListingStatus(p.final_listing_status || ''); break;
      case 'listingIssues': val = String(p.listing_issue_count || 0); break;
    }
    return `<td class="col-optional" data-col="${col}" ${style}>${escHtml(val)}</td>`;
  }).join('');
}

// ===== 11. Pagination =====
function goPage(dir) {
  const totalPages = Math.ceil(filteredProducts.length / pageSize);
  if (dir === 'prev' && currentPage > 1) currentPage--;
  else if (dir === 'next' && currentPage < totalPages) currentPage++;
  renderTable();
}
function changePageSize(val) {
  pageSize = parseInt(val) || 50;
  currentPage = 1;
  renderTable();
}

// ===== 12. Selection =====
function toggleSelect(sku, checked) {
  const product = products.find(x => x.sku === sku);
  if (!product || product.parentage_level === 'parent') return;
  if (checked) selectedSkus.add(sku);
  else selectedSkus.delete(sku);
  updateBatchBar();
  const row = document.querySelector(`tr[data-sku="${sku}"]`);
  if (row) row.classList.toggle('selected', checked);
}
function toggleSelectAll(checked) {
  getFilteredActionableSkus().forEach(sku => {
    if (checked) selectedSkus.add(sku);
    else selectedSkus.delete(sku);
  });
  filteredProducts.forEach(p => {
    if (p.parentage_level === 'parent') return;
    if (checked) selectedSkus.add(p.sku);
    else selectedSkus.delete(p.sku);
  });
  updateBatchBar();
  renderTable();
}
function clearSelection() {
  selectedSkus.clear();
  const selectAllCb = document.getElementById('selectAllCb');
  if (selectAllCb) {
    selectAllCb.checked = false;
    selectAllCb.indeterminate = false;
  }
  updateBatchBar();
  renderTable();
}
function updateBatchBar() {
  const bar = document.getElementById('batchBar');
  const rawCount = selectedSkus.size;
  const actionableCount = getSelectedActionableSkus().length;
  document.getElementById('selectedCount').textContent = actionableCount;
  const rawCountEl = document.getElementById('selectedRawCount');
  const noteEl = document.getElementById('selectedNote');
  if (rawCountEl) rawCountEl.textContent = rawCount;
  if (noteEl) {
    const ignored = rawCount - actionableCount;
    noteEl.textContent = ignored > 0 ? `（已忽略 ${ignored} 个无效/父体/阻断 SKU）` : '';
  }
  bar.classList.toggle('hidden', actionableCount === 0);
  updateToolbarRecommendation();
}

// ===== 13. Column Settings =====
function initializeColumnVisibility() {
  visibleCols = { ...DEFAULT_VISIBLE_COLS };
  document.querySelectorAll('#colSettingsPanel input[data-col]').forEach(input => {
    const col = input.getAttribute('data-col');
    const visible = !!visibleCols[col];
    input.checked = visible;
    document.querySelectorAll(`[data-col="${col}"]`).forEach(el => {
      el.style.display = visible ? '' : 'none';
    });
  });
}

function toggleColumnSettings() {
  const panel = document.getElementById('colSettingsPanel');
  panel.classList.toggle('show');
}
function toggleColumn(col, show) {
  visibleCols[col] = show;
  document.querySelectorAll(`[data-col="${col}"]`).forEach(el => {
    el.style.display = show ? '' : 'none';
  });
}

// ===== 14. Parent Toggle =====
function toggleParent(parentSku) {
  if (expandedParents.has(parentSku)) expandedParents.delete(parentSku);
  else expandedParents.add(parentSku);
  applyFilter();
}

// ===== 15. Inline Edit =====
function inlineEdit(el, field, sku) {
  const current = el.textContent.replace('$','').trim();
  const input = document.createElement('input');
  input.className = 'inline-input';
  input.value = current === '-' ? '' : current;
  input.type = field === 'price' || field === 'quantity' ? 'number' : 'text';
  input.step = field === 'price' ? '0.01' : '1';

  const save = () => {
    const val = input.value;
    // Price validation: reject non-positive numbers
    if ((field === 'price' || field === 'quantity') && val !== '') {
      const num = parseFloat(val);
      if (isNaN(num) || (field === 'price' && num <= 0) || (field === 'quantity' && num < 0)) {
        showToast('error', field === 'price' ? '价格必须为正数' : '库存不能为负数');
        el.textContent = current === '-' ? '-' : (field === 'price' ? '$' + current : current);
        return;
      }
    }
    const p = products.find(x => x.sku === sku);
    if (p) { p[field] = val; }
    // Persist to Excel
    if (currentFile) {
      fetch('/api/update-field', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ file: currentFile, sku, field, value: val })
      }).catch(err => { showToast('error', '保存失败: ' + err.message); el.textContent = current; });
    }
    if (field === 'price') el.textContent = val ? '$' + parseFloat(val).toFixed(2) : '-';
    else el.textContent = val || '-';
  };

  input.onblur = save;
  input.onkeydown = e => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter') { save(); input.blur(); }
    if (e.key === 'Escape') { input.onblur = null; el.textContent = current === '-' ? '-' : (field === 'price' ? '$' + current : current); }
  };
  el.textContent = '';
  el.appendChild(input);
  input.focus();
  input.select();
}

// ===== 16. Image Preview =====
function showImgPreview(e, url) {
  let tip = document.getElementById('imgPreviewTip');
  if (!tip) {
    tip = document.createElement('div');
    tip.id = 'imgPreviewTip';
    tip.className = 'img-preview-tooltip';
    document.body.appendChild(tip);
  }
  tip.innerHTML = `<img src="${escHtml(url)}" alt="">`;
  tip.style.display = 'block';
  tip.style.left = (e.clientX + 16) + 'px';
  tip.style.top = Math.min(e.clientY - 60, window.innerHeight - 260) + 'px';
}
function hideImgPreview() {
  const tip = document.getElementById('imgPreviewTip');
  if (tip) tip.style.display = 'none';
}

// ===== 17. Right Drawer =====
function openDrawer(sku) {
  drawerProduct = products.find(p => p.sku === sku);
  if (!drawerProduct) return;
  diagnosticJumpRegistry.clear();
  schemaFocusState = null;
  schemaFieldFilterMode = 'all';
  document.body.classList.add('drawer-open');
  document.getElementById('drawerSku').textContent = sku;
  document.getElementById('drawerName').textContent = drawerProduct.title || drawerProduct.item_name || '';
  const preferredTab = (drawerProduct.template_id || drawerProduct.template_product_type || drawerProduct.product_type) ? 'category' : 'copy';
  switchDrawerTab(preferredTab);
}
function closeDrawer() {
  document.body.classList.remove('drawer-open');
  diagnosticJumpRegistry.clear();
  schemaFocusState = null;
  schemaFieldFilterMode = 'all';
  drawerProduct = null;
  updateToolbarRecommendation();
}
function switchDrawerTab(tab) {
  drawerTab = tab;
  document.querySelectorAll('.drawer-tab').forEach(t => {
    t.classList.toggle('active', t.getAttribute('data-tab') === tab);
  });
  renderDrawerContent();
}

function renderDrawerContent() {
  const body = document.getElementById('drawerBody');
  if (!drawerProduct) { body.innerHTML = ''; return; }
  const p = drawerProduct;
  let innerHtml = '';

  switch(drawerTab) {
    case 'copy': innerHtml = renderCopyTab(p); break;
    case 'images': innerHtml = renderImagesTab(p); break;
    case 'category': innerHtml = renderCategoryFieldsTab(p); break;
    case 'diagnostics': innerHtml = renderDiagnosticsTab(p); break;
    default: innerHtml = '';
  }
  body.innerHTML = renderStatusOverview(p) + renderVariantFamilyPanel(p) + renderSubmissionWizard(p) + innerHtml;
  if (drawerTab === 'category') hydrateCategoryFieldsTab(p);
  updateToolbarRecommendation();
}

function isWebImageUrl(url) {
  return /^https?:\/\//i.test(String(url || ''));
}

function isMediaLocator(url) {
  return /^s3:\/\//i.test(String(url || '')) || isWebImageUrl(url);
}

function resolveProductMainPreview(p) {
  return p.main_image_preview_url || (isWebImageUrl(p.main_image_url) ? p.main_image_url : '') || p.ai_main_image || '';
}

function resolveProductSubPreview(p, slot) {
  return p['image_' + slot + '_preview_url']
    || (isWebImageUrl(p['image_' + slot]) ? p['image_' + slot] : '')
    || (isWebImageUrl(p['other_image_url_' + (slot - 1)]) ? p['other_image_url_' + (slot - 1)] : '');
}

function renderStatusOverview(p) {
  const aiStatus = p.ai_status || 'PENDING';
  const localValidation = p._validErrors && p._validErrors.length > 0
    ? '本地校验失败'
    : (p._validWarnings && p._validWarnings.length > 0 ? '本地校验有警告' : (p._validPass ? '本地校验通过' : '本地校验未执行'));
  const previewStatus = getPreviewDisplayStatus(p) || '未预览';
  const listingCheckStatus = p.listing_check_status || '';
  const routeText = formatSubmissionRoute(p.submission_route);
  const finalListingStatus = formatFinalListingStatus(p.final_listing_status);
  const asinValue = p.live_asin || p.asin || '未拿到';
  const finalIssues = Number(p.listing_issue_count || 0);
  const requiredTotal = Number(p.template_required_total || 0);
  const requiredFilled = Number(p.template_required_filled || 0);
  const requiredMissing = Number(p.template_required_missing_count || 0);
  const templateReady = !hasTemplateBlockingIssues(p);
  let submitStatus = p.submit_status || '未提交';
  if (submitStatus === 'ACCEPTED') submitStatus = 'ACCEPTED（待平台最终处理）';
  if (submitStatus === 'PENDING') submitStatus = '未提交';
  let imageHint = '暂无 AI 图片';
  if (p.ai_media_locator || p.ai_public_image_url) imageHint = `AI 主图已就绪，可直接采用 (${p.ai_upload_status || 'ready'})`;
  else if (p.ai_main_image || p.ai_image_url) imageHint = 'AI 主图已生成，但目前仅本地预览';
  const listingCheckHint = p.listing_check_summary || (listingCheckStatus ? `最近诊断: ${listingCheckStatus}` : '尚未执行缺项诊断');
  const templateHint = requiredTotal > 0 ? `${requiredFilled}/${requiredTotal} 已填` : '未使用专属模板';

  const chips = [
    { label: '模板必填', value: templateHint, tone: requiredMissing > 0 ? 'danger' : (requiredTotal > 0 ? 'success' : 'default') },
    { label: 'AI', value: aiStatus, tone: aiStatus === 'completed' ? 'success' : (aiStatus === 'failed' ? 'danger' : 'default') },
    { label: '本地校验', value: localValidation, tone: p._validErrors && p._validErrors.length > 0 ? 'danger' : (p._validWarnings && p._validWarnings.length > 0 ? 'warn' : 'success') },
    { label: 'Amazon预览', value: previewStatus, tone: isPreviewValidForSelectedAccount(p) ? 'success' : (previewStatus && previewStatus !== '未预览' ? 'warn' : 'default') },
    { label: '提交', value: submitStatus, tone: String(p.submit_status).toUpperCase() === 'ACCEPTED' ? 'info' : (p.submit_status && p.submit_status !== 'PENDING' ? 'warn' : 'default') },
    { label: '上架路线', value: routeText, tone: routeText === '匹配已有 ASIN' ? 'info' : 'default' },
    { label: '最终 Amazon 状态', value: finalListingStatus, tone: p.final_listing_status === 'discoverable' ? 'success' : (p.final_listing_status === 'suppressed' ? 'danger' : 'default') },
    { label: '最终 ASIN', value: asinValue, tone: asinValue === '未拿到' ? 'default' : 'success' },
    { label: '后台问题数', value: String(finalIssues), tone: finalIssues > 0 ? 'danger' : 'success' },
    { label: '缺项诊断', value: listingCheckHint, tone: listingCheckStatus === 'pass' ? 'success' : (listingCheckStatus === 'warn' ? 'warn' : (listingCheckStatus === 'fail' ? 'danger' : 'default')) },
    { label: '提交就绪', value: templateReady ? '允许提交' : '需先补齐阻断项', tone: templateReady ? 'success' : 'danger' },
    { label: '图片就绪', value: imageHint, tone: (p.ai_media_locator || p.ai_public_image_url) ? 'success' : ((p.ai_main_image || p.ai_image_url) ? 'warn' : 'default') },
  ];

  return `<div class="drawer-status-panel">
    ${chips.map(chip => `<div class="drawer-status-chip ${chip.tone}">
      <span class="drawer-status-label">${chip.label}</span>
      <strong>${escHtml(chip.value)}</strong>
    </div>`).join('')}
  </div>`;
}

function getVariantFamilyMembers(product) {
  if (!product) return { parent: null, children: [], members: [], familySku: '' };
  const level = String(product.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase();
  const familySku = level === 'child' ? String(product.parent_sku || '').trim() : String(product.sku || '').trim();
  if (!familySku && level !== 'parent') return { parent: null, children: [], members: [], familySku: '' };
  const parent = products.find(item => String(item.sku || '').trim() === familySku && String(item.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase() === 'parent')
    || (level === 'parent' ? product : null);
  const children = products.filter(item => String(item.parent_sku || '').trim() === familySku && String(item.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase() === 'child');
  const members = [];
  if (parent) members.push(parent);
  children.forEach(child => members.push(child));
  if (!parent && level === 'child') members.unshift(product);
  return { parent, children, members, familySku };
}

function computeVariantFamilyIssuesLocal(product) {
  return computeVariantFamilyDiagnostics(product).familyIssues;
}

function getVariantIssueSummary(product) {
  const diagnostics = computeVariantFamilyDiagnostics(product);
  const ownIssues = diagnostics.perSkuIssues[String(product?.sku || '').trim()] || [];
  const issues = String(product?.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase() === 'parent'
    ? diagnostics.familyIssues
    : ownIssues;
  const summaryProduct = product || diagnostics.family.parent || null;
  const displayIssues = issues.map(text => formatShortMerchantIssue(summaryProduct, createDerivedIssue(text, 'family_rules'), text));
  return {
    count: displayIssues.length,
    issues: displayIssues,
    tone: issues.length > 0 ? 'danger' : 'success',
  };
}

function computeVariantFamilyDiagnostics(product) {
  const family = getVariantFamilyMembers(product);
  const familyIssues = [];
  const perSkuIssues = {};
  const meta = {
    missingParent: false,
    parentDisplayOnly: false,
    noChildren: false,
    themeMismatch: false,
    productTypeMismatchSkus: [],
    missingParentSkuSkus: [],
    wrongParentSkuSkus: [],
    missingDimensionSkus: [],
    duplicateCombos: [],
  };
  const addFamilyIssue = message => {
    const text = String(message || '').trim();
    if (text && !familyIssues.includes(text)) familyIssues.push(text);
  };
  const addSkuIssue = (sku, message) => {
    const key = String(sku || '').trim();
    const text = String(message || '').trim();
    if (!key || !text) return;
    if (!perSkuIssues[key]) perSkuIssues[key] = [];
    if (!perSkuIssues[key].includes(text)) perSkuIssues[key].push(text);
  };

  if (!family.members.length) {
    return { family, familyIssues, perSkuIssues, inferredTheme: '', requiredDims: [], meta };
  }

  const parent = family.parent;
  if (!parent) {
    meta.missingParent = true;
    addFamilyIssue(`缺少父体 ${family.familySku || '(未指定)'}`);
    family.children.forEach(child => addSkuIssue(child.sku, `缺少父体 ${family.familySku || '(未指定)'}`));
    if (String(product.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase() === 'child') addSkuIssue(product.sku, `缺少父体 ${family.familySku || '(未指定)'}`);
    return { family, familyIssues, perSkuIssues, inferredTheme: '', requiredDims: [], meta };
  }

  const rawParentSku = getRawSkuValue(parent);
  if (rawParentSku && rawParentSku !== parent.sku) {
    meta.parentDisplayOnly = true;
    addFamilyIssue(`父体 ${parent.sku} 当前只存在前端分组视图，Excel 中缺少真实父体行`);
  }
  if (family.children.length === 0) {
    meta.noChildren = true;
    addFamilyIssue('父体至少需要一个子体 SKU');
  }

  const parentTheme = String(parent.variation_theme || '').trim();
  const childThemes = Array.from(new Set(family.children.map(child => String(child.variation_theme || '').trim()).filter(Boolean)));
  if (parentTheme && childThemes.some(theme => theme !== parentTheme)) {
    meta.themeMismatch = true;
    addFamilyIssue('父体与子体的 variation_theme 不一致');
    family.children.forEach(child => {
      if (String(child.variation_theme || '').trim() !== parentTheme) {
        addSkuIssue(child.sku, 'variation_theme 与父体不一致');
      }
    });
  }

  const parentType = String(parent.product_type || parent.template_product_type || '').trim();
  family.children.forEach(child => {
    const childType = String(child.product_type || child.template_product_type || '').trim();
    if (parentType && childType && parentType !== childType) {
      meta.productTypeMismatchSkus.push(child.sku);
      addFamilyIssue(`子体 ${child.sku} 的 product_type 与父体不一致`);
      addSkuIssue(child.sku, 'product_type 与父体不一致');
    }
    if (!String(child.parent_sku || '').trim()) {
      meta.missingParentSkuSkus.push(child.sku);
      addSkuIssue(child.sku, '缺少 parent_sku');
    } else if (String(child.parent_sku || '').trim() !== parent.sku) {
      meta.wrongParentSkuSkus.push(child.sku);
      addSkuIssue(child.sku, `parent_sku 应为 ${parent.sku}`);
    }
  });

  const inferredTheme = inferVariationThemeFromMembers(family.members);
  const themeText = String(parentTheme || childThemes[0] || inferredTheme).toUpperCase();
  const requiredDims = [];
  if (themeText.includes('COLOR')) requiredDims.push('color');
  if (themeText.includes('SIZE')) requiredDims.push('size');

  const seenCombos = new Map();
  family.children.forEach(child => {
    const missing = requiredDims.filter(dim => !String(child[dim] || '').trim());
    if (missing.length > 0) {
      const labels = missing.map(dim => dim === 'color' ? '颜色' : '尺码').join(' / ');
      meta.missingDimensionSkus.push(child.sku);
      addFamilyIssue(`子体 ${child.sku} 缺少 ${labels}`);
      addSkuIssue(child.sku, `缺少 ${labels}`);
    }
    if (requiredDims.length > 0) {
      const combo = requiredDims.map(dim => String(child[dim] || '').trim().toLowerCase()).join('||');
      if (combo && combo.split('||').every(Boolean)) {
        if (!seenCombos.has(combo)) seenCombos.set(combo, []);
        seenCombos.get(combo).push(child.sku);
      }
    }
  });
  seenCombos.forEach((skus, combo) => {
    if (skus.length <= 1) return;
    const comboText = combo.replaceAll('||', ' / ');
    meta.duplicateCombos.push({ combo: comboText, skus: [...skus] });
    addFamilyIssue(`重复变体组合 ${comboText}: ${skus.join(', ')}`);
    skus.forEach(sku => addSkuIssue(sku, `重复组合 ${comboText}`));
  });

  return { family, familyIssues, perSkuIssues, inferredTheme, requiredDims, meta };
}

const FAMILY_ISSUE_BUCKETS = {
  identity: {

    summary: 'GTIN、ASIN、品牌归属或商品身份判定',

    actionLabel: '去补身份字段',
  },

    tone: 'info',
    actionLabel: '去补内容',
  },
  media: {
    label: '图片 / 媒体',
    summary: '主图、副图、媒体地址和抓取问题',
    tone: 'info',
    actionLabel: '去看图片问题',
  },
};

const STRUCTURE_PRIORITY_BY_PRODUCT = {
  PANTS: ['bottoms_size', 'closure', 'rise', 'variation_theme', 'parent_sku', 'parentage_level', 'unit_count', 'import_designation', 'target_gender', 'age_range_description', 'model_name', 'fabric_type'],
  SHIRT: ['size', 'color', 'variation_theme', 'parent_sku', 'parentage_level', 'department', 'target_gender', 'age_range_description', 'material', 'style_name'],
  STORAGE_RACK: ['variation_theme', 'parent_sku', 'parentage_level', 'item_length', 'item_width', 'item_height', 'package_length', 'package_width', 'package_height', 'unit_count'],
};

function createDerivedIssue(message, source = 'derived', attributeNames = []) {
  return normalizeSchemaDiagnosticIssue({
    source,
    level: 'error',
    severity: 'ERROR',
    code: '',
    message,
    attributeNames,
    categories: [],
  }, source);
}

function collectProductDiagnosticIssues(product) {
  if (!product) return [];
  hydratePersistedDiagnosticData(product);
  const issues = [];
  const seen = new Set();
  const addIssue = issue => {
    const normalized = normalizeSchemaDiagnosticIssue(issue, issue?.source || 'derived');
    if (!normalized || !normalized.message) return;
    const signature = [
      normalized.source,
      normalized.level,
      normalized.code,
      normalized.message,
      normalized.attributeNames.join(','),
    ].join('|');
    if (seen.has(signature)) return;
    seen.add(signature);
    issues.push(normalized);
  };

  getTemplateBlockingReasons(product).forEach(message => {
    addIssue(createDerivedIssue(message, 'template_rules', [extractFieldKeyFromSummaryText(message)].filter(Boolean)));
  });

  splitIssueText(product.listing_check_missing_fields || '').forEach(message => {
    addIssue(createDerivedIssue(`缺少字段：${message}`, 'listing_runtime', [extractFieldKeyFromSummaryText(message)].filter(Boolean)));
  });

  (product._previewIssuePayload?.issues || []).forEach(addIssue);
  (product._listingCheck?.preview?.issues || []).forEach(addIssue);
  (product._listingCheck?.listing?.issues || []).forEach(addIssue);

  if (String(product.preview_message || '').trim() && !(product._previewIssuePayload?.issues || []).length) {
    splitIssueText(product.preview_message).forEach(message => addIssue(createDerivedIssue(message, 'amazon_preview')));
  }
  if (String(product.submit_message || '').trim() && String(product.submit_status || '').toUpperCase() !== 'ACCEPTED') {
    splitIssueText(product.submit_message).forEach(message => addIssue(createDerivedIssue(message, 'submit_runtime')));
  }

  return issues;
}

function classifyFamilyIssue(issue) {
  const attrs = (issue?.attributeNames || []).map(item => String(item || '').trim().toLowerCase()).join(' ');
  const text = `${attrs} ${String(issue?.message || '').toLowerCase()} ${String(issue?.code || '').toLowerCase()} ${String(issue?.source || '').toLowerCase()}`;

  const matches = patterns => patterns.some(pattern => pattern.test(text));
  if (matches([
    /media/, /image/, /main_image/, /other_image/, /retrieve media/, /photo/, /cdn/, /url '.+404/i,
  ])) return 'media';

  if (matches([
    /externally_assigned_product_identifier/, /merchant_suggested_asin/, /\basin\b/, /\bgtin\b/, /\bupc\b/, /\bean\b/,
    /product identifier/, /商品标识/, /exemption/, /免码/, /brand ownership/, /品牌归属/,
  ])) return 'identity';

  if (matches([
    /item_name/, /product_description/, /bullet_point/, /generic_keyword/, /keywords/, /\btitle\b/, /卖点/, /描述/, /搜索词/,
  ])) return 'content';

  if (matches([
    /parent_sku/, /parentage_level/, /variation_theme/, /theme/, /bottoms_size/, /size_system/, /size_class/, /\bsize\b/,
    /\bclosure\b/, /\brise\b/, /model_name/, /\bstyle\b/, /target_gender/, /age_range_description/, /unit_count/,
    /import_designation/, /list_price/, /product_type/, /country_of_origin/, /fabric_type/, /尺码/, /父体/, /子体/,
  ])) return 'structure';

  return 'structure';
}

function buildFamilyWorkflowState(product, diagnostics) {
  const family = diagnostics.family;
  const parent = family.parent;
  const members = family.members.filter(Boolean);
  members.forEach(member => hydratePersistedDiagnosticData(member));

  const childCount = family.children.length;
  const parentPreviewValid = !!parent && isPreviewValidForSelectedAccount(parent);
  const childPreviewValidCount = family.children.filter(item => isPreviewValidForSelectedAccount(item)).length;
  const parentAccepted = !!parent && isAlreadySubmittedProduct(parent);
  const childAcceptedCount = family.children.filter(item => isAlreadySubmittedProduct(item)).length;
  const allPreviewPassed = !!parent && childCount > 0 && parentPreviewValid && childPreviewValidCount === childCount;
  const allSubmitted = !!parent && childCount > 0 && parentAccepted && childAcceptedCount === childCount;

  const buckets = Object.fromEntries(Object.entries(FAMILY_ISSUE_BUCKETS).map(([key, config]) => [key, {
    key,
    ...config,
    count: 0,
    issues: [],
    members: new Set(),
    primarySku: '',
  }]));

  const pushBucketIssue = (bucketKey, issue, sku = '') => {
    const bucket = buckets[bucketKey];
    if (!bucket || !issue?.message) return;
    const signature = `${sku}|${issue.source || ''}|${issue.code || ''}|${issue.message || ''}`;
    if (bucket.issues.some(item => item.signature === signature)) return;
    bucket.issues.push({ ...issue, signature, sku });
    bucket.count = bucket.issues.length;
    if (sku) {
      bucket.members.add(sku);
      if (!bucket.primarySku) bucket.primarySku = sku;
    }
  };

  diagnostics.familyIssues.forEach(message => {
    pushBucketIssue('structure', createDerivedIssue(message, 'family_rules'), parent?.sku || product?.sku || '');
  });

  members.forEach(member => {
    collectProductDiagnosticIssues(member).forEach(issue => {
      const bucketKey = classifyFamilyIssue(issue);
      pushBucketIssue(bucketKey, issue, member.sku);
    });
  });

  const nextAction = resolveFamilyNextAction(product, diagnostics, {
    parent,
    childCount,
    parentPreviewValid,
    childPreviewValidCount,
    parentAccepted,
    childAcceptedCount,
    allPreviewPassed,
    allSubmitted,
    buckets,
  });

  return {
    family,
    parent,
    childCount,
    parentPreviewValid,
    childPreviewValidCount,
    parentAccepted,
    childAcceptedCount,
    allPreviewPassed,
    allSubmitted,
    buckets,
    nextAction,
  };
}

function resolveFamilyNextAction(product, diagnostics, state) {
  const childSkus = diagnostics.family.children.map(item => item.sku).filter(Boolean);
  const parentSku = (diagnostics.family.parent || {}).sku || product.sku || '';
  const allFamilySkus = [parentSku, ...childSkus].filter(Boolean);
  if (state.childCount === 0) {
    return {
      title: '先生成子体',
      summary: '当前只有父体，先补出颜色/尺码子体，后面才能做整个 family 的预览和提交。',
      tone: 'active',
      actionHtml: `<button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="openVariantChildGenerator()">${lang === 'zh' ? '生成子体' : 'Generate child rows'}</button>`,
    };
  }
  if (state.buckets.identity.count > 0) {
    return {
      title: '先补商品身份',
      summary: `当前有 ${state.buckets.identity.count} 个商品身份问题，先处理 GTIN / ASIN / 免码这类问题，再继续预览。`,
      tone: 'danger',
      actionHtml: `<button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="focusFamilyIssueBucket('identity')">${lang === 'zh' ? '去补身份字段' : 'Fix identity fields'}</button>`,
    };
  }
  if (state.buckets.structure.count > 0) {
    return {
      title: '先补类目结构字段',
      summary: `当前有 ${state.buckets.structure.count} 个类目结构问题，先修父子关系、尺码结构或类目结构字段。`,
      tone: 'warn',
      actionHtml: `<button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="focusFamilyIssueBucket('structure')">${lang === 'zh' ? '去补结构字段' : 'Fix structure fields'}</button>`,
    };
  }
  if (state.buckets.content.count > 0) {
    return {
      title: '补齐内容字段',
      summary: `当前还有 ${state.buckets.content.count} 个标题/卖点/描述类问题，修完后再重新预览。`,
      tone: 'info',
      actionHtml: `<button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="focusFamilyIssueBucket('content')">${lang === 'zh' ? '去补内容' : 'Fix copy fields'}</button>`,
    };
  }
  if (state.buckets.media.count > 0) {
    return {
      title: '先修图片 / 媒体',
      summary: `当前还有 ${state.buckets.media.count} 个图片或媒体地址问题，先保证图片可用，再继续。`,
      tone: 'info',
      actionHtml: `<button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="focusFamilyIssueBucket('media')">${lang === 'zh' ? '去看图片问题' : 'Fix media issues'}</button>`,
    };
  }
  if (!state.allPreviewPassed) {
    return {
      title: '重新预览整个家族',
      summary: `父体 ${state.parentPreviewValid ? '已' : '未'}通过预览，子体 ${state.childPreviewValidCount}/${state.childCount} 已通过。现在应该重新跑一次整个 family 的 Amazon 预览。`,
      tone: 'active',
      actionHtml: `<button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="requestAmazonSubmission('preview', ${JSON.stringify(allFamilySkus)}, { skipPreflight: true, customTitle: '变体家族 · Amazon预览', description: '系统会自动把父体和所有子体一起带入 Amazon 预览。' })">${lang === 'zh' ? '预览整个家族' : 'Preview family'}</button>`,
    };
  }
  if (!state.allSubmitted) {
    return {
      title: '正式提交整个家族',
      summary: `预览已经全部通过。父体 ${state.parentAccepted ? '已' : '未'}提交，子体 ${state.childAcceptedCount}/${state.childCount} 已提交。现在可以正式提交整个 family。`,
      tone: 'success',
      actionHtml: `<button class="btn btn-success btn-sm" onclick="requestAmazonSubmission('submit', ${JSON.stringify(allFamilySkus)}, { skipPreflight: true, customTitle: '变体家族 · 正式提交', description: '系统会自动先提交父体，再提交所有子体。' })">${lang === 'zh' ? '提交整个家族' : 'Submit family'}</button>`,
    };
  }
  return {
    title: '这个家族已经走完主流程',
    summary: `父体和 ${state.childCount} 个子体都已经通过预览并完成提交。现在更适合做结果复核，而不是继续改字段。`,
    tone: 'success',
    actionHtml: `<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="runVariantFamilyCheck()">${lang === 'zh' ? '复查整个家族' : 'Review family status'}</button>`,
  };
}

function renderFamilyStatusBoard(state) {
  const statusGuide = state.nextAction.tone === 'danger'
    ? '当前先别急着点提交，先把最关键的阻塞问题修掉。'
    : (state.nextAction.tone === 'warn'
      ? '当前还差一步关键修复，先按系统建议补字段。'
      : (state.nextAction.tone === 'success'
        ? '当前已经接近或达到可提交状态，可以继续下一步。'
        : '当前建议按系统推荐动作继续推进。'));
  const cards = [
    {
      label: '整体状态',
      value: state.nextAction.title,
      hint: `${state.nextAction.summary} ${statusGuide}`.trim(),
      tone: state.nextAction.tone === 'danger' ? 'danger' : (state.nextAction.tone === 'warn' ? 'warn' : (state.nextAction.tone === 'success' ? 'success' : 'info')),
    },
    {
      label: '父体',
      value: state.parent ? `${state.parentPreviewValid ? '预览通过' : '未过预览'} / ${state.parentAccepted ? '已提交' : '未提交'}` : '未找到父体',
      hint: state.parent ? `${state.parent.sku}` : '当前 family 没有真实父体行',
      tone: state.parentAccepted ? 'success' : (state.parentPreviewValid ? 'info' : 'warn'),
    },
    {
      label: '子体预览',
      value: `${state.childPreviewValidCount}/${state.childCount}`,
      hint: '已通过 Amazon 预览的子体数量',
      tone: state.childCount > 0 && state.childPreviewValidCount === state.childCount ? 'success' : 'warn',
    },
    {
      label: '子体提交',
      value: `${state.childAcceptedCount}/${state.childCount}`,
      hint: '已完成正式提交的子体数量',
      tone: state.childCount > 0 && state.childAcceptedCount === state.childCount ? 'success' : 'info',
    },
  ];
  return `<div class="family-health-grid">
    ${cards.map(card => `<div class="family-health-card ${card.tone}">
      <div class="family-health-label">${escHtml(card.label)}</div>
      <strong>${escHtml(card.value)}</strong>
      <div class="family-health-hint">${escHtml(card.hint)}</div>
    </div>`).join('')}
  </div>`;
}

function renderFamilyIssueBuckets(state) {
  const order = ['identity', 'structure', 'content', 'media'];
  return `<div class="family-bucket-grid">
    ${order.map(key => {
      const bucket = state.buckets[key];
      const hasIssues = bucket.count > 0;
      const topIssue = hasIssues ? bucket.issues[0] : null;
      const product = topIssue ? (products.find(item => item && item.sku === topIssue.sku) || state.parent || null) : (state.parent || null);
      const detailView = topIssue ? buildMerchantIssueView(product, topIssue, topIssue.message) : { primary: '这部分目前没有发现明显问题。', secondary: '' };
      const detailTech = topIssue ? summarizeTechnicalIssue(topIssue, topIssue.message || '') : '';
      return `<div class="family-bucket-card ${bucket.tone} ${hasIssues ? 'has-issues' : 'is-clear'}">
        <div class="family-bucket-head">
          <strong>${escHtml(bucket.label)}</strong>
          <span class="family-bucket-count">${hasIssues ? `${bucket.count} 个问题` : '当前无阻塞'}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="family-bucket-summary">${escHtml(bucket.summary)}</div>
        <div class="family-bucket-detail">${escHtml(detailView.primary)}</div>
        ${detailView.secondary ? `<div class="family-bucket-raw">${escHtml(detailView.secondary)}</div>` : ''}
        ${detailTech ? `<div class="family-bucket-tech">${escHtml(detailTech)}</div>` : ''}
        <div class="family-bucket-action">
          ${hasIssues ? `<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="focusFamilyIssueBucket('${key}')">${escHtml(bucket.actionLabel)}</button>` : `<span class="family-bucket-ok">${lang === 'zh' ? '暂时不用处理' : 'No action needed'}</span>`}
        </div>
      </div>`;
    }).join('')}
  </div>`;
}

function inferPrimaryIssueBucketForProduct(product) {
  if (!product) return '';
  const level = String(product.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase();
  if (level === 'parent') {
    const diagnostics = computeVariantFamilyDiagnostics(product);
    const state = buildFamilyWorkflowState(product, diagnostics);
    for (const key of ['identity', 'structure', 'content', 'media']) {
      if (state.buckets[key]?.count > 0) return key;
    }
    return '';
  }

  const localIssues = collectProductDiagnosticIssues(product);
  const buckets = { identity: 0, structure: 0, content: 0, media: 0 };
  localIssues.forEach(issue => {
    const bucketKey = classifyFamilyIssue(issue);
    if (bucketKey && buckets[bucketKey] !== undefined) buckets[bucketKey] += 1;
  });
  for (const key of ['identity', 'structure', 'content', 'media']) {
    if (buckets[key] > 0) return key;
  }
  return '';
}

function getStructurePriorityByProduct(productType) {
  const key = String(productType || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  return STRUCTURE_PRIORITY_BY_PRODUCT[key] || ['variation_theme', 'parent_sku', 'parentage_level', 'size', 'color', 'bottoms_size', 'closure', 'rise', 'unit_count', 'import_designation', 'model_name', 'target_gender', 'age_range_description'];
}

async function openPrimaryIssueNavigator(sku, bucketHint = '') {
  const product = products.find(item => item && item.sku === sku);
  if (!product) return;
  if (!drawerProduct || drawerProduct.sku !== sku) openDrawer(sku);
  const bucketKey = bucketHint || inferPrimaryIssueBucketForProduct(product);
  if (!bucketKey) {
    showToast('info', '当前没有可定位的阻塞问题，我先带你打开商品详情。');
    return;
  }
  const level = String(product.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase();
  await focusFamilyIssueBucket(bucketKey, level === 'child' ? { forceSku: sku } : {});
}

function buildResultActionButtons(result, mode = 'diagnose') {
  const sku = String(result?.sku || '').trim();
  if (!sku) return '';
  const dismiss = "dismissResultCenter()";
  const buttons = [
    `<button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="${dismiss}; openDrawer('${escHtml(sku)}')">打开商品</button>`,
    `<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="${dismiss}; openPrimaryIssueNavigator('${escHtml(sku)}')">定位问题</button>`,
  ];
  if (mode === 'diagnose') {
    buttons.push(`<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="${dismiss}; runListingCheck('${escHtml(sku)}')">重新诊断</button>`);
  }
  if (mode === 'preview') {
    buttons.push(`<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="${dismiss}; requestAmazonSubmission('preview', ['${escHtml(sku)}'], { skipPreflight: true, customTitle: '结果中心 · 重新预览', description: '系统将重新预览当前商品。' })">重新预览</button>`);
  }
  if (mode === 'submit') {
    buttons.push(`<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="${dismiss}; requestAmazonSubmission('submit', ['${escHtml(sku)}'], { skipPreflight: true, customTitle: '结果中心 · 再次提交', description: '系统将再次提交当前商品。' })">再次提交</button>`);
  }
  return `<div class="result-action-row">${buttons.join('')}</div>`;
}

function dismissResultCenter() {
  closeModal();
  document.querySelectorAll('.result-center-overlay').forEach(el => el.remove());
}

function renderResultIssueHtml(product, issue, fallbackText = '') {
  const view = buildMerchantIssueView(product, issue, fallbackText);
  const primary = view.primary || fallbackText || '-';
  const tech = summarizeTechnicalIssue(issue, fallbackText);
  return `<div class="result-issue-item">
    <div class="result-issue-primary">${escHtml(primary)}</div>
    ${view.secondary ? `<div class="result-issue-secondary">${escHtml(view.secondary)}</div>` : ''}
    ${tech ? `<div class="result-issue-tech">${escHtml(tech)}</div>` : ''}
  </div>`;
}

function getBucketPreferredFieldCandidates(bucketKey, issue, productType = '') {
  const text = `${String(issue?.message || '').toLowerCase()} ${(issue?.attributeNames || []).join(' ').toLowerCase()}`;
  if (bucketKey === 'identity') {
    return ['product_identity_mode', 'external_product_id_type', 'upc', 'asin', 'brand', 'item_type_keyword'];
  }
  if (bucketKey === 'structure') {
    const candidates = [];
    const categoryDefaults = getStructurePriorityByProduct(productType);
    if (/variation_theme|theme/.test(text)) candidates.push('variation_theme');
    if (/parent_sku|父sku|父体/.test(text)) candidates.push('parent_sku', 'parentage_level');
    if (/bottoms_size|size_system|size_class|尺码/.test(text)) candidates.push('bottoms_size', 'size');
    if (/\bclosure\b|闭合/.test(text)) candidates.push('closure');
    if (/\brise\b|腰/.test(text)) candidates.push('rise');
    if (/unit_count|单位数量/.test(text)) candidates.push('unit_count');
    if (/import_designation|进口/.test(text)) candidates.push('import_designation');
    if (/target_gender|性别/.test(text)) candidates.push('target_gender');
    if (/age_range_description|年龄/.test(text)) candidates.push('age_range_description');
    if (/model_name|型号/.test(text)) candidates.push('model_name');
    return [...candidates, ...categoryDefaults];
  }
  if (bucketKey === 'content') {
    return ['item_name', 'bullet_point_1', 'product_description', 'generic_keywords'];
  }
  if (bucketKey === 'media') {
    return ['main_image_url', 'other_image_url_1'];
  }
  return [];
}

function getToolbarFocusContext() {
  const selectedProducts = products.filter(item => item && selectedSkus.has(item.sku));
  const sourceProducts = selectedProducts.length > 0
    ? selectedProducts
    : (drawerProduct ? [drawerProduct] : products.filter(Boolean));

  const familyMap = new Map();
  sourceProducts.forEach(product => {
    const level = String(product.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase();
    if (!['parent', 'child'].includes(level)) return;
    const familyKey = level === 'child' ? String(product.parent_sku || '').trim() : String(product.sku || '').trim();
    if (!familyKey) return;
    if (!familyMap.has(familyKey)) familyMap.set(familyKey, []);
    familyMap.get(familyKey).push(product);
  });

  if (familyMap.size === 0) {
    return { kind: 'none' };
  }
  if (familyMap.size > 1) {
    return {
      kind: 'multiple',
      familyCount: familyMap.size,
      selectedCount: selectedProducts.length,
    };
  }

  const familyKey = Array.from(familyMap.keys())[0];
  const family = products.find(item => item && item.sku === familyKey && String(item.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase() === 'parent')
    || familyMap.get(familyKey)[0];
  if (!family) return { kind: 'none' };

  const diagnostics = computeVariantFamilyDiagnostics(family);
  const state = buildFamilyWorkflowState(family, diagnostics);
  return {
    kind: 'family',
    product: family,
    diagnostics,
    state,
    childSkus: [((diagnostics.family.parent || {}).sku || ''), ...diagnostics.family.children.map(item => item.sku)].filter(Boolean),
  };
}

function updateToolbarRecommendation() {
  const bar = document.getElementById('toolbarRecommendationBar');
  const listingCheckBtn = document.getElementById('btnListingCheck');
  const submitBtn = document.getElementById('btnSubmit');
  if (!bar || !listingCheckBtn || !submitBtn) return;

  listingCheckBtn.classList.remove('toolbar-recommended');
  submitBtn.classList.remove('toolbar-recommended');
  listingCheckBtn.title = '';
  submitBtn.title = '';

  const context = getToolbarFocusContext();
  if (context.kind === 'none') {
    bar.className = 'toolbar-recommendation hidden';
    bar.innerHTML = '';
    return;
  }

  if (context.kind === 'multiple') {
    bar.className = 'toolbar-recommendation warn';
    bar.innerHTML = `<div class="toolbar-recommendation-main">
      <div class="toolbar-recommendation-label">当前工作台建议</div>
      <div class="toolbar-recommendation-title">先只看一个变体家族</div>
      <div class="toolbar-recommendation-summary">你当前同时选中了多个 family。为了让“缺项诊断 / 预览 / 提交”更准确，建议先只处理一个 family。</div>
    </div>
    <div class="toolbar-recommendation-action"><button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="clearSelection()">${lang === 'zh' ? '清空选择' : 'Clear selection'}</button></div>`;
    return;
  }

  const state = context.state;
  let tone = 'warn';
  let title = '';
  let summary = '';
  let actionHtml = '';
  if (state.buckets.identity.count > 0 || state.buckets.structure.count > 0 || state.buckets.content.count > 0 || state.buckets.media.count > 0) {
    tone = state.buckets.identity.count > 0 ? 'danger' : 'warn';
    title = '建议先点「缺项诊断」';
    summary = `当前 family 还没修干净。先重新跑一次缺项诊断，让系统把最阻塞的问题重新对齐到字段。`;
    actionHtml = `<button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="runVariantFamilyCheckForSku('${escHtml(context.product.sku)}')">${lang === 'zh' ? '诊断这个家族' : 'Diagnose family'}</button>`;
    listingCheckBtn.classList.add('toolbar-recommended');
    listingCheckBtn.title = '当前推荐先做缺项诊断';
  } else if (!state.allPreviewPassed) {
    tone = 'info';
    title = '建议先点「提交上架」里的「预览验证」';
    summary = `当前 family 结构基本就绪。下一步最划算的是先跑整家族 Amazon 预览，而不是直接正式提交。`;
    actionHtml = `<button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="requestAmazonSubmission('preview', ${JSON.stringify(context.childSkus)}, { skipPreflight: true, customTitle: '工具栏推荐 · Amazon预览', description: '系统将直接对当前 family 执行 Amazon 预览。' })">${lang === 'zh' ? '预览整个家族' : 'Preview family'}</button>`;
    submitBtn.classList.add('toolbar-recommended');
    submitBtn.title = '当前推荐先做 Amazon 预览';
  } else if (!state.allSubmitted) {
    tone = 'success';
    title = '建议直接正式提交';
    summary = `当前 family 预览已经全部通过。下一步可以正式提交整个 family。`;
    actionHtml = `<button class="btn btn-success btn-sm" onclick="requestAmazonSubmission('submit', ${JSON.stringify(context.childSkus)}, { skipPreflight: true, customTitle: '工具栏推荐 · 正式提交', description: '系统将直接正式提交当前 family。' })">${lang === 'zh' ? '提交整个家族' : 'Submit family'}</button>`;
    submitBtn.classList.add('toolbar-recommended');
    submitBtn.title = '当前推荐直接正式提交';
  } else {
    tone = 'success';
    title = '这个家族已经走完主流程';
    summary = `父体和子体都已经走到提交阶段。现在更适合复查结果，而不是继续操作。`;
    actionHtml = `<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="runVariantFamilyCheckForSku('${escHtml(context.product.sku)}')">${lang === 'zh' ? '复查这个家族' : 'Review family'}</button>`;
  }

  bar.className = `toolbar-recommendation ${tone}`;
  bar.innerHTML = `<div class="toolbar-recommendation-main">
    <div class="toolbar-recommendation-label">当前工作台建议</div>
    <div class="toolbar-recommendation-title">${escHtml(title)}</div>
    <div class="toolbar-recommendation-summary">${escHtml(summary)}</div>
  </div>
  <div class="toolbar-recommendation-action">${actionHtml}</div>`;
}

function runVariantFamilyCheckForSku(sku) {
  const product = products.find(item => item && item.sku === sku);
  if (!product) return;
  const family = getVariantFamilyMembers(product);
  const skus = family.members.filter(item => String(item.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase() !== 'parent').map(item => item.sku);
  if (skus.length === 0) return showToast('warning', '当前没有可诊断的子体 SKU');
  runListingCheck('', skus);
}

async function focusFamilyIssueBucket(bucketKey, options = {}) {
  if (!drawerProduct) return;
  const diagnostics = computeVariantFamilyDiagnostics(drawerProduct);
  const state = buildFamilyWorkflowState(drawerProduct, diagnostics);
  const bucket = state.buckets[bucketKey];
  if (!bucket || bucket.count === 0) return showToast('info', '当前这类问题已经清掉了');

  const fallbackFields = {
    identity: ['product_identity_mode', 'external_product_id_type', 'upc', 'asin', 'brand', 'item_type_keyword'],
    structure: ['variation_theme', 'parent_sku', 'parentage_level', 'bottoms_size', 'size', 'closure', 'rise', 'unit_count', 'import_designation', 'model_name', 'target_gender', 'age_range_description'],
    content: ['item_name', 'bullet_point_1', 'product_description', 'generic_keywords'],
    media: ['main_image_url', 'other_image_url_1'],
  };

  const issueCandidates = (() => {
    const childFirst = [...(bucket.issues || [])].sort((a, b) => {
      const aProduct = products.find(item => item && item.sku === a.sku) || null;
      const bProduct = products.find(item => item && item.sku === b.sku) || null;
      if (options.forceSku) {
        const aForced = aProduct?.sku === options.forceSku ? 0 : 1;
        const bForced = bProduct?.sku === options.forceSku ? 0 : 1;
        if (aForced !== bForced) return aForced - bForced;
      }
      const aIsChild = String(aProduct?.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase() === 'child' ? 0 : 1;
      const bIsChild = String(bProduct?.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase() === 'child' ? 0 : 1;
      return aIsChild - bIsChild;
    });
    return childFirst;
  })();

  const resolveFallbackProduct = () => {
    const candidateSku = issueCandidates.find(issue => issue?.sku)?.sku || bucket.primarySku || drawerProduct.sku;
    return products.find(item => item && item.sku === candidateSku) || drawerProduct;
  };

  const focusTarget = async () => {
    if (bucketKey === 'content') {
      switchDrawerTab('copy');
      showToast('info', '我已经把你带到内容区域，先修这个家族当前最影响上架的问题。');
      return;
    }
    if (bucketKey === 'media') {
      switchDrawerTab('images');
      showToast('info', '我已经把你带到图片区域，先修图片或媒体地址问题。');
      return;
    }

    try {
      let targetProduct = null;
      let preferredFieldKey = '';

      for (const issue of issueCandidates) {
        const issueProduct = products.find(item => item && item.sku === issue.sku) || null;
        if (!issueProduct) continue;
        const schema = await loadFormSchemaForProduct(issueProduct);
        const feedback = computeSchemaFormFeedback(issueProduct, schema);
        const actionableFields = getSchemaActionableFieldOrder(schema, feedback);
        const resolved = resolveDiagnosticTargetKeys(schema, issue);
        const preferredCandidates = [...resolved, ...getBucketPreferredFieldCandidates(bucketKey, issue, issueProduct.product_type || issueProduct.template_product_type || ''), ...(fallbackFields[bucketKey] || [])];
        const candidateField = preferredCandidates.find(key => actionableFields.includes(key))
          || resolved[0]
          || '';
        if (candidateField) {
          targetProduct = issueProduct;
          preferredFieldKey = candidateField;
          break;
        }
      }

      if (!targetProduct) {
        targetProduct = resolveFallbackProduct();
      }
      if (!targetProduct) return showToast('warning', '找不到要修的商品');

      if (drawerProduct.sku !== targetProduct.sku) {
        openDrawer(targetProduct.sku);
        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 30));
      }

      const schema = await loadFormSchemaForProduct(targetProduct);
      const feedback = computeSchemaFormFeedback(targetProduct, schema);
      const actionableFields = getSchemaActionableFieldOrder(schema, feedback);
      if (!preferredFieldKey) {
        preferredFieldKey = fallbackFields[bucketKey]?.find(key => actionableFields.includes(key))
          || actionableFields[0]
          || fallbackFields[bucketKey]?.[0]
          || '';
      }

      switchDrawerTab('category');
      await startSchemaFixFlow(targetProduct, {
        preferredFieldKey,
        message: bucketKey === 'identity'
          ? '我已经带你定位到当前最影响建品成功的身份字段。先修它，再重新预览。'
          : '我已经带你定位到当前最影响上架通过的结构字段。先修它，再重新预览。',
      });
    } catch (e) {
      switchDrawerTab('category');
      showToast('error', '定位字段失败: ' + e.message);
    }
  };

  focusTarget();
}

function renderFamilyNextStep(state) {
  return `<div class="family-next-step ${state.nextAction.tone}">
    <div class="family-next-step-label">${lang === 'zh' ? '现在最该做的事' : 'Next best action'}</div>
    <div class="family-next-step-main">
      <div>
        <div class="family-next-step-title">${escHtml(state.nextAction.title)}</div>
        <div class="family-next-step-summary">${escHtml(state.nextAction.summary)}</div>
      </div>
      <div class="family-next-step-action">${state.nextAction.actionHtml || ''}</div>
    </div>
  </div>`;
}

function renderFamilyTableSummary(product) {
  if (!product || String(product.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase() !== 'parent') return '';
  const diagnostics = computeVariantFamilyDiagnostics(product);
  const state = buildFamilyWorkflowState(product, diagnostics);
