  return `<button type="button" class="row-family-summary" onclick="openPrimaryIssueNavigator('${escHtml(product.sku)}')">
    <span>${escHtml(state.nextAction.title)}</span>
    <span>父体 ${state.parentPreviewValid ? '已' : '未'}预览</span>
    <span>子体预览 ${state.childPreviewValidCount}/${state.childCount}</span>
    <span>子体提交 ${state.childAcceptedCount}/${state.childCount}</span>
  </button>`;
}

function inferVariationThemeFromMembers(members) {
  const rows = (members || []).filter(Boolean);
  let hasColor = false;
  let hasSize = false;
  rows.forEach(item => {
    if (String(item.color || '').trim()) hasColor = true;
    if (String(item.size || '').trim()) hasSize = true;
  });
  if (hasColor && hasSize) return 'COLOR_SIZE';
  if (hasColor) return 'COLOR_NAME';
  if (hasSize) return 'SIZE_NAME';
  return '';
}

function renderVariantIssueFixActions(issues, diagnostics) {
  const family = diagnostics.family;
  const parent = family.parent;
  const actions = [];
  if (!issues || issues.length === 0) return '';
  actions.push(`<button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="autoFixVariantFamily()">${lang === 'zh' ? '一键自动修复常见问题' : 'Auto-fix common issues'}</button>`);
  const inferredTheme = diagnostics.inferredTheme;
  if (diagnostics.meta.themeMismatch && inferredTheme) {
    actions.push(`<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="inferVariantThemeForFamily()">${lang === 'zh' ? `统一 Theme 为 ${inferredTheme}` : `Align theme to ${inferredTheme}`}</button>`);
  }
  if (parent && (diagnostics.meta.missingParentSkuSkus.length > 0 || diagnostics.meta.wrongParentSkuSkus.length > 0)) {
    actions.push(`<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="fillVariantParentSkuForFamily()">${lang === 'zh' ? '一键补全子体父SKU' : 'Fill missing parent SKU'}</button>`);
  }
  if (parent && diagnostics.meta.productTypeMismatchSkus.length > 0) {
    actions.push(`<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="syncVariantProductTypeForFamily()">${lang === 'zh' ? '统一子体产品类型' : 'Align child product type'}</button>`);
  }
  if (diagnostics.meta.missingDimensionSkus.length > 0 || diagnostics.meta.duplicateCombos.length > 0) {
    actions.push(`<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="focusVariantFamilyMatrix()">${lang === 'zh' ? '打开矩阵修问题' : 'Open matrix to fix'}</button>`);
  }
  if (diagnostics.meta.noChildren) {
    actions.push(`<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="openVariantChildGenerator()">${lang === 'zh' ? '先生成子体' : 'Generate child rows first'}</button>`);
  }
  if (actions.length === 0) return '';
  return `<div class="variant-issue-fixes">${actions.join('')}</div>`;
}

function renderVariantMatrix(product, diagnostics) {
  const family = diagnostics.family;
  const parent = family.parent;
  if (!parent || family.children.length === 0) return '';
  const requiredDims = diagnostics.requiredDims.length > 0 ? diagnostics.requiredDims : ['color', 'size'];
  const theme = parent.variation_theme || diagnostics.inferredTheme || '';
  return `<div class="variant-matrix-card" id="variantMatrixCard">
    <div class="variant-matrix-head">
      <div>
        <div class="variant-matrix-title">${lang === 'zh' ? '颜色/尺码矩阵' : 'Variant matrix'}</div>
        <div class="variant-matrix-subtitle">${lang === 'zh' ? '直接在这里改颜色、尺码、价格、库存，保存后系统会继续引导。' : 'Edit color, size, price, and quantity here, then save.'}</div>
      </div>
      <div class="variant-matrix-actions">
        <button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="openVariantChildGenerator()">${lang === 'zh' ? '新增子体' : 'Add children'}</button>
        <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="saveVariantFamilyMatrix()">${lang === 'zh' ? '保存矩阵' : 'Save matrix'}</button>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="variant-matrix-summary">
      <span>${lang === 'zh' ? 'Theme' : 'Theme'}: <strong>${escHtml(theme || '-')}</strong></span>
      <span>${lang === 'zh' ? '当前维度' : 'Dimensions'}: <strong>${escHtml(requiredDims.map(dim => dim === 'color' ? '颜色' : '尺码').join(' / '))}</strong></span>
    </div>
    <div class="variant-matrix-wrap">
      <table class="variant-matrix-table">
        <thead>
          <tr>
            <th>SKU</th>
            <th>${lang === 'zh' ? '颜色' : 'Color'}${tipFor('color')}</th>
            <th>${lang === 'zh' ? '尺码' : 'Size'}${tipFor('size')}</th>
            <th>${lang === 'zh' ? '价格' : 'Price'}${tipFor('standard_price')}</th>
            <th>${lang === 'zh' ? '库存' : 'Qty'}${tipFor('quantity')}</th>
            <th>${lang === 'zh' ? '问题' : 'Issues'}</th>
          </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>
          ${family.children.map(child => {
            const issues = diagnostics.perSkuIssues[child.sku] || [];
            return `<tr class="variant-matrix-row" data-sku="${escHtml(child.sku)}">
              <td><strong>${escHtml(child.sku)}</strong></td>
              <td><input class="drawer-form-input variant-matrix-input" data-field="color" value="${escHtml(child.color || '')}"></td>
              <td><input class="drawer-form-input variant-matrix-input" data-field="size" value="${escHtml(child.size || '')}"></td>
              <td><input class="drawer-form-input variant-matrix-input" data-field="price" value="${escHtml(child.price || child.standard_price || '')}"></td>
              <td><input class="drawer-form-input variant-matrix-input" data-field="quantity" value="${escHtml(child.quantity || '')}"></td>
              <td>${issues.length > 0 ? `<div class="variant-matrix-issue">${escHtml(issues[0])}</div>` : `<div class="variant-matrix-ok">${lang === 'zh' ? '正常' : 'OK'}</div>`}</td>
            </tr>`;
          }).join('')}
        </tbody>
      </table>
    </div>
  </div>`;
}

function renderVariantSubmissionWizard(product, diagnostics) {
  const family = diagnostics.family;
  const parent = family.parent;
  if (!parent) return '';
  const familyIssues = diagnostics.familyIssues || [];
  const state = buildFamilyWorkflowState(product, diagnostics);
  const childSkus = family.children.map(child => child.sku).filter(Boolean);
  const parentSku = (parent || {}).sku || product.sku || '';
  const allFamilySkus = [parentSku, ...childSkus].filter(Boolean);
  const previewReady = allFamilySkus.length > 0 && familyIssues.length === 0;
  const allPreviewPassed = state.allPreviewPassed;
  const allSubmitted = state.allSubmitted;
  return `<div class="variant-submit-guide">
    <div class="variant-submit-guide-title">${lang === 'zh' ? '变体家族提交流程' : 'Variant family submit flow'}</div>
    <div class="variant-submit-steps">
      <div class="variant-submit-step ${familyIssues.length > 0 ? 'active' : 'done'}">
        <strong>${lang === 'zh' ? '1. 先修家族结构' : '1. Fix family structure'}</strong>
        <span>${familyIssues.length > 0 ? escHtml(familyIssues[0]) : (lang === 'zh' ? '家族结构已通过基础检查。' : 'Family structure looks good.')}</span>
        ${familyIssues.length > 0 ? renderVariantIssueFixActions(familyIssues, diagnostics) : ''}
      </div>
      <div class="variant-submit-step ${allPreviewPassed ? 'done' : (previewReady ? 'active' : 'locked')}">
        <strong>${lang === 'zh' ? '2. 预览整个家族' : '2. Preview the whole family'}</strong>
        <span>${previewReady
          ? (allPreviewPassed
            ? `父体已通过，子体 ${state.childPreviewValidCount}/${state.childCount} 已通过预览。`
            : `父体 ${state.parentPreviewValid ? '已' : '未'}通过预览，子体 ${state.childPreviewValidCount}/${state.childCount} 已通过。`)
          : (lang === 'zh' ? '先把上面的家族问题修掉。' : 'Resolve family issues first.')}</span>
        <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="requestAmazonSubmission('preview', ${JSON.stringify(allFamilySkus)}, { skipPreflight: true, customTitle: '变体家族 · Amazon预览', description: '系统会自动把父体和所有子体一起带入 Amazon 预览。' })" ${previewReady ? '' : 'disabled'}>${lang === 'zh' ? '预览整个家族' : 'Preview family'}</button>
      </div>
      <div class="variant-submit-step ${allSubmitted ? 'done' : (allPreviewPassed ? 'active' : 'locked')}">
        <strong>${lang === 'zh' ? '3. 正式提交整个家族' : '3. Submit the whole family'}</strong>
        <span>${allSubmitted
          ? `父体已提交，子体 ${state.childAcceptedCount}/${state.childCount} 已提交。`
          : (allPreviewPassed
            ? `父体会先提交，子体会自动挂到父体下面。当前子体 ${state.childAcceptedCount}/${state.childCount} 已提交。`
            : (lang === 'zh' ? '先把整个 family 的预览跑通，再正式提交。' : 'Pass preview for the whole family first.'))}</span>
        <button class="btn btn-success btn-sm" onclick="requestAmazonSubmission('submit', ${JSON.stringify(allFamilySkus)}, { skipPreflight: true, customTitle: '变体家族 · 正式提交', description: '系统会自动先提交父体，再提交所有子体。' })" ${allPreviewPassed ? '' : 'disabled'}>${lang === 'zh' ? '提交整个家族' : 'Submit family'}</button>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>`;
}

function renderVariantFamilyPanel(product) {
  const level = String(product.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase();
  const diagnostics = computeVariantFamilyDiagnostics(product);
  const family = diagnostics.family;
  if (!family.parent && level !== 'child') return '';
  if (!family.parent && !family.familySku) return '';
  const state = buildFamilyWorkflowState(product, diagnostics);
  const role = level === 'parent' ? '父体' : (level === 'child' ? '子体' : '单品');
  const issues = diagnostics.familyIssues;
  const familyTheme = String((family.parent && family.parent.variation_theme) || product.variation_theme || '').trim() || '-';
  const childCount = family.children.length;
  const parentLabel = family.parent ? family.parent.sku : (family.familySku || '-');
  const canSync = !!(family.parent && childCount > 0);
  const familySkus = family.members.map(item => item.sku).filter(Boolean);
  const inferredTheme = diagnostics.inferredTheme;
  return `<div class="variant-family-card">
    <div class="variant-family-head">
      <div>
        <div class="variant-family-title">变体家族工作台</div>
        <div class="variant-family-subtitle">${role} · 父体 ${escHtml(parentLabel)} · 子体 ${childCount} 个 · Theme ${escHtml(familyTheme)}</div>
      </div>
      <span class="variant-family-badge ${issues.length > 0 ? 'danger' : 'success'}">${issues.length > 0 ? `${issues.length} 个家族问题` : '家族结构正常'}</span>
    </div>
    <div class="variant-family-actions">
      <button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="inferVariantThemeForFamily()">${lang === 'zh' ? `自动推断 Theme${inferredTheme ? ` (${inferredTheme})` : ''}` : `Infer Theme${inferredTheme ? ` (${inferredTheme})` : ''}`}</button>
      <button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="openVariantChildGenerator()">${lang === 'zh' ? '批量生成子体' : 'Generate child rows'}</button>
      <button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="openVariantFamilyEditor()">${lang === 'zh' ? '批量编辑颜色/尺码' : 'Edit family matrix'}</button>
      <button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="runVariantFamilyCheck()">${lang === 'zh' ? '诊断整个家族' : 'Diagnose family'}</button>
      <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="syncVariantSharedFields()" ${canSync ? '' : 'disabled'}>${lang === 'zh' ? '父体公共字段同步到子体' : 'Sync parent fields to children'}</button>
      ${level === 'child' && family.parent ? `<button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="openDrawer('${escHtml(family.parent.sku)}')">${lang === 'zh' ? '打开父体' : 'Open parent'}</button>` : ''}
    </div>
    ${renderFamilyStatusBoard(state)}
    ${renderFamilyNextStep(state)}
    ${renderVariantMemberIssueSummary(diagnostics)}
    ${renderFamilyIssueBuckets(state)}
    ${renderVariantIssueCards(diagnostics)}
    ${renderVariantIssueFixActions(issues, diagnostics)}
    ${issues.length > 0 ? `<ul class="variant-family-issues">${issues.map(issue => `<li>${escHtml(issue)}</li>`).join('')}</ul>` : `<div class="variant-family-empty">${lang === 'zh' ? '当前没有检测到明显的家族级问题。' : 'No obvious family-level issues detected.'}</div>`}
    ${familySkus.length > 0 ? `<div class="variant-family-members">${familySkus.map(sku => `<span class="variant-family-member">${escHtml(sku)}</span>`).join('')}</div>` : ''}
    ${renderVariantMatrix(product, diagnostics)}
    ${renderVariantSubmissionWizard(product, diagnostics)}
  </div>`;
}

function renderVariantMemberIssueSummary(diagnostics) {
  const family = diagnostics.family;
  const parent = family.parent;
  const parentIssues = parent ? collectProductDiagnosticIssues(parent) : [];
  const parentSummaries = parentIssues
    .map(issue => buildMerchantIssueView(parent, issue, issue.message || '').primary)
    .filter(Boolean)
    .slice(0, 3);

  const childSummaries = family.children.map(child => {
    const childIssues = collectProductDiagnosticIssues(child);
    const primary = childIssues[0]
      ? buildMerchantIssueView(child, childIssues[0], childIssues[0].message || '').primary
      : '';
    return {
      sku: child.sku,
      issue: primary,
      count: childIssues.length,
    };
  }).filter(item => item.issue);

  if (!parent && childSummaries.length === 0) return '';

  const parentHtml = parent
    ? `<div class="variant-member-card ${parentSummaries.length > 0 ? 'has-issues' : 'is-clear'}">
        <div class="variant-member-head">
          <strong>父体</strong>
          <span>${escHtml(parent.sku || '-')}</span>
        </div>
        ${parentSummaries.length > 0
          ? `<ul class="variant-member-issues">${parentSummaries.map(text => `<li>${escHtml(text)}</li>`).join('')}</ul>
             <div class="variant-member-actions">
               <button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="openPrimaryIssueNavigator('${escHtml(parent.sku)}')">定位父体问题</button>
               <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="openDrawer('${escHtml(parent.sku)}')">打开父体</button>
             </div>`
          : `<div class="variant-member-empty">父体当前没有直接暴露的字段阻断问题。</div>`}
      </div>`
    : `<div class="variant-member-card has-issues">
        <div class="variant-member-head"><strong>父体</strong><span>缺失</span></div>
        <div class="variant-member-empty">当前 family 没有真实父体行，必须先补父体。</div>
      </div>`;

  const childHtml = `<div class="variant-member-card ${childSummaries.length > 0 ? 'has-issues' : 'is-clear'}">
      <div class="variant-member-head">
        <strong>子体</strong>
        <span>${family.children.length} 个</span>
      </div>
      ${childSummaries.length > 0
        ? `<div class="variant-member-list">
            ${childSummaries.slice(0, 4).map(item => `<div class="variant-member-row">
              <div class="variant-member-row-main">
                <span class="variant-member-sku">${escHtml(item.sku)}</span>
                <span class="variant-member-text">${escHtml(item.issue)}</span>
              </div>
              <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="openPrimaryIssueNavigator('${escHtml(item.sku)}')">定位</button>
            </div>`).join('')}
          </div>
          <div class="variant-member-actions">
            <button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="focusVariantFamilyMatrix()">打开矩阵修问题</button>
            ${childSummaries.length > 4 ? `<span class="variant-member-more">还有 ${childSummaries.length - 4} 个子体问题可在矩阵里继续处理</span>` : ''}
          </div>`
        : `<div class="variant-member-empty">当前所有子体的直接字段问题都已清掉，可以继续预览整个家族。</div>`}
    </div>`;

  return `<div class="variant-member-grid">
    ${parentHtml}
    ${childHtml}
  </div>`;
}

function renderVariantIssueCards(diagnostics) {
  const cards = [];
  if (diagnostics.meta.noChildren) {
    cards.push({
      title: '还没有子体',
      body: '当前父体下面没有任何颜色/尺码子体。先生成子体，后面才能预览和提交整个家族。',
      action: `<button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="openVariantChildGenerator()">${lang === 'zh' ? '现在生成子体' : 'Generate children now'}</button>`,
    });
  }
  if (diagnostics.meta.themeMismatch) {
    cards.push({
      title: '变体主题不统一',
      body: '有的子体用颜色变体，有的子体用颜色+尺码变体。一个家族只能用同一套 Theme。',
      action: diagnostics.inferredTheme
        ? `<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="inferVariantThemeForFamily()">${lang === 'zh' ? `统一为 ${diagnostics.inferredTheme}` : `Align to ${diagnostics.inferredTheme}`}</button>`
        : '',
    });
  }
  if (diagnostics.meta.missingParentSkuSkus.length > 0 || diagnostics.meta.wrongParentSkuSkus.length > 0) {
    cards.push({
      title: '子体父SKU不完整',
      body: `有 ${diagnostics.meta.missingParentSkuSkus.length + diagnostics.meta.wrongParentSkuSkus.length} 个子体没有正确指向父体。`,
      action: `<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="fillVariantParentSkuForFamily()">${lang === 'zh' ? '一键补全父SKU' : 'Fill parent SKU'}</button>`,
    });
  }
  if (diagnostics.meta.productTypeMismatchSkus.length > 0) {
    cards.push({
      title: '父子产品类型不一致',
      body: `有 ${diagnostics.meta.productTypeMismatchSkus.length} 个子体的 product_type 与父体不一致。`,
      action: `<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="syncVariantProductTypeForFamily()">${lang === 'zh' ? '统一产品类型' : 'Align product type'}</button>`,
    });
  }
  if (diagnostics.meta.missingDimensionSkus.length > 0 || diagnostics.meta.duplicateCombos.length > 0) {
    cards.push({
      title: '颜色/尺码矩阵有问题',
      body: diagnostics.meta.duplicateCombos.length > 0
        ? '有重复的颜色/尺码组合，或者某些子体缺少颜色/尺码。'
        : '有子体缺少颜色或尺码，先在矩阵里补齐后再提交。',
      action: `<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="focusVariantFamilyMatrix()">${lang === 'zh' ? '去矩阵里修' : 'Fix in matrix'}</button>`,
    });
  }

  if (cards.length === 0) return '';
  return `<div class="variant-issue-card-list">
    ${cards.map(card => `<div class="variant-issue-card">
      <strong>${escHtml(card.title)}</strong>
      <div>${escHtml(card.body)}</div>
      <div class="variant-issue-card-action">${card.action || ''}</div>
    </div>`).join('')}
  </div>`;
}

function renderWizardStep(stepNumber, title, status, summary, actionHtml, helperText = '') {
  return `<div class="wizard-step ${status}">
    <div class="wizard-step-marker">${stepNumber}</div>
    <div class="wizard-step-main">
      <div class="wizard-step-head">
        <strong>${escHtml(title)}</strong>
        <span class="wizard-step-badge ${status}">${escHtml(status === 'done' ? '已完成' : (status === 'active' ? '现在做' : '下一步'))}</span>
      </div>
      <div class="wizard-step-summary">${escHtml(summary)}</div>
      ${helperText ? `<div class="wizard-step-helper">${escHtml(helperText)}</div>` : ''}
    </div>
    <div class="wizard-step-action">${actionHtml || ''}</div>
  </div>`;
}

function renderSubmissionWizard(p) {
  const templateBlocked = hasTemplateBlockingIssues(p);
  const previewStatus = getPreviewDisplayStatus(p);
  const previewValid = isPreviewValidForSelectedAccount(p);
  const previewAttempted = !!previewStatus && previewStatus !== '未预览';
  const submitStatus = String(p.submit_status || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  const submitted = isAlreadySubmittedProduct(p);
  const templateReasons = getTemplateBlockingReasons(p);

  const step1Status = templateBlocked ? 'active' : 'done';
  const step2Status = templateBlocked ? 'locked' : (previewValid ? 'done' : 'active');
  const step3Status = submitted ? 'done' : ((templateBlocked || !previewValid) ? 'locked' : 'active');

  const step1Summary = templateBlocked
    ? (templateReasons[0] || '还有字段没补齐，先跟着系统把阻断项修完。')
    : '模板阻断项和缺失字段已经清掉，可以继续做 Amazon 预览。';
  const step2Summary = previewValid
    ? 'Amazon 预览已经通过，说明当前资料基本符合提交要求。'
    : (templateBlocked
      ? '这一步会在你修完字段后自动变成可操作。'
      : (previewAttempted
        ? `最近预览状态：${previewStatus}。建议先修掉系统定位出来的问题，再重新预览。`
        : '先跑一次 Amazon 预览，让系统替你检查真实提交前的问题。'));
  const step3Summary = submitted
    ? `最近一次提交状态：${p.submit_status || '-'}${p.asin ? ` · ASIN ${p.asin}` : ''}`
    : ((templateBlocked || !previewValid)
      ? '正式提交会在“字段修复 + Amazon 预览通过”后解锁。'
      : '当前已经满足正式提交条件，可以直接推送到 Amazon。');

  const step1Action = templateBlocked
    ? `<button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="startDrawerIssueRepair()">${lang === 'zh' ? '去修字段' : 'Fix fields now'}</button>`
    : `<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="startDrawerIssueRepair()">${lang === 'zh' ? '复查字段' : 'Review fields'}</button>`;
  const step2Action = templateBlocked
    ? `<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" disabled>${lang === 'zh' ? '先完成上一步' : 'Finish step 1 first'}</button>`
    : `<button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="requestAmazonSubmission('preview', [drawerProduct.sku], { skipPreflight: true, customTitle: '新手向导 · Amazon预览', description: '系统将直接用当前商品跑一次 Amazon 预览验证。' })">${previewValid ? (lang === 'zh' ? '重新预览' : 'Preview again') : (lang === 'zh' ? '预览此商品' : 'Preview this SKU')}</button>`;
  const step3Action = submitted
    ? `<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" disabled>${lang === 'zh' ? '已经提交成功' : 'Already submitted'}</button>`
    : (templateBlocked || !previewValid)
    ? `<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" disabled>${lang === 'zh' ? '先通过预览' : 'Pass preview first'}</button>`
    : `<button class="btn btn-success btn-sm" onclick="requestAmazonSubmission('submit', [drawerProduct.sku], { skipPreflight: true, customTitle: '新手向导 · 正式提交', description: '系统将直接把当前商品正式提交到 Amazon。' })">${submitted ? (lang === 'zh' ? '再次提交' : 'Submit again') : (lang === 'zh' ? '正式提交此商品' : 'Submit this SKU')}</button>`;

  return `<div class="drawer-guide">
    <div class="drawer-guide-head">
      <div>
        <div class="drawer-guide-title">${lang === 'zh' ? '新手上架向导' : 'Beginner Listing Guide'}</div>
        <div class="drawer-guide-subtitle">${lang === 'zh' ? '你不用自己判断流程，按 1 → 2 → 3 做就行。' : 'No need to guess the flow — just follow steps 1 → 2 → 3.'}</div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="wizard-step-list">
      ${renderWizardStep(1, lang === 'zh' ? '先修字段和模板阻断项' : 'Fix fields and template blockers first', step1Status, step1Summary, step1Action, lang === 'zh' ? '系统会自动带你去对应字段。' : 'The system will take you to the right field.')}
      ${renderWizardStep(2, lang === 'zh' ? '再做 Amazon 预览' : 'Run Amazon preview next', step2Status, step2Summary, step2Action, lang === 'zh' ? '预览通过后再正式提交，风险更低。' : 'Preview before submit to reduce risk.')}
      ${renderWizardStep(3, lang === 'zh' ? '最后正式提交' : 'Submit to Amazon last', step3Status, step3Summary, step3Action, lang === 'zh' ? '只在前两步完成后再点它。' : 'Only use this after the first two steps are done.')}
    </div>
  </div>`;
}

async function startDrawerIssueRepair() {
  if (!drawerProduct) return;
  switchDrawerTab('category');
  await startSchemaFixFlow(drawerProduct, {
    preferredFieldKey: (getCurrentSchemaFocus(drawerProduct)?.fieldKeys || [])[0] || '',
    message: lang === 'zh' ? '我已经把你带到下一项最该先修的字段。' : 'I brought you to the next field that needs attention first.',
  });
}

async function applyVariantFamilyUpdates(updatesBySku, successMessage) {
  if (!drawerProduct || !currentFile) return false;
  const payload = {};
  Object.entries(updatesBySku || {}).forEach(([sku, updates]) => {
    const skuText = String(sku || '').trim();
    const normalized = {};
    Object.entries(updates || {}).forEach(([field, value]) => {
      if (field && value !== undefined) normalized[field] = value;
    });
    if (skuText && Object.keys(normalized).length > 0) payload[skuText] = normalized;
  });
  if (Object.keys(payload).length === 0) {
    showToast('warning', '没有可保存的变体更新');
    return false;
  }

  try {
    const response = await fetch('/api/update-family', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ file: currentFile, file_version: currentFileVersion, updates_by_sku: payload })
    });
    const data = await response.json();
    if (!response.ok || data.error) throw new Error(data.error || ('HTTP ' + response.status));
    if (data.file_version) currentFileVersion = Number(data.file_version || currentFileVersion);

    Object.entries(payload).forEach(([sku, updates]) => {
      const product = products.find(item => item.sku === sku);
      if (!product) return;
      Object.entries(updates).forEach(([field, value]) => {
        product[field] = value;
        if (product._raw) product._raw[field] = value;
      });
    });

    const refreshed = products.find(item => item.sku === drawerProduct.sku);
    if (refreshed) drawerProduct = refreshed;
    applyFilter();
    renderDrawerContent();
    showToast('success', successMessage || '变体家族已更新');
    return true;
  } catch (e) {
    showToast('error', '保存变体家族失败: ' + e.message);
    return false;
  }
}

async function syncVariantSharedFields() {
  if (!drawerProduct) return;
  const family = getVariantFamilyMembers(drawerProduct);
  const parent = family.parent;
  if (!parent || family.children.length === 0) return showToast('warning', '当前没有可同步的子体');

  const sharedFields = ['brand', 'manufacturer', 'material', 'product_type', 'variation_theme', 'department', 'target_gender', 'age_range', 'country_of_origin'];
  const updatesBySku = {};
  family.children.forEach(child => {
    updatesBySku[child.sku] = {};
    sharedFields.forEach(field => {
      const value = parent[field];
      if (value !== undefined && value !== null && String(value).trim() !== '') {
        updatesBySku[child.sku][field] = value;
      }
    });
  });
  await applyVariantFamilyUpdates(updatesBySku, '已将父体公共字段同步到所有子体');
}

async function fillVariantParentSkuForFamily() {
  if (!drawerProduct) return;
  const family = getVariantFamilyMembers(drawerProduct);
  const parent = family.parent;
  if (!parent) return showToast('warning', '当前没有可补全的父体');
  const updatesBySku = {};
  family.children.forEach(child => {
    if (String(child.parent_sku || '').trim() !== parent.sku) {
      updatesBySku[child.sku] = { parent_sku: parent.sku };
    }
  });
  await applyVariantFamilyUpdates(updatesBySku, '已补全所有子体的父SKU');
}

async function syncVariantProductTypeForFamily() {
  if (!drawerProduct) return;
  const family = getVariantFamilyMembers(drawerProduct);
  const parent = family.parent;
  const parentType = String(parent?.product_type || parent?.template_product_type || '').trim();
  if (!parent || !parentType) return showToast('warning', '父体缺少产品类型，暂时无法自动统一');
  const updatesBySku = {};
  family.children.forEach(child => {
    if (String(child.product_type || child.template_product_type || '').trim() !== parentType) {
      updatesBySku[child.sku] = { product_type: parentType };
    }
  });
  await applyVariantFamilyUpdates(updatesBySku, '已统一所有子体的产品类型');
}

async function autoFixVariantFamily() {
  if (!drawerProduct) return;
  const diagnostics = computeVariantFamilyDiagnostics(drawerProduct);
  const family = diagnostics.family;
  const parent = family.parent;
  if (!parent) return showToast('warning', '当前缺少真实父体，无法自动修复整个家族');

  const updatesBySku = {};
  const inferredTheme = diagnostics.inferredTheme;
  if (inferredTheme) {
    family.members.forEach(item => {
      if (String(item.variation_theme || '').trim() !== inferredTheme) {
        updatesBySku[item.sku] = { ...(updatesBySku[item.sku] || {}), variation_theme: inferredTheme };
      }
    });
  }

  const parentType = String(parent.product_type || parent.template_product_type || '').trim();
  family.children.forEach(child => {
    if (String(child.parent_sku || '').trim() !== parent.sku) {
      updatesBySku[child.sku] = { ...(updatesBySku[child.sku] || {}), parent_sku: parent.sku };
    }
    if (parentType && String(child.product_type || child.template_product_type || '').trim() !== parentType) {
      updatesBySku[child.sku] = { ...(updatesBySku[child.sku] || {}), product_type: parentType };
    }
  });
  const sharedFields = ['brand', 'manufacturer', 'material', 'department', 'target_gender', 'age_range', 'country_of_origin'];
  family.children.forEach(child => {
    sharedFields.forEach(field => {
      const value = parent[field];
      if (value !== undefined && value !== null && String(value).trim() !== '' && String(child[field] || '').trim() === '') {
        updatesBySku[child.sku] = { ...(updatesBySku[child.sku] || {}), [field]: value };
      }
    });
  });

  if (Object.keys(updatesBySku).length === 0) return showToast('success', '当前没有可自动修复的家族问题');
  await applyVariantFamilyUpdates(updatesBySku, '已自动修复一批常见变体家族问题');
}

async function saveVariantFamilyMatrix() {
  if (!drawerProduct) return;
  const updatesBySku = {};
  document.querySelectorAll('.variant-matrix-row').forEach(row => {
    const sku = row.getAttribute('data-sku');
    if (!sku) return;
    updatesBySku[sku] = {};
    row.querySelectorAll('.variant-matrix-input').forEach(input => {
      const field = input.getAttribute('data-field');
      if (!field) return;
      updatesBySku[sku][field] = input.value;
    });
  });
  await applyVariantFamilyUpdates(updatesBySku, '已保存变体矩阵');
}

function focusVariantFamilyMatrix() {
  const card = document.getElementById('variantMatrixCard');
  if (!card) return showToast('warning', '当前没有可编辑的变体矩阵');
  card.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
  card.classList.remove('highlight');
  void card.offsetWidth;
  card.classList.add('highlight');
  window.setTimeout(() => card.classList.remove('highlight'), 1800);
}

async function inferVariantThemeForFamily() {
  if (!drawerProduct) return;
  const family = getVariantFamilyMembers(drawerProduct);
  const inferredTheme = inferVariationThemeFromMembers(family.members);
  if (!inferredTheme) return showToast('warning', '当前家族还没有足够的颜色/尺码信息，无法自动推断 Theme');

  const updatesBySku = {};
  family.members.forEach(item => {
    updatesBySku[item.sku] = { variation_theme: inferredTheme };
  });
  await applyVariantFamilyUpdates(updatesBySku, `已为整个家族应用 ${inferredTheme}`);
}

function buildGeneratedVariantSku(parentSku, parts, rule = 'parent-values', customPrefix = '', index = 0) {
  const basePrefix = String(customPrefix || parentSku || '').trim() || String(parentSku || '').trim() || 'PARENT';
  if (rule === 'parent-seq') {
    return `${String(parentSku || '').trim() || basePrefix}-VAR${String(index + 1).padStart(2, '0')}`;
  }
  const suffix = parts
    .map(part => String(part || '').trim().toUpperCase())
    .filter(Boolean)
    .map(part => part.replace(/[^0-9A-Z]+/g, '-').replace(/^-+|-+$/g, ''))
    .filter(Boolean)
    .join('-');
  const prefix = rule === 'custom-prefix' ? basePrefix : (String(parentSku || '').trim() || basePrefix);
  return suffix ? `${prefix}-${suffix}` : `${prefix}-CHILD`;
}

function openVariantChildGenerator() {
  if (!drawerProduct) return;
  const family = getVariantFamilyMembers(drawerProduct);
  const parent = family.parent;
  if (!parent) return showToast('warning', '请先打开父体商品，再批量生成子体');
  const inferredTheme = inferVariationThemeFromMembers(family.members) || parent.variation_theme || 'COLOR_SIZE';
  document.getElementById('modalTitle').textContent = '批量生成子体';
  document.getElementById('modalBody').innerHTML = `
    <div class="family-edit-note">
      根据父体自动生成子体行。每行一个子体，格式按 Theme 填写：
      <br>COLOR_NAME: 颜色
      <br>SIZE_NAME: 尺码
      <br>COLOR_SIZE: 颜色|尺码
      ${family.children.length > 0 ? `<br><br>当前已有子体：${escHtml(family.children.map(child => child.sku).join('、'))}` : ''}
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-grid" style="margin-bottom:12px;">
      <div class="drawer-form-group">
        <label class="drawer-form-label">父SKU</label>
        <input class="drawer-form-input" id="variantGeneratorParentSku" value="${escHtml(parent.sku || '')}" disabled>
      </div>
      <div class="drawer-form-group">
        <label class="drawer-form-label">Variation Theme</label>
        <select class="drawer-form-select" id="variantGeneratorTheme">
          <option value="COLOR_NAME" ${inferredTheme === 'COLOR_NAME' ? 'selected' : ''}>COLOR_NAME</option>
          <option value="SIZE_NAME" ${inferredTheme === 'SIZE_NAME' ? 'selected' : ''}>SIZE_NAME</option>
          <option value="COLOR_SIZE" ${inferredTheme === 'COLOR_SIZE' ? 'selected' : ''}>COLOR_SIZE</option>
        </select>
      </div>
      <div class="drawer-form-group">
        <label class="drawer-form-label">SKU生成规则</label>
        <select class="drawer-form-select" id="variantGeneratorSkuRule">
          <option value="parent-values" ${variantGeneratorSkuRule === 'parent-values' ? 'selected' : ''}>父SKU-颜色尺码</option>
          <option value="parent-seq" ${variantGeneratorSkuRule === 'parent-seq' ? 'selected' : ''}>父SKU-序号</option>
          <option value="custom-prefix" ${variantGeneratorSkuRule === 'custom-prefix' ? 'selected' : ''}>自定义前缀-颜色尺码</option>
        </select>
      </div>
      <div class="drawer-form-group">
        <label class="drawer-form-label">自定义前缀</label>
        <input class="drawer-form-input" id="variantGeneratorPrefix" value="${escHtml(parent.sku || '')}" placeholder="PARENT-SHIRT">
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">子体定义</label>
      <textarea class="drawer-form-input" id="variantGeneratorEntries" rows="8" placeholder="Red|S\nBlue|M"></textarea>
    </div>`;
  document.getElementById('modalFooter').innerHTML = `
    <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="closeModal()">取消</button>
    <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="saveGeneratedVariantChildren()">生成子体</button>`;
  document.getElementById('modal').classList.add('show');
}

async function saveGeneratedVariantChildren() {
  if (!drawerProduct || !currentFile) return;
  const family = getVariantFamilyMembers(drawerProduct);
  const parent = family.parent;
  if (!parent) return showToast('warning', '请先打开父体商品');

  const theme = String(document.getElementById('variantGeneratorTheme')?.value || '').trim();
  const skuRule = String(document.getElementById('variantGeneratorSkuRule')?.value || 'parent-values').trim();
  const customPrefix = String(document.getElementById('variantGeneratorPrefix')?.value || '').trim();
  variantGeneratorSkuRule = skuRule;
  const rawText = String(document.getElementById('variantGeneratorEntries')?.value || '').trim();
  const lines = rawText.split(/\n+/).map(line => line.trim()).filter(Boolean);
  if (!theme || lines.length === 0) return showToast('warning', '请先填写子体定义');

  const rows = [];
  for (const [index, line] of lines.entries()) {
    const parts = line.split('|').map(item => item.trim()).filter(Boolean);
    let color = '';
    let size = '';
    if (theme === 'COLOR_NAME') {
      color = parts[0] || '';
    } else if (theme === 'SIZE_NAME') {
      size = parts[0] || '';
    } else {
      color = parts[0] || '';
      size = parts[1] || '';
    }
    if ((theme === 'COLOR_NAME' && !color) || (theme === 'SIZE_NAME' && !size) || (theme === 'COLOR_SIZE' && (!color || !size))) {
      return showToast('warning', `子体定义格式不正确: ${line}`);
    }
    const sku = buildGeneratedVariantSku(parent.sku, [color, size], skuRule, customPrefix, index);
    rows.push({
      sku,
      item_name: parent.item_name || parent.title || '',
      title: parent.title || parent.item_name || '',
      product_type: parent.product_type || parent.template_product_type || '',
      parentage_level: 'child',
      parent_sku: parent.sku,
      variation_theme: theme,
      color,
      size,
      brand: parent.brand || '',
      main_image_url: parent.main_image_url || '',
      price: parent.price || parent.standard_price || '',
      quantity: parent.quantity || '',
    });
  }

  try {
    const response = await fetch('/api/append-family-rows', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ file: currentFile, rows })
    });
    const data = await response.json();
    if (!response.ok || data.error) throw new Error(data.error || ('HTTP ' + response.status));
    closeModal();
    showToast('success', `已新增 ${data.added || rows.length} 个子体`);
    loadProducts();
  } catch (e) {
    showToast('error', '生成子体失败: ' + e.message);
  }
}

function openVariantFamilyEditor() {
  if (!drawerProduct) return;
  const family = getVariantFamilyMembers(drawerProduct);
  if (!family.members.length) return showToast('warning', '当前商品不在变体家族中');

  const rows = family.members.map(item => {
    const role = String(item.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase() === 'parent' ? 'parent' : 'child';
    const persistable = role !== 'parent' || !getRawSkuValue(item) || getRawSkuValue(item) === item.sku;
    return `<tr data-sku="${escHtml(item.sku)}">
      <td>${escHtml(item.sku)}</td>
      <td>${escHtml(role)}</td>
      <td><input class="drawer-form-input family-edit-input" data-field="parent_sku" value="${escHtml(item.parent_sku || '')}" ${role === 'parent' || !persistable ? 'disabled' : ''}></td>
      <td>
        <select class="drawer-form-select family-edit-input" data-field="variation_theme" ${!persistable ? 'disabled' : ''}>
          <option value="" ${!item.variation_theme ? 'selected' : ''}>-</option>
          <option value="COLOR_NAME" ${item.variation_theme === 'COLOR_NAME' ? 'selected' : ''}>COLOR_NAME</option>
          <option value="SIZE_NAME" ${item.variation_theme === 'SIZE_NAME' ? 'selected' : ''}>SIZE_NAME</option>
          <option value="COLOR_SIZE" ${item.variation_theme === 'COLOR_SIZE' ? 'selected' : ''}>COLOR_SIZE</option>
        </select>
      </td>
      <td><input class="drawer-form-input family-edit-input" data-field="color" value="${escHtml(item.color || '')}" ${!persistable ? 'disabled' : ''}></td>
      <td><input class="drawer-form-input family-edit-input" data-field="size" value="${escHtml(item.size || '')}" ${!persistable ? 'disabled' : ''}></td>
    </tr>`;
  }).join('');

  document.getElementById('modalTitle').textContent = '变体家族批量编辑';
  document.getElementById('modalBody').innerHTML = `
    <div class="family-edit-note">修改后会一次性回写到当前 Excel。父体的 parent_sku 保持留空，子体请指向同一个父体。若父体行在 Excel 中不存在，对应输入框会自动锁定。</div>
    <div class="family-edit-wrap">
      <table class="family-edit-table">
        <thead>
          <tr><th>SKU</th><th>角色${tipFor('parentage_level')}</th><th>父SKU${tipFor('parent_sku')}</th><th>Theme${tipFor('variation_theme')}</th><th>颜色${tipFor('color')}</th><th>尺码${tipFor('size')}</th></tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>${rows}</tbody>
      </table>
    </div>`;
  document.getElementById('modalFooter').innerHTML = `
    <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="closeModal()">取消</button>
    <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="saveVariantFamilyEditor()">保存整个家族</button>`;
  document.getElementById('modal').classList.add('show');
}

async function saveVariantFamilyEditor() {
  const updatesBySku = {};
  document.querySelectorAll('.family-edit-table tbody tr').forEach(row => {
    const sku = row.getAttribute('data-sku');
    if (!sku) return;
    updatesBySku[sku] = {};
    row.querySelectorAll('.family-edit-input').forEach(input => {
      const field = input.getAttribute('data-field');
      if (!field || input.disabled) return;
      updatesBySku[sku][field] = input.value;
    });
  });
  const ok = await applyVariantFamilyUpdates(updatesBySku, '已保存变体家族矩阵');
  if (ok) closeModal();
}

function runVariantFamilyCheck() {
  if (!drawerProduct) return;
  const family = getVariantFamilyMembers(drawerProduct);
  const skus = family.members.filter(item => String(item.parentage_level || '').toLowerCase() !== 'parent').map(item => item.sku);
  if (skus.length === 0) return showToast('warning', '当前没有可诊断的子体 SKU');
  runListingCheck('', skus);
}

function renderCopyTab(p) {
  const fields = [
    { key: 'title', aiKey: 'ai_title', label: '标题 (item_name)', origKey: 'item_name' },
    { key: 'bullet_1', aiKey: 'ai_bullet_1', label: '卖点 1', origKey: 'bullet_point_1' },
    { key: 'bullet_2', aiKey: 'ai_bullet_2', label: '卖点 2', origKey: 'bullet_point_2' },
    { key: 'bullet_3', aiKey: 'ai_bullet_3', label: '卖点 3', origKey: 'bullet_point_3' },
    { key: 'bullet_4', aiKey: 'ai_bullet_4', label: '卖点 4', origKey: 'bullet_point_4' },
    { key: 'bullet_5', aiKey: 'ai_bullet_5', label: '卖点 5', origKey: 'bullet_point_5' },
    { key: 'description', aiKey: 'ai_description', label: '描述', origKey: 'product_description' },
    { key: 'keywords', aiKey: 'ai_keywords', label: '搜索词', origKey: 'generic_keywords' },
  ];

  return fields.map(f => {
    const orig = p[f.origKey] || (p._raw && (p._raw[f.origKey] || p._raw[f.key])) || p[f.key] || '';
    const ai = p[f.aiKey] || (p._raw && p._raw[f.aiKey]) || '';
    return `<div class="compare-group">
      <div class="compare-label">${f.label}${tipFor(f.origKey)}</div>
      <div class="compare-row">
        <div class="compare-box">
          <div class="compare-box-label">${t('original')}</div>
          ${escHtml(orig) || '<em style="color:var(--text-disabled)">-</em>'}
        </div>
        <div class="compare-box compare-box-ai">
          <div class="compare-box-label">${t('ai_generated')}</div>
          ${escHtml(ai) || '<em style="color:var(--text-disabled)">-</em>'}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="compare-actions">
        <button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="regenerateField('${p.sku}','${f.key}')">${t('regenerate')}</button>
        <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="adoptField('${p.sku}','${f.key}')" ${ai?'':'disabled'}>${t('adopt')}</button>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

function renderImagesTab(p) {
  const mainOrig = resolveProductMainPreview(p);
  const mainAi = p.ai_main_image || p.ai_image_url || '';
  const bgStyle = p._bgStyle || 'white';
  const hasAnyAiSub = Array.from({ length: 8 }, (_, idx) => idx + 2)
    .some(i => !!(p['ai_image_' + i] || p['ai_media_locator_' + i] || p['ai_public_image_' + i]));

  let html = `<div class="drawer-section">
    <div class="drawer-section-title">${t('main_img')}</div>
    <div class="img-compare-grid">
      <div class="img-compare-item">
        ${mainOrig ? `<img src="${escHtml(mainOrig)}" alt="">` : `<div class="sub-img-empty">${t('no_data_title')}</div>`}
        <div class="img-label">${t('original')}</div>
      </div>
      <div class="img-compare-item ai-img">
        ${mainAi ? `<img src="${escHtml(mainAi)}" alt="">` : `<div class="sub-img-empty">${t('no_data_title')}</div>`}
        <div class="img-label">${t('ai_generated')}</div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="sub-img-label" style="margin:8px 0 0;color:var(--text-secondary);">
      ${p.ai_media_locator ? `提交地址：${escHtml(p.ai_media_locator)}` : (p.ai_upload_error ? `上传失败：${escHtml(p.ai_upload_error)}` : '尚未上传到媒体存储')}
    </div>
    <div class="bg-selector">
      <span class="bg-opt ${bgStyle === 'white' ? 'active' : ''}" onclick="selectBg(this,'white')">${t('pure_white')}</span>
      <span class="bg-opt ${bgStyle === 'scene' ? 'active' : ''}" onclick="selectBg(this,'scene')">${t('scene')}</span>
      <span class="bg-opt ${bgStyle === 'gradient' ? 'active' : ''}" onclick="selectBg(this,'gradient')">${t('gradient')}</span>
    </div>
    <div class="compare-actions">
      <button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="regenerateImage('${p.sku}','main')">${t('generate')}</button>
      <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="quickImageProcess('${escHtml(mainOrig)}','${bgStyle}')">快速预览</button>
      <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="adoptImage('${p.sku}','main')" ${mainAi?'':'disabled'}>${t('adopt')}</button>
    </div>
  </div>`;

  html += `<div class="drawer-section">
    <div class="drawer-section-title">${t('sub_images')}</div>
    <div class="sub-images-grid">`;

  for (let i = 2; i <= 9; i++) {
    const url = resolveProductSubPreview(p, i);
    const aiUrl = p['ai_image_' + i] || '';
    const displayUrl = aiUrl || url;
    const label = aiUrl ? `AI ${t('img_label')}${i}` : `${t('img_label')}${i}`;
    html += `<div class="sub-img-item">
      ${displayUrl ? `<img src="${escHtml(displayUrl)}" alt="">` : '<div class="sub-img-empty">' + i + '</div>'}
      <div class="sub-img-label">${label}${p['ai_media_locator_' + i] ? ' · 已上传' : ''}</div>
    </div>`;
  }

  html += `</div>
    <div class="compare-actions" style="margin-top:10px">
      <button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="regenerateImage('${p.sku}','all')">${t('generate_all')}</button>
      <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="adoptImage('${p.sku}','all')" ${hasAnyAiSub || mainAi ? '' : 'disabled'}>${t('adopt_all')}</button>
    </div>
  </div>`;

  return html;
}

function renderDiagnosticsTab(p) {
  hydratePersistedDiagnosticData(p);
  const check = p._listingCheck || null;
  const summary = (check && check.summary_text) || p.listing_check_summary || '尚未执行缺项诊断';
  const checkedAt = (check && check.checked_at) || p.listing_check_time || '';
  const status = (check && check.status) || p.listing_check_status || '';
  const missingFields = (check && check.missing_fields) || [];
  const previewIssues = (check && check.preview && check.preview.issues) || [];
  const listingIssues = (check && check.listing && check.listing.issues) || [];
  const mediaChecks = (check && check.media && check.media.checks) || [];
  const localErrors = (check && check.local && check.local.errors) || [];
  const localWarnings = (check && check.local && check.local.warnings) || [];
  const templateRequiredMissing = (p.template_required_missing_fields || '').split(';').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean);
  const templateRecommendedMissing = (p.template_recommended_missing_fields || '').split(';').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean);
  const templateBlocking = (p.template_blocking_issues || '').split(';').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean);
  const templateLabel = p.template_product_type ? `${p.template_product_type} · ${p.template_variation_mode || 'single'}` : '未绑定模板';

  const statusTone = status === 'pass' ? 'success' : (status === 'warn' ? 'warn' : (status === 'fail' ? 'danger' : 'default'));
  const issueList = (items, emptyText) => {
    if (!items || items.length === 0) return `<div class="sub-img-empty">${emptyText}</div>`;
    return `<ul class="diagnostic-list">${items.map(item => {
      const text = typeof item === 'string' ? item : (item.text || '');
      const subtext = typeof item === 'string' ? '' : (item.subtext || '');
      const jump = item && typeof item === 'object' ? renderDiagnosticJumpButton(item.jump) : '';
      return `<li class="diagnostic-list-item">
        <div class="diagnostic-list-copy">
          <span class="diagnostic-list-text">${escHtml(text)}</span>
          ${subtext ? `<span class="diagnostic-list-subtext">${escHtml(subtext)}</span>` : ''}
        </div>
        ${jump}
      </li>`;
    }).join('')}</ul>`;
  };
  const issueBlock = (title, bodyHtml) => `
    <div class="drawer-section">
      <div class="drawer-section-title">${escHtml(title)}</div>
      ${bodyHtml}
    </div>
  `;
  const previewMessages = previewIssues.map(issue => {
    const prefix = [issue.severity || issue.level || '', issue.code || ''].filter(Boolean).join('/');
    return prefix ? `[${prefix}] ${issue.message || ''}` : (issue.message || '');
  }).filter(Boolean);
  const listingMessages = listingIssues.map(issue => {
    const prefix = [issue.severity || issue.level || '', issue.code || ''].filter(Boolean).join('/');
    return prefix ? `[${prefix}] ${issue.message || ''}` : (issue.message || '');
  }).filter(Boolean);
  const mediaMessages = mediaChecks.map(item => {
    const prefix = item.ok ? 'OK' : 'FAIL';
    const code = item.status_code ? ` (${item.status_code})` : '';
    return `${prefix} ${item.field}${code}: ${item.message || item.url || ''}`;
  });
  const buildNamedFieldEntries = (items, sourceLabel) => items.map(text => {
    const key = extractFieldKeyFromSummaryText(text);
    const formatted = formatTemplateFieldText(text, p);
    return {
      text: formatted,
      jump: key ? {
        sku: p.sku,
        fieldKeys: [key],
        message: sourceLabel ? `${sourceLabel}: ${formatted}` : formatted,
      } : null,
    };
  });
  const missingFieldEntries = missingFields.map(item => ({
    text: `${formatSchemaFieldReference(p, item.name || '', item.title || item.name)} — 来源: ${item.source || '-'}`,
    jump: item.name ? {
      sku: p.sku,
      fieldKeys: [item.name],
      message: `${formatSchemaFieldReference(p, item.name || '', item.title || item.name)}`,
    } : null,
  }));
  const previewEntries = previewIssues.map(issue => {
    const prefix = [issue.severity || issue.level || '', issue.code || ''].filter(Boolean).join('/');
    const view = buildMerchantIssueView(p, issue, issue.message || '');
    const text = prefix ? `[${prefix}] ${view.primary || issue.message || ''}` : (view.primary || issue.message || '');
    const attrs = (issue.attributeNames || []).map(item => String(item || '').trim()).filter(Boolean);
    return {
      text,
      subtext: view.secondary,
      jump: attrs.length > 0 ? {
        sku: p.sku,
        attributeNames: attrs,
        message: `Amazon预览: ${text}`,
      } : null,
    };
  }).filter(item => item.text);
  const listingEntries = listingIssues.map(issue => {
    const prefix = [issue.severity || issue.level || '', issue.code || ''].filter(Boolean).join('/');
    const attrs = (issue.attributeNames || []).map(item => String(item || '').trim()).filter(Boolean);
    const view = buildMerchantIssueView(p, issue, issue.message || '');
    const text = prefix ? `[${prefix}] ${view.primary || issue.message || ''}` : (view.primary || issue.message || '');
    return {
      text,
      subtext: view.secondary,
      jump: attrs.length > 0 ? {
        sku: p.sku,
        attributeNames: attrs,
        message: `Amazon后台: ${text}`,
      } : null,
    };
  }).filter(item => item.text);

  let html = `
    <div class="drawer-section">
      <div class="drawer-section-title">${t('diagnostics')}</div>
      <div class="drawer-status-panel" style="margin-top:0;">
        <div class="drawer-status-chip ${statusTone}">
          <span class="drawer-status-label">${t('status')}</span>
          <strong>${escHtml(status || '未执行')}</strong>
        </div>
        <div class="drawer-status-chip default">
          <span class="drawer-status-label">${t('last_checked')}</span>
          <strong>${escHtml(checkedAt || '-')}</strong>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="margin-top:12px; color:var(--text-secondary); line-height:1.6;">${escHtml(summary)}</div>
      <div style="margin-top:8px; color:var(--text-secondary); line-height:1.6;">模板：${escHtml(templateLabel)}</div>
      <div class="compare-actions" style="margin-top:12px;">
        <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="runListingCheck('${escHtml(p.sku)}')">${t('diagnose_this')}</button>
      </div>
    </div>
  `;

  html += issueBlock('模板阻断项', issueList(
    buildNamedFieldEntries(templateBlocking, '模板阻断项'),
    '当前模板没有阻断项。'
  ));
  html += issueBlock('模板必填缺失', issueList(
    buildNamedFieldEntries(templateRequiredMissing, '模板必填缺失'),
    '当前模板必填字段已补齐。'
  ));
  html += issueBlock('模板建议补充', issueList(
    buildNamedFieldEntries(templateRecommendedMissing, '模板建议补充'),
    '当前模板建议字段已基本补齐。'
  ));
  html += issueBlock(t('missing_fields'), issueList(
    missingFieldEntries,
    '当前未发现缺失字段。'
  ));
  html += issueBlock('本地校验详情', issueList(
    [].concat(localErrors.map(msg => `错误: ${msg}`), localWarnings.map(msg => `警告: ${msg}`)),
    '当前无本地校验问题。'
  ));
  html += issueBlock(t('preview_issues'), issueList(
    previewEntries.length ? previewEntries : ((check && check.preview && check.preview.message) ? [{ text: check.preview.message, jump: null }] : []),
    '当前无 Amazon 预览问题。'
  ));
  html += issueBlock(t('listing_issues'), issueList(
    listingEntries,
    '当前无后台 issues。'
  ));
  html += issueBlock(t('media_check'), issueList(
    mediaMessages,
    '当前未检测到图片链接。'
  ));

  return html;
}

function renderAttrsTab(p) {
  const fields = [
    ['brand', t('brand'), p.brand || p.brand_name || ''],
    ['manufacturer', t('manufacturer'), p.manufacturer || ''],
    ['model_number', t('model_number'), p.model_number || p.part_number || ''],
    ['product_type', t('product_category'), p.product_type || ''],
    ['item_type_keyword', t('item_type_keyword'), p.item_type_keyword || ''],
    ['color', t('color'), p.color || p.color_name || ''],
    ['size', t('size'), p.size || p.size_name || ''],
    ['material', t('material'), p.material || p.material_type || ''],
    ['style_name', t('style_name'), p.style_name || ''],
    ['pattern_type', t('pattern_type'), p.pattern_type || p.pattern_name || ''],
    ['closure_type', t('closure_type'), p.closure_type || ''],
    ['department', t('department'), p.department || p.department_name || ''],
    ['target_gender', t('target_gender'), p.target_gender || ''],
    ['age_range', t('age_range'), p.age_range || ''],
    ['country_of_origin', t('country_of_origin'), p.country_of_origin || ''],
    ['number_of_items', t('number_of_items'), p.number_of_items || ''],
    ['unit_count', t('unit_count'), p.unit_count || ''],
    ['unit_count_type', t('unit_count_type'), p.unit_count_type || ''],
  ];
  return `<div class="drawer-form-grid">${fields.map(([key, label, val]) =>
    `<div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${label}${tipFor(key)}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" data-field="${key}" value="${escHtml(val)}">
    </div>`
  ).join('')}</div>`;
}

function renderOfferTab(p) {
  const price = p.price || p.standard_price || '';
  const qty = p.quantity || '';
  const cond = p.condition_type || 'New';
  const fulfill = p.fulfillment_channel || '';
  const upc = p.upc || p.product_id || '';
  const cur = p.currency || 'USD';
  const salePrice = p.sale_price || '';
  const saleFrom = p.sale_from_date || '';
  const saleEnd = p.sale_end_date || '';
  const listPrice = p.list_price || '';
  const maxQty = p.max_order_quantity || '';
  const handling = p.handling_time || '';
  const shipGroup = p.merchant_shipping_group_name || '';
  const taxCode = p.product_tax_code || '';
  const idType = p.external_product_id_type || 'UPC';
  const identityMode = p.product_identity_mode || '';

  return `<div class="drawer-form-grid">
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('price_usd')}${tipFor('standard_price')}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" type="number" step="0.01" min="0.01" data-field="price" value="${escHtml(price)}">
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('currency')}</label>
      <select class="drawer-form-select" data-field="currency">
        <option value="USD" ${cur==='USD'?'selected':''}>USD</option>
        <option value="CAD" ${cur==='CAD'?'selected':''}>CAD</option>
        <option value="GBP" ${cur==='GBP'?'selected':''}>GBP</option>
        <option value="EUR" ${cur==='EUR'?'selected':''}>EUR</option>
        <option value="JPY" ${cur==='JPY'?'selected':''}>JPY</option>
        <option value="MXN" ${cur==='MXN'?'selected':''}>MXN</option>
        <option value="AUD" ${cur==='AUD'?'selected':''}>AUD</option>
        <option value="INR" ${cur==='INR'?'selected':''}>INR</option>
        <option value="SGD" ${cur==='SGD'?'selected':''}>SGD</option>
        <option value="SAR" ${cur==='SAR'?'selected':''}>SAR</option>
        <option value="AED" ${cur==='AED'?'selected':''}>AED</option>
        <option value="PLN" ${cur==='PLN'?'selected':''}>PLN</option>
        <option value="SEK" ${cur==='SEK'?'selected':''}>SEK</option>
        <option value="BRL" ${cur==='BRL'?'selected':''}>BRL</option>
        <option value="TRY" ${cur==='TRY'?'selected':''}>TRY</option>
      </select>
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('list_price')}${tipFor('list_price')}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" type="number" step="0.01" min="0" data-field="list_price" value="${escHtml(listPrice)}">
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('sale_price')}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" type="number" step="0.01" min="0" data-field="sale_price" value="${escHtml(salePrice)}">
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('sale_from_date')}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" type="date" data-field="sale_from_date" value="${escHtml(saleFrom)}">
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('sale_end_date')}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" type="date" data-field="sale_end_date" value="${escHtml(saleEnd)}">
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('inventory')}${tipFor('quantity')}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" type="number" data-field="quantity" value="${escHtml(qty)}">
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('max_order_quantity')}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" type="number" min="1" data-field="max_order_quantity" value="${escHtml(maxQty)}">
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('condition')}</label>
      <select class="drawer-form-select" data-field="condition_type">
        <option value="New" ${cond==='New'?'selected':''}>New</option>
        <option value="Refurbished" ${cond==='Refurbished'?'selected':''}>Refurbished</option>
        <option value="UsedLikeNew" ${cond==='UsedLikeNew'?'selected':''}>Used - Like New</option>
        <option value="UsedVeryGood" ${cond==='UsedVeryGood'?'selected':''}>Used - Very Good</option>
        <option value="UsedGood" ${cond==='UsedGood'?'selected':''}>Used - Good</option>
        <option value="UsedAcceptable" ${cond==='UsedAcceptable'?'selected':''}>Used - Acceptable</option>
      </select>
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('fulfillment')}${tipFor('fulfillment_channel')}</label>
      <select class="drawer-form-select" data-field="fulfillment_channel">
        <option value="DEFAULT" ${fulfill==='DEFAULT'?'selected':''}>FBM</option>
        <option value="AMAZON_NA" ${fulfill==='AMAZON_NA'?'selected':''}>FBA (NA)</option>
        <option value="AMAZON_EU" ${fulfill==='AMAZON_EU'?'selected':''}>FBA (EU)</option>
        <option value="AMAZON_IN" ${fulfill==='AMAZON_IN'?'selected':''}>FBA (IN)</option>
        <option value="AMAZON_JP" ${fulfill==='AMAZON_JP'?'selected':''}>FBA (JP)</option>
      </select>
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('handling_time')}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" type="number" min="0" data-field="handling_time" value="${escHtml(handling)}">
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('merchant_shipping_group')}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" data-field="merchant_shipping_group_name" value="${escHtml(shipGroup)}">
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('product_tax_code')}${tipFor('product_tax_code')}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" data-field="product_tax_code" value="${escHtml(taxCode)}">
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('upc_ean')}${tipFor('upc')}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" data-field="upc" value="${escHtml(upc)}">
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('product_identity_mode')}${tipFor('product_identity_mode')}</label>
      <select class="drawer-form-select" data-field="product_identity_mode">
        <option value="" ${!identityMode?'selected':''}>-</option>
        <option value="real_gtin" ${identityMode==='real_gtin'?'selected':''}>${t('identity_real_gtin')}</option>
        <option value="gtin_exemption" ${identityMode==='gtin_exemption'?'selected':''}>${t('identity_exemption')}</option>
        <option value="internal_code" ${identityMode==='internal_code'?'selected':''}>${t('identity_internal')}</option>
      </select>
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('external_product_id_type')}${tipFor('external_product_id_type')}</label>
      <select class="drawer-form-select" data-field="external_product_id_type">
        <option value="UPC" ${idType==='UPC'?'selected':''}>UPC</option>
        <option value="EAN" ${idType==='EAN'?'selected':''}>EAN</option>
        <option value="GTIN" ${idType==='GTIN'?'selected':''}>GTIN</option>
        <option value="ISBN" ${idType==='ISBN'?'selected':''}>ISBN</option>
        <option value="ASIN" ${idType==='ASIN'?'selected':''}>ASIN</option>
      </select>
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group" style="grid-column:1/-1;">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">Hint</label>
      <div style="padding:10px 12px;border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:10px;color:var(--text-secondary);font-size:12px;line-height:1.6;">
        ${lang==='zh'
          ? '真实GTIN: 提交真实 UPC/EAN/GTIN。GTIN免码: 不提交条码，但店铺必须已有免码资格。内部码: 只用于你们内部识别，系统会阻止正式新建。'
          : 'Real GTIN: submit a real UPC/EAN/GTIN. GTIN Exemption: no barcode is submitted, but the store must already have approval. Internal Code: only for internal ERP use and will be blocked from listing creation.'}
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>`;
}

function renderComplianceTab(p) {
  const batReq = p.batteries_required || '';
  const batInc = p.batteries_included || p.are_batteries_included || '';
  const batType = p.battery_type || '';
  const numBat = p.number_of_batteries || '';
  const batComp = p.battery_cell_composition || '';
  const lithPkg = p.lithium_battery_packaging || '';
  const lithEnergy = p.lithium_battery_energy_content || '';
  const lithWeight = p.lithium_battery_weight || '';
  const hazmat = p.hazmat_declaration || '';
  const cpsia = p.cpsia_cautionary_statement || '';
  const legalDisc = p.legal_disclaimer || '';
  const safetyWarn = p.safety_warning || '';

  return `<div class="drawer-form-grid">
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('needs_battery')}</label>
      <select class="drawer-form-select" data-field="batteries_required">
        <option value="" ${!batReq?'selected':''}>-</option>
        <option value="Yes" ${batReq==='Yes'?'selected':''}>Yes</option>
        <option value="No" ${batReq==='No'?'selected':''}>No</option>
      </select>
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('includes_battery')}</label>
      <select class="drawer-form-select" data-field="batteries_included">
        <option value="" ${!batInc?'selected':''}>-</option>
        <option value="Yes" ${batInc==='Yes'?'selected':''}>Yes</option>
        <option value="No" ${batInc==='No'?'selected':''}>No</option>
      </select>
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('battery_type')}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" data-field="battery_type" value="${escHtml(batType)}">
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('num_batteries')}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" type="number" min="0" data-field="number_of_batteries" value="${escHtml(numBat)}">
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('battery_composition')}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" data-field="battery_cell_composition" value="${escHtml(batComp)}">
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('lithium_packaging')}</label>
      <select class="drawer-form-select" data-field="lithium_battery_packaging">
        <option value="" ${!lithPkg?'selected':''}>-</option>
        <option value="batteries_contained_in_equipment" ${lithPkg==='batteries_contained_in_equipment'?'selected':''}>Contained in equipment</option>
        <option value="batteries_packed_with_equipment" ${lithPkg==='batteries_packed_with_equipment'?'selected':''}>Packed with equipment</option>
        <option value="batteries_only" ${lithPkg==='batteries_only'?'selected':''}>Batteries only</option>
      </select>
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('lithium_energy')}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" type="number" step="0.01" min="0" data-field="lithium_battery_energy_content" value="${escHtml(lithEnergy)}">
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('lithium_weight')}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" type="number" step="0.01" min="0" data-field="lithium_battery_weight" value="${escHtml(lithWeight)}">
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('hazmat')}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" data-field="hazmat_declaration" value="${escHtml(hazmat)}">
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('cpsia_warning')}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" data-field="cpsia_cautionary_statement" value="${escHtml(cpsia)}">
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('safety_warning')}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" data-field="safety_warning" value="${escHtml(safetyWarn)}">
    </div>
    <div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${t('legal_disclaimer')}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" data-field="legal_disclaimer" value="${escHtml(legalDisc)}">
    </div>
  </div>`;
}

    ['item_length', t('item_length'), p.item_length || ''],
    ['item_width', t('item_width'), p.item_width || ''],
    ['item_height', t('item_height'), p.item_height || ''],
    ['dimension_unit', t('dimension_unit'), p.dimension_unit || ''],
    ['package_weight', t('pkg_weight'), p.package_weight || ''],
    ['package_weight_unit', t('pkg_weight_unit'), p.package_weight_unit || ''],
    ['package_length', t('pkg_length'), p.package_length || ''],
    ['package_width', t('pkg_width'), p.package_width || ''],
    ['package_height', t('pkg_height'), p.package_height || ''],
  ];
  return `<div class="drawer-form-grid">${fields.map(([key, label, val]) =>
    `<div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${label}${tipFor(key)}</label>
      <input class="drawer-form-input" data-field="${key}" value="${escHtml(val)}">
    </div>`
  ).join('')}</div>`;
}

  const fields = categoryFieldsConfig.fields || [];
  if (!fields.length) {
    return `<div style="text-align:center;padding:40px 20px;color:var(--text-secondary);">
      <svg width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" style="margin-bottom:12px;opacity:.5;">

      </svg>
      <div style="font-size:14px;margin-bottom:8px;">${t('no_category_fields')}</div>
      <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="openFieldSelector()">${t('configure_fields')}</button>
    </div>`;
  }

  const raw = p._raw || p;
  const catName = categoryFieldsConfig.category || '';
  let html = `<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;margin-bottom:12px;">
    <span style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text-secondary);">${catName ? (lang==='zh'? _getCatZhName(catName): _getCatEnName(catName)) : t('category_fields')} (${fields.length})</span>
    <button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="openFieldSelector()" style="padding:2px 8px;">
      <svg width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="3"></circle><path d="M19.4 15a1.65 1.65 0 0 0 .33 1.82l.06.06a2 2 0 0 1-2.83 2.83l-.06-.06a1.65 1.65 0 0 0-1.82-.33 1.65 1.65 0 0 0-1 1.51V21a2 2 0 0 1-4 0v-.09A1.65 1.65 0 0 0 9 19.4a1.65 1.65 0 0 0-1.82.33l-.06.06a2 2 0 0 1-2.83-2.83l.06-.06A1.65 1.65 0 0 0 4.68 15a1.65 1.65 0 0 0-1.51-1H3a2 2 0 0 1 0-4h.09A1.65 1.65 0 0 0 4.6 8.82 1.65 1.65 0 0 0 4.27 7l-.06-.06a2 2 0 0 1 2.83-2.83l.06.06A1.65 1.65 0 0 0 9 4.6a1.65 1.65 0 0 0 1-1.51V3a2 2 0 0 1 4 0v.09a1.65 1.65 0 0 0 1.08 1.51 1.65 1.65 0 0 0 1.82-.33l.06-.06a2 2 0 0 1 2.83 2.83l-.06.06a1.65 1.65 0 0 0-.33 1.82V9a1.65 1.65 0 0 0 1.51 1H21a2 2 0 0 1 0 4h-.09a1.65 1.65 0 0 0-1.51 1.08z"></path></svg>
    </button>
  </div>
  <div class="drawer-form-grid">`;

  for (const f of fields) {
    const val = raw[f.key] || p[f.key] || '';
    const label = lang === 'zh' ? (f.label_zh || f.key) : (f.label_en || f.key);
    if (f.type === 'select' && f.options) {
      html += `<div class="drawer-form-group">
        <label class="drawer-form-label">${escHtml(label)}</label>
        <select class="drawer-form-select" data-field="${f.key}">
          <option value="" ${!val?'selected':''}>-</option>
          ${f.options.map(o => `<option value="${escHtml(o)}" ${val===o?'selected':''}>${escHtml(o)}</option>`).join('')}
        </select>
      </div>`;
    } else {
      html += `<div class="drawer-form-group">
        <label class="drawer-form-label">${escHtml(label)}</label>
        <input class="drawer-form-input" data-field="${f.key}" value="${escHtml(val)}"
          ${f.type==='number'?'type="number"':'type="text"'}
          ${f.example?`placeholder="${escHtml(f.example)}"`:''}>
      </div>`;
    }
  }
  html += '</div>';
  return html;
}

function renderCategoryFieldsTab(p) {
  return `<div id="dynamicCategoryForm" class="schema-form-shell">
    <div class="task-empty">正在加载官方字段...</div>
  </div>`;
}

function getFormSchemaKey(p) {
  const templateId = p.template_id || '';
  const productType = p.template_product_type || p.product_type || '';
  const variationMode = p.template_variation_mode || 'single';
  return templateId ? `template:${templateId}` : `product:${productType}:${variationMode}`;
}

async function loadFormSchemaForProduct(p) {
  const templateId = p.template_id || '';
  const productType = p.template_product_type || p.product_type || '';
  if (!templateId && !productType) return null;
  const cacheKey = getFormSchemaKey(p);
  if (formSchemaCache.has(cacheKey)) return formSchemaCache.get(cacheKey);

  const params = new URLSearchParams();
  if (templateId) params.set('template_id', templateId);
  if (productType) params.set('product_type', productType);
  if (p.template_variation_mode) params.set('variation_mode', p.template_variation_mode);
  const response = await fetch('/api/form-schema?' + params.toString());
  const data = await response.json();
  if (!data.success) throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to load form schema');
  formSchemaCache.set(cacheKey, data.schema);
  return data.schema;
}

function getDynamicFieldValue(p, field) {
  const raw = p._raw || {};
  const candidates = [
    p[field.key],
    raw[field.key],
    p[field.source_attribute],
    raw[field.source_attribute],
    field.default,
  ];
  for (const candidate of candidates) {
    if (candidate !== undefined && candidate !== null && String(candidate).trim() !== '') {
      return String(candidate);
    }
  }
  return '';
}

function getChildFieldValue(p, child) {
  return getDynamicFieldValue(p, child);
}

function safeJsonParse(text, fallback = null) {
  const raw = String(text || '').trim();
  if (!raw) return fallback;
  try {
    return JSON.parse(raw);
  } catch (_e) {
    return fallback;
  }
}

function hydratePersistedDiagnosticData(product) {
  if (!product) return;
  if (product._previewIssuePayload === undefined) {
    const previewPayload = safeJsonParse(product.preview_issue_payload || product._raw?.preview_issue_payload || '', null);
    product._previewIssuePayload = previewPayload && typeof previewPayload === 'object' ? previewPayload : null;
  }
  if (!product._listingCheck) {
    const listingPayload = safeJsonParse(product.listing_check_payload || product._raw?.listing_check_payload || '', null);
    if (listingPayload && typeof listingPayload === 'object') {
      product._listingCheck = listingPayload;
    }
  }
}

function appendUniqueMessage(items, seen, message) {
  const text = String(message || '').trim();
  if (!text || seen.has(text)) return;
  seen.add(text);
  items.push(text);
}

function appendFieldFeedback(target, key, message) {
  const normalizedKey = String(key || '').trim();
  const normalizedMessage = String(message || '').trim();
  if (!normalizedKey || !normalizedMessage) return;
  const existing = String(target[normalizedKey] || '')
    .split(' | ')
    .map(item => item.trim())
    .filter(Boolean);
  if (!existing.includes(normalizedMessage)) existing.push(normalizedMessage);
  target[normalizedKey] = existing.join(' | ');
}

function normalizeSchemaDiagnosticIssue(issue, defaultSource = 'amazon_preview') {
  if (!issue || typeof issue !== 'object') return null;
  const severity = String(issue.severity || issue.level || 'ERROR').trim().toUpperCase();
  const levelMap = { ERROR: 'error', WARNING: 'warning', WARN: 'warning', INFO: 'info' };
  const attrs = Array.isArray(issue.attributeNames)
    ? issue.attributeNames
    : (Array.isArray(issue.attributes) ? issue.attributes : [issue.attributeNames || issue.attributes].filter(Boolean));
  const categories = Array.isArray(issue.categories)
    ? issue.categories
    : [issue.categories].filter(Boolean);
  return {
    source: String(issue.source || defaultSource || 'amazon_preview').trim() || 'amazon_preview',
    level: levelMap[severity] || String(issue.level || 'error').trim() || 'error',
    severity,
    code: String(issue.code || '').trim(),
    message: String(issue.message || issue.details || '').trim(),
    attributeNames: attrs.map(item => String(item || '').trim()).filter(Boolean),
    categories: categories.map(item => String(item || '').trim().toUpperCase()).filter(Boolean),
  };
}

function getSchemaIssueSourceLabel(source) {
  const key = String(source || '').trim();
  const labels = {
    amazon_preview: lang === 'zh' ? 'Amazon预览' : 'Amazon Preview',
    listing_runtime: lang === 'zh' ? 'Amazon后台' : 'Amazon Listing',
    local_validation: lang === 'zh' ? '本地校验' : 'Local Validation',
    template_rules: lang === 'zh' ? '模板要求' : 'Template Rules',
  };
  return labels[key] || (lang === 'zh' ? '诊断' : 'Diagnostic');
}

function collectTemplateFieldIssues(p) {
  const entries = [];
  const seen = new Set();
  const pushIssues = (texts, level) => {
    (texts || []).forEach(text => {
      const message = String(text || '').trim();
      const key = extractFieldKeyFromSummaryText(message);
      if (!message || !key) return;
      const signature = `${level}|${key}|${message}`;
      if (seen.has(signature)) return;
      seen.add(signature);
      entries.push({
        source: 'template_rules',
        level,
        severity: level === 'error' ? 'ERROR' : 'WARNING',
        code: '',
        message,
        attributeNames: [key],
        categories: [],
        targets: [key],
      });
    });
  };
  pushIssues((p.template_required_missing_fields || '').split(';').map(item => item.trim()).filter(Boolean), 'error');
  pushIssues((p.template_blocking_issues || '').split(';').map(item => item.trim()).filter(Boolean), 'error');
  pushIssues((p.template_recommended_missing_fields || '').split(';').map(item => item.trim()).filter(Boolean), 'warning');
  return entries;
}

function buildSchemaFieldLookup(schema) {
  const lookup = new Map();
  const add = (alias, targets) => {
    const value = String(alias || '').trim();
    if (!value) return;
    [value, value.toLowerCase()].forEach(key => {
      if (!lookup.has(key)) lookup.set(key, new Set());
      const bucket = lookup.get(key);
      (targets || []).forEach(target => {
        const normalizedTarget = String(target || '').trim();
        if (normalizedTarget) bucket.add(normalizedTarget);
      });
    });
  };

  (schema?.sections || []).forEach(section => {
    (section.fields || []).forEach(field => {
      if (field.children && field.children.length) {
        const childKeys = field.children.map(child => child.key).filter(Boolean);
        add(field.key, childKeys);
        add(field.source_attribute, childKeys);
        field.children.forEach(child => {
          add(child.key, [child.key]);
          add(child.source_attribute, [child.key]);
        });
        return;
      }
      add(field.key, [field.key]);
      add(field.source_attribute, [field.key]);
    });
  });

  return lookup;
}

function buildSchemaFieldSectionLookup(schema) {
  const lookup = new Map();
  (schema?.sections || []).forEach(section => {
    (section.fields || []).forEach(field => {
      const keys = field.children && field.children.length
        ? field.children.map(child => child.key).filter(Boolean)
        : [field.key].filter(Boolean);
      keys.forEach(key => lookup.set(String(key || '').trim(), section.key));
    });
  });
  return lookup;
}

function getSchemaSectionStateKey(p, schema, sectionKey) {
  return `${getFormSchemaKey(p)}::${schema?.variation_mode || ''}::${sectionKey}`;
}

function isSchemaSectionExpanded(p, schema, sectionKey) {
  const stateKey = getSchemaSectionStateKey(p, schema, sectionKey);
  if (!schemaSectionState.has(stateKey)) return true;
  return !!schemaSectionState.get(stateKey);
}

function setSchemaSectionExpanded(p, schema, sectionKey, expanded) {
  schemaSectionState.set(getSchemaSectionStateKey(p, schema, sectionKey), !!expanded);
}

function getCurrentSchemaFocus(p) {
  return schemaFocusState && p && schemaFocusState.sku === p.sku ? schemaFocusState : null;
}

function getSchemaSectionLabel(schema, sectionKey) {
  const section = (schema?.sections || []).find(item => item.key === sectionKey);
  if (!section) return sectionKey;
  return lang === 'zh' ? (section.title_zh || section.key) : (section.title_en || section.key);
}

function expandSchemaSectionsForFields(p, schema, fieldKeys) {
  const fieldToSection = buildSchemaFieldSectionLookup(schema);
  const sectionKeys = new Set();
  (fieldKeys || []).forEach(fieldKey => {
    const sectionKey = fieldToSection.get(String(fieldKey || '').trim());
    if (!sectionKey) return;
    sectionKeys.add(sectionKey);
    setSchemaSectionExpanded(p, schema, sectionKey, true);
  });
  return Array.from(sectionKeys);
}

function getSectionIssueCounts(section, feedback) {
  const keys = new Set();
  (section?.fields || []).forEach(field => {
    if (field.children && field.children.length) {
      field.children.forEach(child => {
        if (child?.key) keys.add(child.key);
      });
      return;
    }
    if (field?.key) keys.add(field.key);
  });
  let errorCount = 0;
  let warningCount = 0;
  keys.forEach(key => {
    if (feedback?.fieldErrors?.[key]) errorCount += 1;
    else if (feedback?.fieldWarnings?.[key]) warningCount += 1;
  });
  return { errorCount, warningCount };
}

function appendFieldLinkedIssue(target, key, issue) {
  const normalizedKey = String(key || '').trim();
  if (!normalizedKey || !issue) return;
  if (!target[normalizedKey]) target[normalizedKey] = [];
  const signature = [
    issue.source || '',
    issue.level || '',
    issue.code || '',
    issue.message || '',
  ].join('|');
  if (target[normalizedKey].some(item => item.signature === signature)) return;
  target[normalizedKey].push({
    signature,
    source: issue.source || '',
    level: issue.level || '',
    code: issue.code || '',
    severity: issue.severity || '',
    message: issue.message || '',
  });
}

function countSchemaRenderableFields(schema) {
  return (schema?.sections || []).reduce((total, section) => total + ((section.fields || []).length), 0);
}

function fieldMatchesSchemaIssueFilter(field, feedback) {
  const keys = field.children && field.children.length
    ? field.children.map(child => child.key).filter(Boolean)
    : [field.key].filter(Boolean);
  return keys.some(key => Boolean(feedback?.fieldErrors?.[key] || feedback?.fieldWarnings?.[key]));
}

function hasMeaningfulProductFieldValue(product, fieldKey) {
  const raw = product?._raw || {};
  const candidates = [product?.[fieldKey], raw[fieldKey]];
  return candidates.some(value => value !== undefined && value !== null && String(value).trim() !== '');
}

function issueCanResolveLocally(issue) {
  if (!issue) return false;
  if (issue.source === 'template_rules') return true;
