  const categories = (issue.categories || []).map(item => String(item || '').trim().toUpperCase());
  return categories.includes('MISSING_ATTRIBUTE') || String(issue.code || '').trim() === '90220';
}

function isSchemaIssueResolvedLocally(issue, product) {
  if (!issueCanResolveLocally(issue)) return false;
  const targets = (issue.targets || issue.attributeNames || []).map(item => String(item || '').trim()).filter(Boolean);
  if (targets.length === 0) return false;
  return targets.every(key => hasMeaningfulProductFieldValue(product, key));
}

function getSchemaActionableFieldOrder(schema, feedback) {
  const ordered = [];
  const seen = new Set();
  (schema?.sections || []).forEach(section => {
    (section.fields || []).forEach(field => {
      const keys = field.children && field.children.length
        ? field.children.map(child => child.key).filter(Boolean)
        : [field.key].filter(Boolean);
      keys.forEach(key => {
        if (seen.has(key)) return;
        if (!feedback?.fieldErrors?.[key] && !feedback?.fieldWarnings?.[key]) return;
        seen.add(key);
        ordered.push(key);
      });
    });
  });
  return ordered;
}

function buildSchemaFocusStateForField(p, schema, feedback, fieldKey, fallbackMessage = '') {
  const sectionKey = buildSchemaFieldSectionLookup(schema).get(String(fieldKey || '').trim()) || '';
  const linkedIssue = (feedback?.fieldLinkedIssues?.[fieldKey] || [])[0] || null;
  const fieldMessage = linkedIssue
    ? `${getSchemaIssueSourceLabel(linkedIssue.source)}: ${linkedIssue.message || linkedIssue.code || fieldKey}`
    : (feedback?.fieldErrors?.[fieldKey] || feedback?.fieldWarnings?.[fieldKey] || fallbackMessage || fieldKey);
  const sectionTitles = sectionKey ? [getSchemaSectionLabel(schema, sectionKey)] : [];
  return {
    sku: p.sku,
    message: fieldMessage,
    fieldKeys: [fieldKey],
    sectionKeys: sectionKey ? [sectionKey] : [],
    sectionTitles,
    source: linkedIssue?.source || '',
  };
}

function collectSchemaLinkedIssues(p, schema) {
  hydratePersistedDiagnosticData(p);
  const issues = [];
  const seen = new Set();
  const addIssue = (issue, defaultSource) => {
    const normalized = normalizeSchemaDiagnosticIssue(issue, defaultSource);
    if (!normalized) return;
    const signature = [
      normalized.source,
      normalized.level,
      normalized.code,
      normalized.message,
      normalized.attributeNames.join(','),
    ].join('|');
    if (seen.has(signature)) return;
    seen.add(signature);
    issues.push(normalized);
  };

  const listingCheck = p._listingCheck || null;
  (listingCheck?.preview?.issues || []).forEach(issue => addIssue(issue, 'amazon_preview'));
  (listingCheck?.listing?.issues || []).forEach(issue => addIssue(issue, 'listing_runtime'));
  (p._previewIssuePayload?.issues || []).forEach(issue => addIssue(issue, 'amazon_preview'));

  const lookup = buildSchemaFieldLookup(schema);
  return issues.map(issue => {
    const targetSet = new Set();
    (issue.attributeNames || []).forEach(attribute => {
      const key = String(attribute || '').trim();
      if (!key) return;
      const matches = lookup.get(key) || lookup.get(key.toLowerCase());
      if (!matches) return;
      matches.forEach(fieldKey => targetSet.add(fieldKey));
    });
    return { ...issue, targets: Array.from(targetSet) };
  });
}

function registerDiagnosticJump(payload) {
  const id = `diag_jump_${++diagnosticJumpSeq}`;
  diagnosticJumpRegistry.set(id, payload);
  return id;
}

function extractFieldKeyFromSummaryText(text) {
  const match = /\(([^()]+)\)\s*$/.exec(String(text || '').trim());
  return match ? String(match[1] || '').trim() : '';
}

function resolveDiagnosticTargetKeys(schema, payload) {
  const directKeys = (payload?.fieldKeys || []).map(item => String(item || '').trim()).filter(Boolean);
  if (directKeys.length > 0) return Array.from(new Set(directKeys));
  const attributeNames = (payload?.attributeNames || []).map(item => String(item || '').trim()).filter(Boolean);
  if (!schema || attributeNames.length === 0) return [];
  const lookup = buildSchemaFieldLookup(schema);
  const resolved = new Set();
  attributeNames.forEach(attribute => {
    const matches = lookup.get(attribute) || lookup.get(attribute.toLowerCase());
    if (!matches) return;
    matches.forEach(key => resolved.add(key));
  });
  return Array.from(resolved);
}

function flashDiagnosticField(shell) {
  if (!shell) return;
  shell.classList.remove('diagnostic-focus');
  void shell.offsetWidth;
  shell.classList.add('diagnostic-focus');
  window.setTimeout(() => shell.classList.remove('diagnostic-focus'), 2200);
}

function escapeFieldSelector(value) {
  const text = String(value || '');
  if (window.CSS && typeof window.CSS.escape === 'function') return window.CSS.escape(text);
  return text.replace(/["\\]/g, '\\$&');
}

function focusSchemaFieldKeys(fieldKeys, message = '') {
  const keys = Array.from(new Set((fieldKeys || []).map(item => String(item || '').trim()).filter(Boolean)));
  if (keys.length === 0) {
    showToast('warning', message || '暂时无法定位到对应字段');
    return false;
  }

  let firstShell = null;
  keys.forEach(key => {
    const input = document.querySelector(`#dynamicCategoryForm [data-field="${escapeFieldSelector(key)}"]`);
    if (!input) return;
    const shell = input.closest('.field-input-shell') || input.closest('.drawer-form-group') || input;
    if (!firstShell) firstShell = shell;
    flashDiagnosticField(shell);
  });

  if (!firstShell) {
    showToast('warning', message || '字段未显示在当前官方表单中');
    return false;
  }

  firstShell.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center', inline: 'nearest' });
  const focusable = firstShell.querySelector('[data-field]');
  if (focusable && typeof focusable.focus === 'function') {
    window.setTimeout(() => focusable.focus({ preventScroll: true }), 120);
  }
  if (message) showToast('info', message);
  return true;
}

function renderFieldLinkedIssues(feedback, key) {
  const issues = (feedback?.fieldLinkedIssues?.[key] || []).filter(item => item && item.message);
  if (issues.length === 0) return '';
  return `<div class="field-linked-issues">
    ${issues.map(issue => {
      const label = getSchemaIssueSourceLabel(issue.source);
      const tone = issue.level === 'error' ? 'error' : 'warn';
      const code = issue.code ? ` · ${issue.code}` : '';
      const view = buildMerchantIssueView(drawerProduct, issue, issue.message || '');
      const tech = summarizeTechnicalIssue(issue, issue.message || '');
      return `<div class="field-linked-issue ${tone}">
        <span class="field-linked-source ${tone}">${escHtml(label + code)}</span>
        <span class="field-linked-message">${escHtml(view.primary || issue.message)}</span>
        ${view.secondary ? `<span class="field-linked-raw">${escHtml(view.secondary)}</span>` : ''}
        <span class="field-linked-tech">${escHtml(tech)}</span>
      </div>`;
    }).join('')}
  </div>`;
}

async function jumpToDiagnosticIssue(id) {
  const payload = diagnosticJumpRegistry.get(id);
  if (!payload) return showToast('warning', '这个诊断定位入口已失效，请重新打开抽屉');

  try {
    if (!drawerProduct || drawerProduct.sku !== payload.sku) {
      openDrawer(payload.sku);
    }
    if (!drawerProduct) return showToast('warning', '当前商品不存在，无法定位字段');

    switchDrawerTab('category');
    const schema = await loadFormSchemaForProduct(drawerProduct);
    const targetKeys = resolveDiagnosticTargetKeys(schema, payload);
    const expandedSections = expandSchemaSectionsForFields(drawerProduct, schema, targetKeys);
    schemaFieldFilterMode = 'issues';
    const message = payload.message || (lang === 'zh' ? '已跳转到对应字段' : 'Jumped to linked field');
    schemaFocusState = {
      sku: drawerProduct.sku,
      message,
      fieldKeys: targetKeys,
      sectionKeys: expandedSections,
      sectionTitles: expandedSections.map(sectionKey => getSchemaSectionLabel(schema, sectionKey)),
      source: payload.source || '',
    };
    await hydrateCategoryFieldsTab(drawerProduct);
    focusSchemaFieldKeys(targetKeys, message);
  } catch (e) {
    showToast('error', '字段定位失败: ' + e.message);
  }
}

async function startSchemaFixFlow(product, options = {}) {
  const targetProduct = product || drawerProduct;
  if (!targetProduct) return false;
  const schema = await loadFormSchemaForProduct(targetProduct);
  const feedback = computeSchemaFormFeedback(targetProduct, schema);
  const actionableFields = getSchemaActionableFieldOrder(schema, feedback);
  if (actionableFields.length === 0) {
    schemaFocusState = null;
    schemaFieldFilterMode = 'all';
    await hydrateCategoryFieldsTab(targetProduct);
    showToast('success', lang === 'zh' ? '当前已经没有待处理字段，可以继续做 Amazon 预览。' : 'No field-level issues remain. You can continue to Amazon preview.');
    return false;
  }

  const preferredField = String(options.preferredFieldKey || '').trim();
  const focusField = actionableFields.includes(preferredField) ? preferredField : actionableFields[0];
  const sectionKeys = expandSchemaSectionsForFields(targetProduct, schema, [focusField]);
  schemaFieldFilterMode = 'issues';
  schemaFocusState = {
    ...buildSchemaFocusStateForField(targetProduct, schema, feedback, focusField, options.message || ''),
    sectionKeys,
    sectionTitles: sectionKeys.map(sectionKey => getSchemaSectionLabel(schema, sectionKey)),
  };
  await hydrateCategoryFieldsTab(targetProduct);
  focusSchemaFieldKeys([focusField], schemaFocusState.message);
  return true;
}

async function advanceSchemaFocusAfterSave(product) {
  const targetProduct = product || drawerProduct;
  if (!targetProduct || !getCurrentSchemaFocus(targetProduct)) return false;

  const schema = await loadFormSchemaForProduct(targetProduct);
  const feedback = computeSchemaFormFeedback(targetProduct, schema);
  const actionableFields = getSchemaActionableFieldOrder(schema, feedback);
  const currentFocus = getCurrentSchemaFocus(targetProduct);
  const currentFields = (currentFocus?.fieldKeys || []).map(item => String(item || '').trim()).filter(Boolean);

  if (currentFields.some(fieldKey => actionableFields.includes(fieldKey))) {
    await hydrateCategoryFieldsTab(targetProduct);
    focusSchemaFieldKeys(currentFields, lang === 'zh' ? '这个问题还没完全解决，请继续修改当前字段。' : 'This issue still needs work. Please keep editing the current field.');
    return false;
  }

  if (actionableFields.length === 0) {
    schemaFocusState = null;
    schemaFieldFilterMode = 'all';
    await hydrateCategoryFieldsTab(targetProduct);
    showToast('success', lang === 'zh' ? '太好了，这个商品当前没有待处理字段了。下一步建议先做 Amazon 预览。' : 'Great — this SKU has no remaining field issues. Next step: run Amazon preview.');
    return true;
  }

  const currentIndex = currentFields.length > 0 ? actionableFields.findIndex(fieldKey => fieldKey === currentFields[0]) : -1;
  const nextField = currentIndex >= 0 && actionableFields[currentIndex + 1]
    ? actionableFields[currentIndex + 1]
    : actionableFields[0];
  const sectionKeys = expandSchemaSectionsForFields(targetProduct, schema, [nextField]);
  schemaFieldFilterMode = 'issues';
  schemaFocusState = {
    ...buildSchemaFocusStateForField(targetProduct, schema, feedback, nextField, lang === 'zh' ? '已自动跳到下一项待处理字段。' : 'Moved to the next field that needs attention.'),
    sectionKeys,
    sectionTitles: sectionKeys.map(sectionKey => getSchemaSectionLabel(schema, sectionKey)),
  };
  await hydrateCategoryFieldsTab(targetProduct);
  focusSchemaFieldKeys([nextField], lang === 'zh' ? '已自动跳到下一项待处理字段。' : 'Moved to the next field that needs attention.');
  return true;
}

function renderDiagnosticJumpButton(payload) {
  const hasTargets = ((payload?.fieldKeys || []).length > 0) || ((payload?.attributeNames || []).length > 0);
  if (!hasTargets) return '';
  const id = registerDiagnosticJump(payload);
  return `<button type="button" class="diagnostic-jump-btn" onclick="jumpToDiagnosticIssue('${id}')">${lang === 'zh' ? '定位字段' : 'Jump to field'}</button>`;
}

function setSchemaFieldFilterMode(mode, rerender = true) {
  schemaFieldFilterMode = mode === 'issues' ? 'issues' : 'all';
  if (rerender && drawerProduct && drawerTab === 'category') renderDrawerContent();
}

async function toggleSchemaSection(sectionKey) {
  if (!drawerProduct) return;
  try {
    const schema = await loadFormSchemaForProduct(drawerProduct);
    const expanded = isSchemaSectionExpanded(drawerProduct, schema, sectionKey);
    setSchemaSectionExpanded(drawerProduct, schema, sectionKey, !expanded);
    renderDrawerContent();
  } catch (e) {
    showToast('error', '分区切换失败: ' + e.message);
  }
}

function computeSchemaFormFeedback(p, schema) {
  const errors = [];
  const warnings = [];
  const errorSet = new Set();
  const warningSet = new Set();
  const fieldErrors = {};
  const fieldWarnings = {};
  const fieldLinkedIssues = {};
  const issueStats = {
    preview: { error: 0, warning: 0 },
    listing: { error: 0, warning: 0 },
    unmapped: 0,
  };
  if (!schema || !schema.sections) {
    return { errors, warnings, fieldErrors, fieldWarnings, fieldLinkedIssues, issueStats, actionableFieldCount: 0 };
  }
  for (const section of schema.sections) {
    for (const field of section.fields || []) {
      if (field.field_type === 'measurement' && field.children) {
        const missing = field.children.filter(child => !String(getChildFieldValue(p, child) || '').trim());
        if (field.level === 'required' && missing.length > 0) {
          const message = `${formatOfficialFieldLabel(field.key, field.label_zh || '', field.label_en || field.key)} 缺少 ${missing.map(item => formatOfficialFieldLabel(item.key, item.label_zh || '', item.label_en || item.key)).join(' / ')}`;
          appendUniqueMessage(errors, errorSet, message);
          missing.forEach(child => appendFieldFeedback(fieldErrors, child.key, message));
        }
        continue;
      }
      if (field.field_type === 'dimension_3d' && field.children) {
        const missing = field.children.filter(child => !String(getChildFieldValue(p, child) || '').trim());
        if (field.level === 'required' && missing.length > 0) {
          const message = `${formatOfficialFieldLabel(field.key, field.label_zh || '', field.label_en || field.key)} 未填写完整`;
          appendUniqueMessage(errors, errorSet, message);
          missing.forEach(child => appendFieldFeedback(fieldErrors, child.key, message));
        }
        continue;
      }
      const value = String(getDynamicFieldValue(p, field) || '').trim();
      if (field.level === 'required' && !value) {
        const message = `缺少 ${formatOfficialFieldLabel(field.key, field.label_zh || '', field.label_en || field.key)}`;
        appendUniqueMessage(errors, errorSet, message);
        appendFieldFeedback(fieldErrors, field.key, message);
        continue;
      }
      if (field.field_type === 'number' && value && Number.isNaN(Number(value))) {
        const message = `${formatOfficialFieldLabel(field.key, field.label_zh || '', field.label_en || field.key)} 不是有效数字`;
        appendUniqueMessage(warnings, warningSet, message);
        appendFieldFeedback(fieldWarnings, field.key, message);
      }
      if (field.field_type === 'image_locator' && value && !isMediaLocator(value)) {
        const message = `${formatOfficialFieldLabel(field.key, field.label_zh || '', field.label_en || field.key)} 不是有效图片地址`;
        appendUniqueMessage(warnings, warningSet, message);
        appendFieldFeedback(fieldWarnings, field.key, message);
      }
    }
  }

  const linkedIssues = collectTemplateFieldIssues(p).concat(collectSchemaLinkedIssues(p, schema));
  linkedIssues.forEach(issue => {
    if (isSchemaIssueResolvedLocally(issue, p)) return;
    if (issue.source === 'listing_runtime') {
      if (issue.level === 'error') issueStats.listing.error += 1;
      else if (issue.level === 'warning') issueStats.listing.warning += 1;
    } else if (issue.source === 'amazon_preview') {
      if (issue.level === 'error') issueStats.preview.error += 1;
      else if (issue.level === 'warning') issueStats.preview.warning += 1;
    }

    const summaryMessage = `${getSchemaIssueSourceLabel(issue.source)}: ${issue.message || issue.code || (lang === 'zh' ? '字段需要处理' : 'Field needs attention')}`;
    if (!issue.targets.length) {
      if (issue.source !== 'template_rules') issueStats.unmapped += 1;
      if (issue.level === 'error') appendUniqueMessage(errors, errorSet, summaryMessage);
      else if (issue.level === 'warning') appendUniqueMessage(warnings, warningSet, summaryMessage);
      return;
    }

    if (issue.level === 'error') appendUniqueMessage(errors, errorSet, summaryMessage);
    else if (issue.level === 'warning') appendUniqueMessage(warnings, warningSet, summaryMessage);

    issue.targets.forEach(key => {
      appendFieldLinkedIssue(fieldLinkedIssues, key, issue);
      const inlineMessage = issue.level === 'error'
        ? `${getSchemaIssueSourceLabel(issue.source)}需要处理，详情见下方`
        : `${getSchemaIssueSourceLabel(issue.source)}需要确认，详情见下方`;
      if (issue.level === 'error') appendFieldFeedback(fieldErrors, key, inlineMessage);
      else if (issue.level === 'warning' && !fieldErrors[key]) appendFieldFeedback(fieldWarnings, key, inlineMessage);
    });
  });

  const actionableFieldCount = Object.keys({ ...fieldErrors, ...fieldWarnings }).length;
  return { errors, warnings, fieldErrors, fieldWarnings, fieldLinkedIssues, issueStats, actionableFieldCount };
}

function renderSchemaFeedback(feedback, p = null) {
  const previewCount = Number(feedback?.issueStats?.preview?.error || 0) + Number(feedback?.issueStats?.preview?.warning || 0);
  const listingCount = Number(feedback?.issueStats?.listing?.error || 0) + Number(feedback?.issueStats?.listing?.warning || 0);
  const unmappedCount = Number(feedback?.issueStats?.unmapped || 0);
  const linkedSummary = [];
  const focus = getCurrentSchemaFocus(p);
  if (previewCount > 0) linkedSummary.push(`${lang === 'zh' ? 'Amazon预览问题' : 'Amazon preview issues'} ${previewCount} ${lang === 'zh' ? '项' : ''}`.trim());
  if (listingCount > 0) linkedSummary.push(`${lang === 'zh' ? 'Amazon后台问题' : 'Amazon listing issues'} ${listingCount} ${lang === 'zh' ? '项' : ''}`.trim());
  if (unmappedCount > 0) linkedSummary.push(`${lang === 'zh' ? '未能定位到字段' : 'Unmapped issues'} ${unmappedCount} ${lang === 'zh' ? '项' : ''}`.trim());
  return `<strong>${feedback.errors.length > 0 ? '当前未就绪' : '当前表单基本可用'}</strong>
    <div class="schema-feedback-body">
      ${feedback.errors.length > 0
        ? `<div>缺少/错误：${escHtml(feedback.errors.slice(0, 6).join('；'))}</div>`
        : `<div>必填字段已基本补齐，可继续执行完整校验或 Amazon preview。</div>`}
      ${feedback.warnings.length > 0 ? `<div>提示：${escHtml(feedback.warnings.slice(0, 4).join('；'))}</div>` : ''}
      ${linkedSummary.length > 0 ? `<div>联动诊断：${escHtml(linkedSummary.join('；'))}</div>` : ''}
      ${focus ? `<div class="schema-focus-banner">
        <strong>${lang === 'zh' ? '正在处理这个问题' : 'Currently fixing this issue'}</strong>
        <div>${escHtml(focus.message || '')}</div>
        <div>${escHtml((lang === 'zh'
          ? `我已经帮你展开 ${focus.sectionTitles?.join(' / ') || '对应分区'}，并切到“只看待处理字段”。请直接修改蓝色高亮字段。`
          : `I expanded ${focus.sectionTitles?.join(' / ') || 'the matching section'} and switched to issue-only mode for you. Edit the blue highlighted field first.`))}</div>
      </div>` : ''}
    </div>`;
}

function renderSchemaFilterBar(schema, feedback) {
  const totalFields = countSchemaRenderableFields(schema);
  const issueFields = (schema?.sections || []).reduce(
    (total, section) => total + ((section.fields || []).filter(field => fieldMatchesSchemaIssueFilter(field, feedback)).length),
    0
  );
  return `<div class="schema-filter-bar">
    <button type="button" class="schema-filter-chip ${schemaFieldFilterMode === 'all' ? 'active' : ''}" onclick="setSchemaFieldFilterMode('all')">
      <span>${lang === 'zh' ? '显示全部字段' : 'Show all fields'}</span>
      <strong>${totalFields}</strong>
    </button>
    <button type="button" class="schema-filter-chip ${schemaFieldFilterMode === 'issues' ? 'active' : ''}" onclick="setSchemaFieldFilterMode('issues')">
      <span>${lang === 'zh' ? '只看需要修改' : 'Only show fields to fix'}</span>
      <strong>${issueFields}</strong>
    </button>
  </div>`;
}

function buildVisibleSchemaSections(schema, feedback) {
  const visibleSections = [];
  for (const section of schema?.sections || []) {
    const filteredFields = schemaFieldFilterMode === 'issues'
      ? (section.fields || []).filter(field => fieldMatchesSchemaIssueFilter(field, feedback))
      : (section.fields || []);
    if (filteredFields.length === 0) continue;
    visibleSections.push({ ...section, fields: filteredFields });
  }
  return visibleSections;
}

function renderSchemaFieldControl(p, field, feedback) {
  const val = getDynamicFieldValue(p, field);
  const label = formatOfficialFieldLabel(field.key, field.label_zh || '', field.label_en || field.key);
  const levelBadge = field.level === 'required'
    ? '<span class="field-level-badge required">必填</span>'
    : (field.level === 'recommended' ? '<span class="field-level-badge recommended">建议</span>' : '<span class="field-level-badge optional">选填</span>');
  const hint = [field.description, field.requirement_note, field.example ? `示例: ${field.example}` : '']
    .filter(Boolean)
    .join(' · ');
  const meta = `<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-top:4px;line-height:1.5;">${escHtml((hint ? `官方字段：${field.key} · ${hint}` : `官方字段：${field.key}`))}</div>`;
  const fieldErrors = (feedback && feedback.fieldErrors) || {};
  const fieldWarnings = (feedback && feedback.fieldWarnings) || {};
  const stateClass = key => fieldErrors[key] ? 'error' : (fieldWarnings[key] ? 'warn' : '');
  const stateText = key => fieldErrors[key] || fieldWarnings[key] || '';

  if (field.field_type === 'measurement' && field.children) {
    const [valueField, unitField] = field.children;
    return `<div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${escHtml(label)} ${levelBadge}</label>
      <div class="compound-row">
        <div class="field-input-shell ${stateClass(valueField.key)}">
          <input class="drawer-form-input ${stateClass(valueField.key)}" type="number" step="0.01" data-field="${valueField.key}" value="${escHtml(getChildFieldValue(p, valueField))}" placeholder="${escHtml(valueField.example || '')}">
          <div class="field-inline-feedback">${escHtml(stateText(valueField.key))}</div>
          ${renderFieldLinkedIssues(feedback, valueField.key)}
        </div>
        <div class="field-input-shell ${stateClass(unitField.key)}">
          <input class="drawer-form-input ${stateClass(unitField.key)}" type="text" data-field="${unitField.key}" value="${escHtml(getChildFieldValue(p, unitField))}" placeholder="${escHtml(unitField.example || unitField.default || 'unit')}">
          <div class="field-inline-feedback">${escHtml(stateText(unitField.key))}</div>
          ${renderFieldLinkedIssues(feedback, unitField.key)}
        </div>
      </div>
      ${meta}
    </div>`;
  }

  if (field.field_type === 'dimension_3d' && field.children) {
    const [lengthField, widthField, heightField, unitField] = field.children;
    return `<div class="drawer-form-group full-width">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${escHtml(label)} ${levelBadge}</label>
      <div class="compound-grid">
        <div class="field-input-shell ${stateClass(lengthField.key)}">
          <input class="drawer-form-input ${stateClass(lengthField.key)}" type="number" step="0.01" data-field="${lengthField.key}" value="${escHtml(getChildFieldValue(p, lengthField))}" placeholder="${escHtml(lengthField.label_en || 'Length')}">
          <div class="field-inline-feedback">${escHtml(stateText(lengthField.key))}</div>
          ${renderFieldLinkedIssues(feedback, lengthField.key)}
        </div>
        <div class="field-input-shell ${stateClass(widthField.key)}">
          <input class="drawer-form-input ${stateClass(widthField.key)}" type="number" step="0.01" data-field="${widthField.key}" value="${escHtml(getChildFieldValue(p, widthField))}" placeholder="${escHtml(widthField.label_en || 'Width')}">
          <div class="field-inline-feedback">${escHtml(stateText(widthField.key))}</div>
          ${renderFieldLinkedIssues(feedback, widthField.key)}
        </div>
        <div class="field-input-shell ${stateClass(heightField.key)}">
          <input class="drawer-form-input ${stateClass(heightField.key)}" type="number" step="0.01" data-field="${heightField.key}" value="${escHtml(getChildFieldValue(p, heightField))}" placeholder="${escHtml(heightField.label_en || 'Height')}">
          <div class="field-inline-feedback">${escHtml(stateText(heightField.key))}</div>
          ${renderFieldLinkedIssues(feedback, heightField.key)}
        </div>
        <div class="field-input-shell ${stateClass(unitField.key)}">
          <input class="drawer-form-input ${stateClass(unitField.key)}" type="text" data-field="${unitField.key}" value="${escHtml(getChildFieldValue(p, unitField))}" placeholder="${escHtml(unitField.default || 'Unit')}">
          <div class="field-inline-feedback">${escHtml(stateText(unitField.key))}</div>
          ${renderFieldLinkedIssues(feedback, unitField.key)}
        </div>
      </div>
      ${meta}
    </div>`;
  }

  if (field.field_type === 'image_locator') {
    const previewable = isWebImageUrl(val);
    return `<div class="drawer-form-group full-width">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${escHtml(label)} ${levelBadge}</label>
      <div class="field-input-shell ${stateClass(field.key)}">
        <input class="drawer-form-input ${stateClass(field.key)}" type="text" data-field="${field.key}" value="${escHtml(val)}" placeholder="${escHtml(field.example || 'https://...')}">
        <div class="field-inline-feedback">${escHtml(stateText(field.key))}</div>
        ${renderFieldLinkedIssues(feedback, field.key)}
      </div>
      ${previewable ? `<div class="schema-image-preview"><img src="${escHtml(val)}" alt=""></div>` : ''}
      ${meta}
    </div>`;
  }

  if (field.field_type === 'textarea') {
    return `<div class="drawer-form-group" style="grid-column:1/-1;">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${escHtml(label)} ${levelBadge}</label>
      <div class="field-input-shell ${stateClass(field.key)}">
        <textarea class="drawer-form-input ${stateClass(field.key)}" data-field="${field.key}" rows="5" placeholder="${escHtml(field.example || '')}">${escHtml(val)}</textarea>
        <div class="field-inline-feedback">${escHtml(stateText(field.key))}</div>
        ${renderFieldLinkedIssues(feedback, field.key)}
      </div>
      ${meta}
    </div>`;
  }

  if (field.field_type === 'select' || field.field_type === 'boolean') {
    const options = field.field_type === 'boolean'
      ? ['', 'true', 'false']
      : [''].concat((field.enum_values || []).map(item => String(item)));
    const optionLabels = field.field_type === 'boolean'
      ? {'': '-', 'true': 'True', 'false': 'False'}
      : {};
    return `<div class="drawer-form-group">
      <label class="drawer-form-label">${escHtml(label)} ${levelBadge}</label>
      <div class="field-input-shell ${stateClass(field.key)}">
        <select class="drawer-form-select ${stateClass(field.key)}" data-field="${field.key}">
          ${options.map(option => {
            const selected = String(val).toLowerCase() === String(option).toLowerCase() ? 'selected' : '';
            return `<option value="${escHtml(option)}" ${selected}>${escHtml(optionLabels[option] || option || '-')}</option>`;
          }).join('')}
        </select>
        <div class="field-inline-feedback">${escHtml(stateText(field.key))}</div>
        ${renderFieldLinkedIssues(feedback, field.key)}
      </div>
      ${meta}
    </div>`;
  }

  const inputType = field.field_type === 'number' ? 'number' : (field.field_type === 'date' ? 'date' : 'text');
  const extraAttrs = field.field_type === 'number' ? 'step="0.01"' : '';
  return `<div class="drawer-form-group">
    <label class="drawer-form-label">${escHtml(label)} ${levelBadge}</label>
    <div class="field-input-shell ${stateClass(field.key)}">
      <input class="drawer-form-input ${stateClass(field.key)}" type="${inputType}" ${extraAttrs} data-field="${field.key}" value="${escHtml(val)}" placeholder="${escHtml(field.example || '')}">
      <div class="field-inline-feedback">${escHtml(stateText(field.key))}</div>
      ${renderFieldLinkedIssues(feedback, field.key)}
    </div>
    ${meta}
  </div>`;
}

function renderFormSchemaIntoHtml(p, schema) {
  if (!schema || !schema.sections || schema.sections.length === 0) {
    return renderLegacyCategoryFieldsTab(p);
  }
  const feedback = computeSchemaFormFeedback(p, schema);
  const visibleSections = buildVisibleSchemaSections(schema, feedback);
  let html = `<div class="schema-form-meta">
    <div class="drawer-status-chip default"><span class="drawer-status-label">Template</span><strong>${escHtml(schema.template_id || '-')}</strong></div>
    <div class="drawer-status-chip default"><span class="drawer-status-label">Product Type</span><strong>${escHtml(schema.product_type || '-')}</strong></div>
    <div class="drawer-status-chip default"><span class="drawer-status-label">Required</span><strong>${escHtml(String(schema.required_total || 0))}</strong></div>
    <div class="drawer-status-chip default"><span class="drawer-status-label">Recommended</span><strong>${escHtml(String(schema.recommended_total || 0))}</strong></div>
  </div>`;
  html += `<div class="schema-feedback ${feedback.errors.length > 0 ? 'danger' : (feedback.warnings.length > 0 ? 'warn' : 'success')}">${renderSchemaFeedback(feedback, p)}</div>`;
  html += renderSchemaFilterBar(schema, feedback);
  if (visibleSections.length === 0) {
    return html + `<div class="schema-empty-state">
      <strong>${lang === 'zh' ? '当前没有需要处理的字段' : 'No fields need attention right now'}</strong>
      <div>${lang === 'zh' ? '这通常表示当前商品没有命中的字段级问题。你也可以切回“显示全部字段”继续人工检查。' : 'This usually means there are no field-level issues for this SKU. You can switch back to show all fields for a manual review.'}</div>
    </div>`;
  }
  for (const section of visibleSections) {
    const expanded = isSchemaSectionExpanded(p, schema, section.key);
    const sectionTitle = lang === 'zh' ? section.title_zh : section.title_en;
    const issueCounts = getSectionIssueCounts(section, feedback);
    const statusBadge = issueCounts.errorCount > 0
      ? `<span class="schema-section-badge error">${issueCounts.errorCount}${lang === 'zh' ? ' 个问题' : ' issues'}</span>`
      : (issueCounts.warningCount > 0
        ? `<span class="schema-section-badge warn">${issueCounts.warningCount}${lang === 'zh' ? ' 个提示' : ' hints'}</span>`
        : `<span class="schema-section-badge default">${(section.fields || []).length}${lang === 'zh' ? ' 项字段' : ' fields'}</span>`);
    html += `<div class="schema-form-section ${expanded ? '' : 'collapsed'}" data-section-key="${escHtml(section.key)}">
      <button type="button" class="schema-form-section-toggle" onclick="toggleSchemaSection(${JSON.stringify(section.key)})" aria-expanded="${expanded ? 'true' : 'false'}">
        <span class="schema-form-section-title"><span class="schema-section-chevron">${expanded ? '▾' : '▸'}</span>${section.icon || '📄'} ${escHtml(sectionTitle)}</span>
        <span class="schema-form-section-tools">
          ${statusBadge}
          <span class="schema-section-toggle-text">${expanded ? (lang === 'zh' ? '收起' : 'Collapse') : (lang === 'zh' ? '展开' : 'Expand')}</span>
        </span>
      </button>
      <div class="schema-form-section-body" ${expanded ? '' : 'hidden'}>
        <div class="drawer-form-grid">
        ${section.fields.map(field => renderSchemaFieldControl(p, field, feedback)).join('')}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }
  return html;
}

async function hydrateCategoryFieldsTab(p) {
  const container = document.getElementById('dynamicCategoryForm');
  if (!container || !drawerProduct || drawerTab !== 'category') return;
  try {
    const schema = await loadFormSchemaForProduct(p);
    container.innerHTML = renderFormSchemaIntoHtml(p, schema);
    const applyFeedback = () => {
      const feedback = computeSchemaFormFeedback(drawerProduct, schema);
      const summary = container.querySelector('.schema-feedback');
      if (summary) {
        summary.classList.remove('success', 'warn', 'danger');
        summary.classList.add(feedback.errors.length > 0 ? 'danger' : (feedback.warnings.length > 0 ? 'warn' : 'success'));
        summary.innerHTML = renderSchemaFeedback(feedback, drawerProduct);
      }
      container.querySelectorAll('[data-field]').forEach(input => {
        const key = input.getAttribute('data-field');
        if (!key) return;
        const shell = input.closest('.field-input-shell');
        const feedbackEl = shell ? shell.querySelector('.field-inline-feedback') : null;
        const error = feedback.fieldErrors[key] || '';
        const warn = feedback.fieldWarnings[key] || '';
        input.classList.remove('error', 'warn');
        if (shell) shell.classList.remove('error', 'warn');
        if (error) {
          input.classList.add('error');
          if (shell) shell.classList.add('error');
        } else if (warn) {
          input.classList.add('warn');
          if (shell) shell.classList.add('warn');
        }
        if (feedbackEl) feedbackEl.textContent = error || warn || '';
      });
    };
    container.querySelectorAll('[data-field]').forEach(input => {
      input.addEventListener('input', () => {
        const field = input.getAttribute('data-field');
        if (!field || !drawerProduct) return;
        drawerProduct[field] = input.value;
        applyFeedback();
      });
      input.addEventListener('change', applyFeedback);
    });
    applyFeedback();
  } catch (e) {
    console.warn('dynamic form schema failed', e);
    container.innerHTML = renderLegacyCategoryFieldsTab(p);
  }
}

function _getCatZhName(key) {
  if (!fieldRegistry) return key;
  const cat = fieldRegistry.categories[key];
  return cat ? cat.name_zh : key;
}
function _getCatEnName(key) {
  if (!fieldRegistry) return key;
  const cat = fieldRegistry.categories[key];
  return cat ? cat.name_en : key;
}

// ===== 17c. Field Selector Modal =====
async function loadFieldRegistry() {
  if (fieldRegistry) return fieldRegistry;
  try {
    const r = await fetch('/api/field-registry');
    const d = await r.json();
    if (d.success) fieldRegistry = d.registry;
    return fieldRegistry;
  } catch(e) { return null; }
}

async function loadSelectedFields() {
  try {
    const r = await fetch('/api/selected-fields');
    const d = await r.json();
    if (d.success && d.config) {
      categoryFieldsConfig = d.config;
      // 需要从注册表补全字段定义
      if (categoryFieldsConfig.fields && categoryFieldsConfig.fields.length && typeof categoryFieldsConfig.fields[0] === 'string') {
        await loadFieldRegistry();
        if (fieldRegistry) {
          const allFields = {};
          for (const cat of Object.values(fieldRegistry.categories || {})) {
            for (const f of cat.fields || []) allFields[f.key] = f;
          }
          for (const f of fieldRegistry.cross_category_fields || []) allFields[f.key] = f;
          categoryFieldsConfig.fields = categoryFieldsConfig.fields.map(k => allFields[k] || {key:k, label_en:k, label_zh:k, type:'text'});
        }
      }
    }
  } catch(e) {}
}

async function openFieldSelector() {
  await loadFieldRegistry();
  if (!fieldRegistry) { showToast('error', 'Failed to load field registry'); return; }

  const selectedKeys = new Set((categoryFieldsConfig.fields || []).map(f => typeof f === 'string' ? f : f.key));
  const currentCat = categoryFieldsConfig.category || '';

  let html = `<div class="field-selector-modal" id="fieldSelectorModal">
    <div class="field-selector-backdrop" onclick="closeFieldSelector()"></div>
    <div class="field-selector-dialog">
      <div class="field-selector-header">
        <h3>${t('field_selector')}</h3>
        <button class="drawer-close" onclick="closeFieldSelector()">&times;</button>
      </div>
      <div class="field-selector-body">
        <div class="field-selector-cats">
          <div class="field-selector-cat-title">${t('select_category')}</div>`;

  // Category buttons
  for (const [key, cat] of Object.entries(fieldRegistry.categories)) {
    const name = lang === 'zh' ? cat.name_zh : cat.name_en;
    const icon = cat.icon || '';
    html += `<button class="field-cat-btn ${currentCat===key?'active':''}"
      onclick="selectFieldCategory('${key}')" data-cat="${key}">
      ${icon} ${name} <span class="field-cat-count">${cat.fields.length}</span>
    </button>`;
  }

  html += `</div>
        <div class="field-selector-fields" id="fieldSelectorFields">
          <div class="field-selector-search">
            <input type="text" placeholder="${t('search_fields')}" oninput="filterFieldList(this.value)" id="fieldSearchInput">
          </div>
          <div class="field-selector-list" id="fieldSelectorList">`;

  // If a category is selected, show its fields; otherwise show cross-category
  const fieldsToShow = currentCat && fieldRegistry.categories[currentCat]
    ? fieldRegistry.categories[currentCat].fields
    : fieldRegistry.cross_category_fields || [];

  for (const f of fieldsToShow) {
    const checked = selectedKeys.has(f.key) ? 'checked' : '';
    const label = lang === 'zh' ? (f.label_zh || f.key) : (f.label_en || f.key);
    html += `<label class="field-item" data-key="${f.key}" data-search="${f.key} ${f.label_en||''} ${f.label_zh||''}">
      <input type="checkbox" ${checked} value="${f.key}" onchange="toggleFieldSelection(this)">
      <span class="field-item-label">${escHtml(label)}</span>
      <span class="field-item-key">${f.key}</span>
    </label>`;
  }

  // cross-category fields at bottom
  if (currentCat) {
    html += `<div class="field-section-divider">${lang==='zh'?'跨品类通用字段':'Cross-Category Fields'}</div>`;
    for (const f of fieldRegistry.cross_category_fields || []) {
      const checked = selectedKeys.has(f.key) ? 'checked' : '';
      const label = lang === 'zh' ? (f.label_zh || f.key) : (f.label_en || f.key);
      html += `<label class="field-item" data-key="${f.key}" data-search="${f.key} ${f.label_en||''} ${f.label_zh||''}">
        <input type="checkbox" ${checked} value="${f.key}" onchange="toggleFieldSelection(this)">
        <span class="field-item-label">${escHtml(label)}</span>
        <span class="field-item-key">${f.key}</span>
      </label>`;
    }
  }

  html += `</div></div>
        <div class="field-selector-selected" id="fieldSelectorSelected">
          <div class="field-selector-cat-title">${t('selected_fields')} (<span id="selectedCount">${selectedKeys.size}</span>)</div>
          <div class="field-selected-list" id="fieldSelectedList">`;
  for (const key of selectedKeys) {
    html += `<span class="field-tag" data-key="${key}">${key} <button onclick="removeFieldSelection('${key}')">&times;</button></span>`;
  }
  html += `</div></div></div>
      <div class="field-selector-footer">
        <button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="closeFieldSelector()">${t('cancel')}</button>
        <button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="applyFieldSelection()">${t('apply_fields')}</button>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>`;

  document.body.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', html);
}

function closeFieldSelector() {
  const modal = document.getElementById('fieldSelectorModal');
  if (modal) modal.remove();
}

function selectFieldCategory(catKey) {
  if (!fieldRegistry) return;
  // Update active button
  document.querySelectorAll('.field-cat-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.cat === catKey));
  // Update category in config
  categoryFieldsConfig.category = catKey;

  // Collect selected keys from right panel TAGS (not checkboxes - those get destroyed on category switch)
  const selectedKeys = new Set();
  document.querySelectorAll('#fieldSelectedList .field-tag').forEach(tag => selectedKeys.add(tag.dataset.key));

  const cat = fieldRegistry.categories[catKey];
  if (!cat) return;

  let html = '';
  for (const f of cat.fields) {
    const checked = selectedKeys.has(f.key) ? 'checked' : '';
    const label = lang === 'zh' ? (f.label_zh || f.key) : (f.label_en || f.key);
    html += `<label class="field-item" data-key="${f.key}" data-search="${f.key} ${f.label_en||''} ${f.label_zh||''}">
      <input type="checkbox" ${checked} value="${f.key}" onchange="toggleFieldSelection(this)">
      <span class="field-item-label">${escHtml(label)}</span>
      <span class="field-item-key">${f.key}</span>
    </label>`;
  }
  // Cross-category
  html += `<div class="field-section-divider">${lang==='zh'?'跨品类通用字段':'Cross-Category Fields'}</div>`;
  for (const f of fieldRegistry.cross_category_fields || []) {
    const checked = selectedKeys.has(f.key) ? 'checked' : '';
    const label = lang === 'zh' ? (f.label_zh || f.key) : (f.label_en || f.key);
    html += `<label class="field-item" data-key="${f.key}" data-search="${f.key} ${f.label_en||''} ${f.label_zh||''}">
      <input type="checkbox" ${checked} value="${f.key}" onchange="toggleFieldSelection(this)">
      <span class="field-item-label">${escHtml(label)}</span>
      <span class="field-item-key">${f.key}</span>
    </label>`;
  }

  document.getElementById('fieldSelectorList').innerHTML = html;
  // Clear search
  const si = document.getElementById('fieldSearchInput');
  if (si) si.value = '';
}

function filterFieldList(query) {
  const q = query.toLowerCase().trim();
  document.querySelectorAll('#fieldSelectorList .field-item').forEach(el => {
    const search = (el.dataset.search || '').toLowerCase();
    el.style.display = !q || search.includes(q) ? '' : 'none';
  });
}

function toggleFieldSelection(cb) {
  const key = cb.value;
  const list = document.getElementById('fieldSelectedList');
  const countEl = document.getElementById('selectedCount');
  if (cb.checked) {
    // Avoid duplicate tags
    if (!list.querySelector(`[data-key="${key}"]`)) {
      list.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend',
        `<span class="field-tag" data-key="${key}">${key} <button onclick="removeFieldSelection('${key}')">&times;</button></span>`);
    }
  } else {
    const tag = list.querySelector(`[data-key="${key}"]`);
    if (tag) tag.remove();
  }
  countEl.textContent = list.querySelectorAll('.field-tag').length;
}

function removeFieldSelection(key) {
  // Uncheck the checkbox
  const cb = document.querySelector(`#fieldSelectorList input[value="${key}"]`);
  if (cb) cb.checked = false;
  // Remove tag
  const tag = document.querySelector(`#fieldSelectedList [data-key="${key}"]`);
  if (tag) tag.remove();
  document.getElementById('selectedCount').textContent =
    document.querySelectorAll('#fieldSelectedList .field-tag').length;
}

async function applyFieldSelection() {
  const selectedKeys = [];
  document.querySelectorAll('#fieldSelectedList .field-tag').forEach(tag => {
    selectedKeys.push(tag.dataset.key);
  });

  const catKey = categoryFieldsConfig.category || '';

  // Build full field definitions from registry
  const allFields = {};
  if (fieldRegistry) {
    for (const cat of Object.values(fieldRegistry.categories || {})) {
      for (const f of cat.fields || []) allFields[f.key] = f;
    }
    for (const f of fieldRegistry.cross_category_fields || []) allFields[f.key] = f;
  }

  categoryFieldsConfig = {
    category: catKey,
    fields: selectedKeys.map(k => allFields[k] || {key:k, label_en:k, label_zh:k, type:'text'})
  };

  // Save to server
  try {
    await fetch('/api/selected-fields', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},
      body: JSON.stringify({ category: catKey, fields: selectedKeys })
    });
  } catch(e) {}

  closeFieldSelector();
  showToast('success', lang==='zh' ? `已选择 ${selectedKeys.length} 个品类字段` : `${selectedKeys.length} category fields selected`);
  // Re-render drawer if open
  if (drawerProduct && drawerTab === 'category') renderDrawerContent();
}

// ===== 18. Drawer Actions =====
async function saveDrawerChanges() {
  if (!drawerProduct) return;
  const inputs = document.querySelectorAll('#drawerBody [data-field]');
  const updates = {};
  inputs.forEach(inp => {
    const field = inp.getAttribute('data-field');
    updates[field] = inp.value;
    drawerProduct[field] = inp.value;
  });

  if (currentFile) {
    try {
      const response = await fetch('/api/update-product', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ file: currentFile, file_version: currentFileVersion, sku: drawerProduct.sku, updates })
      });
      const data = await response.json();
      if (data.error) return showToast('error', data.error);
      if (data.file_version) currentFileVersion = Number(data.file_version || currentFileVersion);
    } catch (e) {
      return showToast('error', '保存失败: ' + e.message);
    }
  }

  showToast('success', '已保存到文件');
  applyFilter();
  if (drawerTab === 'category' && getCurrentSchemaFocus(drawerProduct)) {
    await advanceSchemaFocusAfterSave(drawerProduct);
  }
}

async function validateDrawerProduct() {
  if (!drawerProduct) return;
  try {
    const response = await fetch('/api/validate', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ products: [normalizeProductForValidation(drawerProduct)] })
    });
    const data = await response.json();
    if (data.error) return showToast('error', data.error);
    if (data.results && data.results[0]) {
      applyValidationResult(drawerProduct, data.results[0]);
      renderDrawerContent();
      updateStats();
      applyFilter();
      loadTaskCenter();
      if (drawerProduct._validErrors && drawerProduct._validErrors.length > 0) {
        showValidationIssues(drawerProduct.sku);
      } else {
        showToast(drawerProduct._validWarnings && drawerProduct._validWarnings.length > 0 ? 'warning' : 'success', '校验完成');
      }
    }
  } catch (e) {
    showToast('error', '校验失败: ' + e.message);
  }
}

function showListingCheckReport(results) {
  const statusBadge = (s) => {
    const map = { pass: ['通过', 'success'], warn: ['警告', 'warn'], fail: ['失败', 'danger'] };
    const [label, tone] = map[s] || [s || '-', 'default'];
    return `<span class="task-badge ${tone}">${label}</span>`;
  };
  const issueIcon = (level) => level === 'error' ? '&#10060;' : (level === 'warning' ? '&#9888;&#65039;' : '&#8505;&#65039;');

  const rows = (results || []).map(result => {
    const local = result.local || {};
    const preview = result.preview || {};
    const listing = result.listing || {};
    const media = result.media || {};
    const product = products.find(item => item && item.sku === result.sku) || null;
    const missing = (result.missing_fields || []).map(item => formatSchemaFieldReference(product, item.name || '', item.title || item.name || '')).join('，');
    const counts = result.summary_counts || {};

    // 本地校验明细
    const localErrors = (local.errors || []).map(e => `<div class="diagnostic-list-item"><span style="color:var(--danger)">${issueIcon('error')} ${escHtml(e)}</span></div>`).join('');
    const localWarnings = (local.warnings || []).map(w => `<div class="diagnostic-list-item"><span style="color:var(--warning)">${issueIcon('warning')} ${escHtml(w)}</span></div>`).join('');

    // Amazon 预览明细
    const previewIssues = (preview.issues || []).map(issue => {
      const code = issue.code ? `[${escHtml(issue.code)}] ` : '';
      const attrs = (issue.attributeNames || []).length > 0 ? ` (${escHtml(issue.attributeNames.join(', '))})` : '';
      const color = issue.level === 'error' ? 'var(--danger)' : 'var(--warning)';
      const hint = issue.hint ? `<div style="margin-left:20px;font-size:11px;color:var(--text-muted)">${escHtml(issue.hint)}</div>` : '';
      const fix = issue.fix ? `<div style="margin-left:20px;font-size:11px;color:var(--primary)">${escHtml(issue.fix)}</div>` : '';
      return `<div class="diagnostic-list-item"><span style="color:${color}">${issueIcon(issue.level)} ${code}${escHtml(issue.message || '')}${attrs}</span>${hint}${fix}</div>`;
    }).join('');

    // Listing 后台 issues
    const listingIssues = (listing.issues || []).map(issue => {
      const code = issue.code ? `[${escHtml(issue.code)}] ` : '';
      const color = issue.level === 'error' ? 'var(--danger)' : 'var(--warning)';
      return `<div class="diagnostic-list-item"><span style="color:${color}">${issueIcon(issue.level)} ${code}${escHtml(issue.message || '')}</span></div>`;
    }).join('');

    // 媒体连通性
    const mediaChecks = (media.checks || []).map(chk => {
      const ok = chk.status === 'ok' || chk.status === 'pass';
      return `<div class="diagnostic-list-item"><span style="color:${ok ? 'var(--success)' : 'var(--danger)'}">
        ${ok ? '&#9989;' : '&#10060;'} ${escHtml(chk.slot || chk.label || '')} ${escHtml(chk.message || chk.url || '')}
      </span></div>`;
    }).join('');

    const section = (title, content) => content ? `<div style="margin-top:8px"><div style="font-weight:600;font-size:12px;margin-bottom:4px">${title}</div>${content}</div>` : '';

    return `
      <div style="padding:12px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--line);">
        <div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; gap:12px; align-items:center;">
          <strong>${escHtml(result.sku || '-')}</strong>
          ${statusBadge(result.status)}
        </div>
        <div style="margin-top:4px; color:var(--text-secondary); font-size:13px;">${escHtml(result.summary_text || '-')}</div>
        <div style="margin-top:4px; font-size:12px; color:var(--text-muted);">
          错误 ${counts.errors || 0} · 警告 ${counts.warnings || 0} · 缺失字段 ${counts.missing_fields || 0} · 媒体失败 ${counts.media_failed || 0}
        </div>
        ${missing ? `<div style="margin-top:6px; font-size:12px; color:var(--text-secondary);">缺失字段：${escHtml(missing)}</div>` : ''}
        ${section('本地校验', localErrors + localWarnings)}
        ${section('Amazon 预览' + (preview.status ? ' (' + escHtml(preview.status) + ')' : ''), preview.message ? `<div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted)">${escHtml(preview.message)}</div>` + previewIssues : previewIssues)}
        ${section('Listing 后台问题', listingIssues)}
        ${section('媒体连通性', mediaChecks)}
        ${buildResultActionButtons(result, 'diagnose')}
      </div>
    `;
  }).join('');
  showModal('缺项诊断结果', `<div style="max-height:65vh; overflow:auto;">${rows || '<p>暂无结果</p>'}</div>`, { wide: true });
}

async function runListingCheck(targetSku = '', overrideSkus = null) {
  if (!await ensureCustomerPrerequisite('file')) return;
  const skus = Array.isArray(overrideSkus) && overrideSkus.length > 0
    ? overrideSkus
    : (targetSku ? [targetSku] : getSelectedActionableSkus());
  if (skus.length === 0) return showToast('warning', '没有可诊断的商品');

  try {
    showToast('info', `正在诊断 ${skus.length} 个商品...`);
    const response = await fetch('/api/listing-check', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ file: currentFile, skus, account_id: selectedAccountId || '' })
    });
    const data = await response.json();
    if (data.error) return showToast('error', data.error);
    if (data.account_message) showToast('warning', data.account_message);

    (data.results || []).forEach(result => {
      const product = products.find(item => item.sku === result.sku);
      if (product) applyListingCheckResult(product, result);
    });

    renderTable();
    updateStats();

    if (drawerProduct) {
      const refreshed = products.find(item => item.sku === drawerProduct.sku);
      if (refreshed) drawerProduct = refreshed;
      renderDrawerContent();
    }

    if (skus.length === 1 && drawerProduct && drawerProduct.sku === skus[0]) {
      switchDrawerTab('diagnostics');
    } else {
      showListingCheckReport(data.results || []);
    }

    const fail = Number(data.fail || 0);
    const warn = Number(data.warn || 0);
    const tone = fail > 0 ? 'warning' : (warn > 0 ? 'warning' : 'success');
    showToast(tone, `诊断完成：${data.pass || 0} 通过，${warn} 警告，${fail} 失败`);
  } catch (e) {
    showToast('error', '缺项诊断失败: ' + e.message);
  }
}

async function batchListingCheck() {
  if (!await ensureCustomerPrerequisite('file')) return;
  const plan = collectActionPlan('validate', 'all');
  if (plan.actionableSkus.length === 0) return showToast('warning', '没有可诊断的商品');
  runListingCheck('', plan.actionableSkus);
}

async function regenerateField(sku, field) {
  if (!await ensureCustomerPrerequisite('file')) return;
  if (!await ensureCustomerPrerequisite('ai')) return;
  showToast('info', '正在生成 ' + field + '...');
  const textFieldMap = {
    title: ['title'],
    bullet_1: ['bullets'],
    bullet_2: ['bullets'],
    bullet_3: ['bullets'],
    bullet_4: ['bullets'],
    bullet_5: ['bullets'],
    bullets: ['bullets'],
    description: ['description'],
    keywords: ['keywords'],
  };
  fetch('/api/process-single', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({ sku, field, text_fields: textFieldMap[field] || ['title','bullets','description','keywords'], file: currentFile, action: 'rewrite' })
  }).then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
    if (d.error) return showToast('error', d.error);
    const p = products.find(x => x.sku === sku);
    if (p && d.result) Object.assign(p, d.result);
    if (drawerProduct && drawerProduct.sku === sku) renderDrawerContent();
    showToast('success', field + ' 生成完成');
  }).catch(e => showToast('error', e.message));
}

function adoptField(sku, field) {
  const p = products.find(x => x.sku === sku);
  if (!p) return;
  const aiKeyMap = { title:'ai_title', bullet_1:'ai_bullet_1', bullet_2:'ai_bullet_2',
    bullet_3:'ai_bullet_3', bullet_4:'ai_bullet_4', bullet_5:'ai_bullet_5',
    description:'ai_description', keywords:'ai_keywords' };
  const origKeyMap = { title:'item_name', bullet_1:'bullet_point_1', bullet_2:'bullet_point_2',
    bullet_3:'bullet_point_3', bullet_4:'bullet_point_4', bullet_5:'bullet_point_5',
    description:'product_description', keywords:'generic_keywords' };
  const aiVal = p[aiKeyMap[field]];
  if (!aiVal) return;
  const targetField = origKeyMap[field] || field;

  fetch('/api/update-field', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({ file: currentFile, sku, field: targetField, value: aiVal })
  }).then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
    if (d.error) return showToast('error', d.error);
    p[targetField] = aiVal;
    if (field === 'title') {
      p.title = aiVal;
      p.item_name = aiVal;
    }
    if (drawerProduct && drawerProduct.sku === sku) renderDrawerContent();
    showToast('success', '已采用AI结果');
    applyFilter();
  }).catch(e => showToast('error', e.message));
}

async function regenerateImage(sku, scope) {
  if (!await ensureCustomerPrerequisite('file')) return;
  if (!await ensureCustomerPrerequisite('ai')) return;
  showToast('info', '正在生成图片...');
  const bgStyle = (drawerProduct && drawerProduct.sku === sku && drawerProduct._bgStyle) || 'white';
  fetch('/api/process-single', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({ sku, action: 'image', scope, bg_style: bgStyle, file: currentFile })
  }).then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
    if (d.error) return showToast('error', d.error);
    const p = products.find(x => x.sku === sku);
    if (p && d.result) Object.assign(p, d.result);
    if (drawerProduct && drawerProduct.sku === sku) renderDrawerContent();
    showToast('success', '图片生成完成');
  }).catch(e => showToast('error', e.message));
}

async function adoptImage(sku, scope) {
  const p = products.find(x => x.sku === sku);
  if (!p) return;
  const aiLocator = p.ai_media_locator || p.ai_public_image_url || (isMediaLocator(p.ai_image_url) ? p.ai_image_url : '');
  const aiPreview = p.ai_main_image_preview || p.ai_main_image || (isWebImageUrl(p.ai_image_url) ? p.ai_image_url : '');
  const snapshot = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify({
    main_image_url: p.main_image_url || '',
    main_image_preview_url: p.main_image_preview_url || '',
    images: Object.fromEntries(Array.from({ length: 8 }, (_, idx) => {
      const i = idx + 2;
      return [i, {
        image: p['image_' + i] || '',
        other: p['other_image_url_' + (i - 1)] || '',
        preview: p['image_' + i + '_preview_url'] || '',
      }];
    })),
  }));

  if (scope === 'main') {
    if (!aiLocator) return showToast('warning', '当前图片尚未完成媒体上传，暂不能提交到亚马逊');
    p.main_image_url = aiLocator;
    p.main_image_preview_url = aiPreview;
    // Persist to Excel
    if (currentFile) {
      try {
        const response = await fetch('/api/update-field', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ file: currentFile, sku, field: 'main_image_url', value: aiLocator })
        });
        const data = await response.json();
        if (!response.ok || data.error) {
          throw new Error(data.error || ('HTTP ' + response.status));
        }
      } catch (err) {
        p.main_image_url = snapshot.main_image_url;
        p.main_image_preview_url = snapshot.main_image_preview_url;
        if (drawerProduct && drawerProduct.sku === sku) renderDrawerContent();
        applyFilter();
        return showToast('error', '保存失败: ' + err.message);
      }
    }
  } else if (scope === 'all') {
    const updates = {};
    // Adopt main image
    if (aiLocator) {
      p.main_image_url = aiLocator;
      p.main_image_preview_url = aiPreview;
      updates.main_image_url = aiLocator;
    }
    // Adopt sub images
    for (let i = 2; i <= 9; i++) {
      const aiSub = p['ai_media_locator_' + i] || p['ai_public_image_' + i] || '';
      const aiSubPreview = p['ai_image_' + i + '_preview'] || p['ai_image_' + i] || '';
      if (aiSub) {
        p['image_' + i] = aiSub;
        p['other_image_url_' + (i - 1)] = aiSub;
        p['image_' + i + '_preview_url'] = aiSubPreview;
        updates['image_' + i] = aiSub;
      }
    }
    if (currentFile && Object.keys(updates).length > 0) {
      try {
        const response = await fetch('/api/update-product', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ file: currentFile, file_version: currentFileVersion, sku, updates })
        });
        const data = await response.json();
        if (!response.ok || data.error) {
          throw new Error(data.error || ('HTTP ' + response.status));
        }
        if (data.file_version) currentFileVersion = Number(data.file_version || currentFileVersion);
      } catch (err) {
        p.main_image_url = snapshot.main_image_url;
        p.main_image_preview_url = snapshot.main_image_preview_url;
        for (let i = 2; i <= 9; i++) {
          p['image_' + i] = snapshot.images[i].image;
          p['other_image_url_' + (i - 1)] = snapshot.images[i].other;
          p['image_' + i + '_preview_url'] = snapshot.images[i].preview;
        }
        if (drawerProduct && drawerProduct.sku === sku) renderDrawerContent();
        applyFilter();
        return showToast('error', '保存失败: ' + err.message);
      }
    } else if (!aiLocator && Object.keys(updates).length === 0) {
      return showToast('warning', '当前图片尚未完成媒体上传，暂不能提交到亚马逊');
    }
  }

  if (drawerProduct && drawerProduct.sku === sku) renderDrawerContent();
  applyFilter();
  showToast('success', '已采用AI图片');
}

function selectBg(el, bg) {
  el.parentElement.querySelectorAll('.bg-opt').forEach(o => o.classList.remove('active'));
  el.classList.add('active');
  // Store background preference for current drawer product
  if (drawerProduct) {
    drawerProduct._bgStyle = bg;
  }
}

// ===== 19. AI Processing =====
async function processSingle(sku) {
  if (!await ensureCustomerPrerequisite('file')) return;
  if (!await ensureCustomerPrerequisite('ai')) return;
  showToast('info', '正在AI处理: ' + sku);
  fetch('/api/process-single', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({ sku, file: currentFile, action: 'rewrite' })
  }).then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
    if (d.error) return showToast('error', d.error);
    const p = products.find(x => x.sku === sku);
    if (p && d.result) { Object.assign(p, d.result); p.ai_status = 'completed'; }
    if (drawerProduct && drawerProduct.sku === sku) renderDrawerContent();
    updateStats(); applyFilter();
    showToast('success', 'AI处理完成: ' + sku);
  }).catch(e => showToast('error', e.message));
}

async function batchProcess(action, scope) {
  if (!await ensureCustomerPrerequisite('file')) return;
  if ((action === 'rewrite' || action === 'image') && !await ensureCustomerPrerequisite('ai')) return;
  const plan = collectActionPlan(action, scope);
  if (plan.actionableSkus.length === 0) {
    return showToast('warning', plan.skipped.length > 0 ? '没有可执行商品，请先修复摘要中的问题' : '没有可处理的商品');
  }
  closeAllDropdowns();
  showActionPreflight(plan, () => {
    processing = true;
    cancelRequested = false;
    showProgress(action === 'image' ? '批量生图' : '批量AI文案', 0, plan.actionableSkus.length);

    const options = { selected_skus: plan.actionableSkus };
    if (action === 'rewrite') {
      options.process_text = true;
      options.process_images = false;
      options.text_fields = scope === 'title' ? ['title']
        : scope === 'bullets' ? ['bullets']
        : ['title', 'bullets', 'description', 'keywords'];
    } else {
      options.process_text = false;
      options.process_images = true;
      options.image_scope = scope === 'all' ? 'all' : 'main';
      options.image_style = (drawerProduct && drawerProduct._bgStyle) || 'white';
    }

    fetch('/api/process', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ stage: 1, file: currentFile, action, scope, options })
    }).then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
      if (d.error) { processing = false; hideProgress(); return showToast('error', d.error); }
      pollRetries = 0;
      loadTaskCenter();
      pollStatus();
    }).catch(e => { processing = false; hideProgress(); showToast('error', e.message); });
  });
}

let pollRetries = 0;
const MAX_POLL_RETRIES = 40; // ~60 seconds

function pollStatus() {
  if (!processing) return;
  if (pollRetries >= MAX_POLL_RETRIES) {
    processing = false;
    cancelRequested = false;
    hideProgress();
    showToast('error', '轮询超时，请检查任务状态');
    return;
  }
  pollRetries++;
  fetch('/api/status').then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
    loadTaskCenter();
    const done = d.completed ?? d.progress ?? 0;
    const total = d.total || 1;
    const current = d.current_sku || d.current_item || '';
    updateProgress(done, total, current);

    if (d.status === 'cancelling') {
      document.getElementById('progressTitle').textContent = '正在取消...';
      document.getElementById('progressItem').textContent = '等待当前任务安全停止';
      setTimeout(pollStatus, 1000);
      return;
    }

    if (d.status === 'cancelled') {
      processing = false;
      cancelRequested = false;
      hideProgress();
      loadProducts();
      showToast('info', '任务已取消，已保留当前结果');
    } else if (d.status === 'completed' || (!d.running && done >= total)) {
      processing = false;
      cancelRequested = false;
      hideProgress();
      loadProducts();
      showToast('success', `处理完成: ${done}/${total}`);
    } else {
      setTimeout(pollStatus, 1500);
    }
  }).catch(() => {
    if (pollRetries >= MAX_POLL_RETRIES) { processing = false; cancelRequested = false; hideProgress(); showToast('error', '轮询超时'); return; }
    setTimeout(pollStatus, 3000);
  });
}

function cancelProcess() {
  if (!processing || cancelRequested) return;
  cancelRequested = true;
  fetch('/api/process/cancel', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }
  }).then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
    if (d.error) {
      cancelRequested = false;
      return showToast('error', d.error);
    }
    document.getElementById('progressTitle').textContent = '正在取消...';
    document.getElementById('progressItem').textContent = '等待当前任务安全停止';
    showToast('info', d.message || '正在取消');
  }).catch(e => {
    cancelRequested = false;
    showToast('error', '取消失败: ' + e.message);
  });
}

// ===== 20. Validation =====
function validateRow(p) {
  const errors = [];
  if (!p.sku) errors.push('缺少SKU');
  if (p.parentage_level === 'parent') { p._validPass = true; p._validErrors = []; return; }
  const title = p.title || p.item_name || '';
  if (!title) errors.push('缺少标题');
  if (title && title.length > 200) errors.push('标题超200字符');
  const price = p.price || p.standard_price;
  if (!price) errors.push('缺少价格');
  p._validErrors = errors;
  p._validPass = errors.length === 0;
}

async function batchValidate() {
  if (!await ensureCustomerPrerequisite('file')) return;

  const plan = collectActionPlan('validate', 'all');
  if (plan.actionableSkus.length === 0) return showToast('warning', '没有可校验的商品');

  showActionPreflight(plan, async () => {
    showToast('info', `正在校验 ${plan.actionableSkus.length} 个商品...`);

    try {
      const response = await fetch('/api/validate', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ input_file: currentFile, skus: plan.actionableSkus })
      });
      const data = await response.json();
      if (data.error) return showToast('error', data.error);

      const resultMap = new Map((data.results || []).map(result => [result.sku, result]));
      products.forEach(product => {
        const result = resultMap.get(product.sku);
        if (result) applyValidationResult(product, result);
      });

      updateStats();
      applyFilter();
      loadTaskCenter();

      const errorCount = (data.results || []).filter(result =>
        (result.issues || []).some(issue => issue.level === 'error')
      ).length;
      const warningCount = (data.results || []).filter(result =>
        !(result.issues || []).some(issue => issue.level === 'error') &&
        (result.issues || []).some(issue => issue.level === 'warning')
      ).length;

      let message = `校验完成: ${(data.results || []).length - errorCount} 通过, ${errorCount} 有错误`;
      if (warningCount > 0) message += `, ${warningCount} 有警告`;
      showToast(errorCount > 0 ? 'warning' : 'success', message);
    } catch (e) {
      showToast('error', '校验失败: ' + e.message);
    }
  });
}

// ===== 21. Export =====
function exportData() {
  if (!currentFile) return;
  const plan = collectActionPlan('export', 'sp-api');
  if (selectedSkus.size > 0 && plan.actionableSkus.length === 0) {
    return showToast('warning', '当前所选内容里没有可导出的真实 SKU，请取消父体选择后重试');
  }
  if (plan.actionableSkus.length === 0) return showToast('warning', '没有可导出的商品');
  showActionPreflight(plan, () => {
    fetch('/api/export', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        file: currentFile,
        format: 'sp-api',
        selected_skus: selectedSkus.size > 0 ? plan.actionableSkus : []
      })
    }).then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
      if (d.error) return showToast('error', d.error);
      loadTaskCenter();
      if (d.filename) window.location.href = '/api/download/' + encodeURIComponent(d.filename);
    }).catch(e => showToast('error', e.message));
  });
}

function downloadTemplate() {
  window.location.href = '/api/download-template';
}

function createSampleExcel() {
  showToast('info', '正在生成示例 Excel...');
  fetch('/api/sample-excel', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({})
  }).then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
    if (d.error) return showToast('error', d.error);
    currentFile = d.filepath || '';
    if (currentFile) localStorage.setItem('amazon28_currentFile', currentFile);
    currentFileMeta = { type: 'xlsx', warning: '', xlsPreserveSupported: true };
    document.getElementById('fileInfo').dataset.baseName = d.filename || '';
    document.getElementById('fileInfo').textContent = d.filename || '示例 Excel';
    templatePanelCollapsed = true;
    loadProducts();
    refreshSetupStatus({ showFirstRun: false });
    showToast('success', '示例 Excel 已载入，可先测试工具流程');
  }).catch(e => showToast('error', '生成示例失败: ' + e.message));
}

// ===== 21b. AI 全部对比视图 =====
async function showComparisonView() {
  if (!await ensureCustomerPrerequisite('file')) return;
  showToast('info', '正在加载对比数据...');
  try {
    const response = await fetch('/api/comparison?file=' + encodeURIComponent(currentFile));
    const data = await response.json();
    if (data.error) return showToast('error', data.error);
    const items = data.comparisons || [];
    if (items.length === 0) return showToast('warning', '暂无对比数据，请先运行 AI 文案生成');

    const rows = items.map(item => {
      const orig = item.original || {};
      const ai = item.ai_generated || {};
      const bullets = (ai.bullets || []).filter(b => b).map(b => `<li>${escHtml(b)}</li>`).join('');
      const origImg = orig.image ? `<img src="${escHtml(orig.image)}" style="max-height:80px">` : '-';
      const aiImg = ai.image ? `<img src="${escHtml(ai.image)}" style="max-height:80px">` : '-';
      return `<tr>
        <td><strong>${escHtml(item.sku)}</strong></td>
        <td style="max-width:250px">${escHtml(orig.title || '-')}</td>
        <td style="max-width:250px">${escHtml(ai.title || '-')}</td>
        <td>${origImg}</td>
        <td>${aiImg}</td>
        <td>${bullets || '-'}</td>
        <td>${escHtml(ai.keywords || '-')}</td>
      </tr>`;
    }).join('');

    const html = `<div style="max-height:70vh;overflow:auto">
      <table class="data-table data-table-compact">
        <thead><tr>
          <th>SKU</th><th>原始标题</th><th>AI 标题</th>
          <th>原始图</th><th>AI 图</th><th>AI 卖点</th><th>AI 搜索词</th>
        </tr></thead>
        <tbody>${rows}</tbody>
      </table>
    </div>`;
    showModal('AI 前后对比 (' + items.length + ' 条)', html, { wide: true });
  } catch (e) {
    showToast('error', '加载对比数据失败: ' + e.message);
  }
}

// ===== 21c. 单张图片快速换背景 =====
async function quickImageProcess(imageUrl, bgStyle) {
  if (!imageUrl) return showToast('warning', '没有可用的图片 URL');
  if (!await ensureCustomerPrerequisite('ai')) return;
  showToast('info', '正在处理图片...');
  try {
    const response = await fetch('/api/image-process', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ image_url: imageUrl, bg_style: bgStyle || 'white' })
    });
    const data = await response.json();
    if (data.error) return showToast('error', data.error);
    if (data.success && data.result_b64) {
      const imgSrc = 'data:image/png;base64,' + data.result_b64;
      showModal('AI 换背景结果', `<div style="text-align:center">
        <img src="${imgSrc}" style="max-width:100%;max-height:60vh;border-radius:8px">
        <div style="margin-top:12px;color:var(--text-secondary)">预览结果。如需保存到 SKU，请使用抽屉内的"生成"按钮。</div>
      </div>`);
    } else {
      showToast('error', '图片处理未返回结果');
    }
  } catch (e) {
    showToast('error', '图片处理失败: ' + e.message);
  }
}

// ===== 22. Submit =====
async function requestAmazonSubmission(mode, skus, options = {}) {
  const targetSkus = Array.from(new Set((skus || []).map(item => String(item || '').trim()).filter(Boolean)));
  if (!await ensureCustomerPrerequisite('file')) return;
  if (!await ensureCustomerPrerequisite('amazon')) return;
  if (mode === 'submit' && !await ensureCustomerPrerequisite('preview_before_submit', { skus: targetSkus })) return;
  if (targetSkus.length === 0) return showToast('warning', '没有可提交的商品');
  const targetProducts = products.filter(product => targetSkus.includes(product.sku));
  const familyMessage = getIncompleteFamilyMessageForSkus(targetSkus);
  if (familyMessage) {
    return showCustomerBlock('变体家族不完整', familyMessage + '。系统已经拦住，避免只提交一半 family。', 'check', '去诊断');
  }
  const duplicateAsins = getDuplicateAsinMap();
  const duplicateProduct = targetProducts.find(product => duplicateAsins.has(product.sku));
  if (duplicateProduct) {
    const info = duplicateAsins.get(duplicateProduct.sku);
    return showCustomerBlock('ASIN 重复', `ASIN ${info.asin} 被多个 SKU 共用：${info.skus.join('、')}。先改 Excel，不能直接提交。`, 'check', '去校验');
  }
  if (mode === 'submit') {
    const submittedProduct = targetProducts.find(product => isAlreadySubmittedProduct(product));
    if (submittedProduct) {
      return showCustomerBlock('已经上架过', `${submittedProduct.sku || '-'} 已经提交成功${submittedProduct.asin ? `，ASIN ${submittedProduct.asin}` : ''}。系统禁止再次提交，避免重复创建。`, 'check', '看提交结果');
    }
  }
  closeAllDropdowns();

  let accounts = [];
  try {
    accounts = await fetchAccounts(true);
  } catch (e) {
    return showToast('error', '加载账号失败: ' + e.message);
  }

  const readyAccounts = accounts.filter(account => account.has_credentials !== false);
  if (readyAccounts.length === 0) {
    return showToast('error', '没有可用的亚马逊账号，请先在设置页添加账号并补全凭证');
  }

  const executeWithAccount = accountId => {
    const accountMeta = getAccountMeta(accountId);
    if (options.skipPreflight || !options.plan) {
      return confirmFormalSubmitIfNeeded(mode, accountId, targetSkus, () => executeSubmit(mode, accountId, targetSkus));
    }
    return showActionPreflight(
      options.plan,
      () => confirmFormalSubmitIfNeeded(mode, accountId, targetSkus, () => executeSubmit(mode, accountId, targetSkus)),
      { account: accountMeta, mode }
    );
  };

  if (readyAccounts.length === 1) {
    setSelectedAmazonAccount(readyAccounts[0].seller_id, { toast: mode === 'submit', refreshUi: true });
    return executeWithAccount(selectedAccountId);
  }

  const preferredId = readyAccounts.some(account => account.seller_id === selectedAccountId)
    ? selectedAccountId
    : ((readyAccounts.find(account => account.is_default) || readyAccounts[0] || {}).seller_id || '');
  setSelectedAmazonAccount(preferredId, { toast: mode === 'submit', refreshUi: true });
  pendingSubmitPayload = {
    mode,
    skus: targetSkus,
    plan: options.plan || null,
    skipPreflight: !!options.skipPreflight,
  };

  document.getElementById('modalTitle').textContent = options.customTitle || (mode === 'preview' ? '选择预览验证账号' : '选择提交账号');
  document.getElementById('modalBody').innerHTML = `
    <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:10px;">
      <div style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text-secondary);">${escHtml(options.description || `${options.skipPreflight ? '将直接处理' : '预检后将处理'} ${targetSkus.length} 个商品，请选择要使用的亚马逊账号。`)}</div>
      ${readyAccounts.map(account => {
        const checked = account.seller_id === preferredId ? 'checked' : '';
        const site = account.marketplace_name || account.marketplace_id || '-';
        const defaultBadge = account.is_default ? '<span class="badge badge-success">默认</span>' : '';
        return `<label style="display:flex;align-items:flex-start;gap:10px;padding:10px 12px;border:1px solid var(--border-light);border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;">
          <input type="radio" name="submitAccountRadio" value="${escHtml(account.seller_id)}" ${checked} style="margin-top:2px;">
          <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:4px;">
            <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;flex-wrap:wrap;">
              <strong>${escHtml(account.name || account.seller_id)}</strong>
              ${defaultBadge}
            </div>
            <div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);">Seller ID: ${escHtml(account.seller_id)}</div>
            <div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);">站点: ${escHtml(site)}</div>
          </div>
        </label>`;
      }).join('')}
    </div>`;
  document.getElementById('modalFooter').innerHTML = `
    <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="closeModal()">取消</button>
    <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="confirmSubmitAccount()">继续</button>`;
  document.getElementById('modal').classList.add('show');
}

function confirmFormalSubmitIfNeeded(mode, accountId, skus, onConfirm) {
  if (mode !== 'submit') return onConfirm();
  const accountMeta = getAccountMeta(accountId) || { name: accountId || '-', site: '-' };
  const targetSet = new Set((skus || []).map(item => String(item || '').trim()).filter(Boolean));
  const targetProducts = products.filter(product => targetSet.has(product.sku));
  const previewPassed = targetProducts.filter(product => isPreviewValidForSelectedAccount(product)).length;
  const blockedRows = targetProducts.filter(product => !isPreviewValidForSelectedAccount(product)).slice(0, 8);
  showModal('正式提交前最后确认', `
    <div class="preflight-panel danger">
      <div class="preflight-stat-grid">
        <div class="preflight-stat"><span>目标账号</span><strong>${escHtml(accountMeta.name || accountId || '-')}</strong></div>
        <div class="preflight-stat"><span>目标站点</span><strong>${escHtml(accountMeta.site || '-')}</strong></div>
        <div class="preflight-stat"><span>SKU 数量</span><strong>${targetSet.size}</strong></div>
        <div class="preflight-stat"><span>预览通过</span><strong>${previewPassed}</strong></div>
      </div>
      <div class="preflight-note danger">这是正式提交，会把数据发送给 Amazon。提交前请确认账号、站点和 SKU 数量正确；系统会在后端再次阻止未通过同账号/站点预览的 SKU。</div>
      ${blockedRows.length ? `<div class="preflight-block"><div class="preflight-title">仍可能被阻止的 SKU</div><div class="preflight-tags">${blockedRows.map(item => `<span class="preflight-tag warn">${escHtml(item.sku)} 未预览通过</span>`).join('')}</div></div>` : ''}
    </div>
  `);
  document.getElementById('modalFooter').innerHTML = `
    <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="closeModal()">取消</button>
    <button class="btn btn-success btn-sm" id="formalSubmitConfirmBtn">我确认，正式提交 ${targetSet.size} 个 SKU</button>`;
  document.getElementById('formalSubmitConfirmBtn').onclick = () => {
    closeModal();
    onConfirm();
  };
}

async function submitToAmazon(mode) {
  if (!await ensureCustomerPrerequisite('file')) return;
  if (!await ensureCustomerPrerequisite('amazon')) return;
  const plan = collectActionPlan(mode === 'preview' ? 'preview' : 'submit', 'all');
  if (plan.actionableSkus.length === 0) {
    if (plan.skipped.length > 0) return showToast('warning', `当前没有可提交 SKU：${plan.skipped[0].reason}`);
    return showToast('warning', '没有可提交的商品');
  }
  return requestAmazonSubmission(mode, plan.actionableSkus, { plan });
}

function confirmSubmitAccount() {
  if (!pendingSubmitPayload) return;
  const checked = document.querySelector('input[name="submitAccountRadio"]:checked');
  if (!checked) return showToast('warning', '请选择一个账号');
  setSelectedAmazonAccount(checked.value, { toast: payload.mode === 'submit', refreshUi: true });
  const payload = pendingSubmitPayload;
  pendingSubmitPayload = null;
  closeModal();
  if (payload.skipPreflight || !payload.plan) {
    confirmFormalSubmitIfNeeded(payload.mode, selectedAccountId, payload.skus, () => executeSubmit(payload.mode, selectedAccountId, payload.skus));
  } else {
    showActionPreflight(
      payload.plan,
      () => confirmFormalSubmitIfNeeded(payload.mode, selectedAccountId, payload.skus, () => executeSubmit(payload.mode, selectedAccountId, payload.skus)),
      { account: getAccountMeta(selectedAccountId), mode: payload.mode }
    );
  }
}

async function executeSubmit(mode, accountId, skus) {
  const isPreview = mode === 'preview';
  showToast('info', `正在${isPreview ? '预览验证' : '提交上架'} ${skus.length} 个商品...`);
