  showProgress(isPreview ? 'Amazon 预览验证' : '正式提交到亚马逊', 0, skus.length, { cancelable: false });

  try {
    const response = await fetch('/api/submit-task', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ skus, file: currentFile, preview: isPreview, account_id: accountId })
    });
    const data = await response.json();
    if (data.error) {
      hideProgress();
      return showToast('error', data.error);
    }
    pollSubmitTask(data.task_id, isPreview);
  } catch (e) {
    hideProgress();
    showToast('error', '请求失败: ' + e.message);
  }
}

async function pollSubmitTask(taskId, isPreview) {
  if (!taskId) { hideProgress(); return; }
  try {
    const response = await fetch('/api/tasks/' + encodeURIComponent(taskId));
    const task = await response.json();
    if (task.error) throw new Error(task.error);
    const result = task.result || {};
    const total = Number(task.total || result.total || 0) || 1;
    const done = Math.min(Number(task.progress || 0), total);
    const stage = task.stage_name ? `${task.stage_name}` : (isPreview ? 'Amazon 预览' : '正式提交');
    document.getElementById('progressTitle').textContent = isPreview ? 'Amazon 预览验证' : '正式提交到亚马逊';
    updateProgress(done, total, [stage, task.current_item || ''].filter(Boolean).join(' · '));
    loadTaskCenter();

    if (task.status === 'completed') {
      hideProgress();
      if (!isPreview && result.results && result.results.length > 0) {
        await enrichSubmitResults(result);
      }
      if (isPreview && result.results && result.results.length > 0) {
        const previewMap = new Map((result.results || []).map(item => [item.sku, item]));
        products.forEach(product => {
          const previewResult = previewMap.get(product.sku);
          if (previewResult) applyPreviewResult(product, previewResult);
        });
        if (drawerProduct) {
          const refreshed = products.find(item => item.sku === drawerProduct.sku);
          if (refreshed) {
            drawerProduct = refreshed;
            renderDrawerContent();
          }
        }
      }
      if (!isPreview && result.results && result.results.length > 0) {
        recentSubmitHighlights = new Set(result.results.map(item => item.sku).filter(Boolean));
        recentSubmitScrollPending = true;
        if (task.id && !recentSubmitToastTaskIds.has(task.id)) {
          recentSubmitToastTaskIds.add(task.id);
          result.results.forEach(item => {
            if (String(item.status || '').trim().toUpperCase() === 'ACCEPTED') {
              const toastPayload = { ...item, account: result.account || '', marketplace_name: result.marketplace || '' };
              showSubmitSuccessToast(toastPayload);
              showToast('success', `Amazon 已接受 ${toastPayload.sku || '-'} · 提交ID ${compactMiddle(toastPayload.submission_id || toastPayload.submissionId || '', 10, 8) || '未返回'} · ${formatSubmissionRoute(toastPayload.submission_route || 'unknown')}`);
            }
          });
        }
      } else if (!isPreview) {
        recentSubmitHighlights = new Set();
      }
      if (currentFile) loadProducts();
      setTimeout(() => loadTaskCenter(), 200);
      if (result.persist_warning) showToast('warning', result.persist_warning);
      if (result.results && result.results.length > 0) showSubmitResults(result, isPreview);
      else showToast('success', result.message || task.message || '完成');
      return;
    }
    if (task.status === 'failed') {
      hideProgress();
      showToast('error', task.error || task.message || '任务失败');
      return;
    }
    setTimeout(() => pollSubmitTask(taskId, isPreview), 1000);
  } catch (e) {
    hideProgress();
    showToast('error', '任务查询失败: ' + e.message);
  }
}

async function enrichSubmitResults(result) {
  const rows = result.results || [];
  const skus = rows
    .filter(row => row.status === 'ACCEPTED' || row.status === 'UNKNOWN' || !row.asin)
    .map(row => row.sku)
    .filter(Boolean);
  if (skus.length === 0) return result;

  await refreshListingStatuses(skus, { rounds: 6, intervalMs: 3000 });
  rows.forEach(row => {
    const live = listingStatusMap.get(row.sku);
    if (!live) return;
    row.asin = live.asin || row.asin || '';
    row.final_status = live.final_status || '';
    row.discoverable = !!live.discoverable;
    row.issue_count = Number(live.issue_count || 0);
    row.offers = live.offers || [];
    row.fulfillmentAvailability = live.fulfillmentAvailability || [];
    row.issues = (live.issues && live.issues.length > 0) ? live.issues : (row.issues || []);
    row.submission_route = live.route || row.submission_route || 'unknown';
  });
  return result;
}

function showSubmitResults(data, isPreview) {
  const results = data.results || [];
  let html = `<div style="max-height:60vh;overflow-y:auto;">`;
  html += `<p style="margin-bottom:12px;font-weight:600;">${data.message}</p>`;
  html += `<table style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;font-size:13px;">`;
  html += `<tr style="background:#f5f5f5;"><th style="padding:6px 8px;text-align:left;">SKU</th>`;

  if (isPreview) {
    html += `<th style="padding:6px 8px;">状态</th><th style="padding:6px 8px;text-align:left;">详情</th></tr>`;
    for (const r of results) {
      const icon = r.valid ? '✅' : '❌';
      const product = products.find(item => item && item.sku === r.sku) || null;
      const issueHtml = (r.issues || []).map(issue => renderResultIssueHtml(product, issue, issue.message || '')).join('')
        || (r.errors || []).concat(r.warnings || []).map(message => `<div class="result-issue-item"><div class="result-issue-primary">${escHtml(message)}</div></div>`).join('')
        || '<div class="result-issue-item"><div class="result-issue-primary">-</div></div>';
      html += `<tr style="border-bottom:1px solid #eee;">`;
      html += `<td style="padding:6px 8px;font-family:monospace;">${r.sku}</td>`;
      html += `<td style="padding:6px 8px;text-align:center;">${icon}</td>`;
      html += `<td style="padding:6px 8px;color:${r.valid ? '#666' : '#c00'};">${issueHtml}${buildResultActionButtons(r, 'preview')}</td></tr>`;
    }
  } else {
    html += `<th style="padding:6px 8px;">提交</th><th style="padding:6px 8px;">路线</th><th style="padding:6px 8px;">最终状态</th><th style="padding:6px 8px;">ASIN</th><th style="padding:6px 8px;text-align:left;">信息</th></tr>`;
    for (const r of results) {
      const statusMap = {
        'ACCEPTED': ['✅', '#28a745'], 'VALID': ['✅', '#28a745'],
        'INVALID': ['❌', '#dc3545'], 'ERROR': ['❌', '#dc3545'],
        'SKIPPED': ['⏭️', '#ffc107'], 'UNKNOWN': ['❓', '#999'],
      };
      const [icon, color] = statusMap[r.status] || ['❓', '#999'];
      const asin = r.asin || '-';
      const route = formatSubmissionRoute(r.submission_route || 'unknown');
      const finalStatus = formatFinalListingStatus(r.final_status || '');
      const product = products.find(item => item && item.sku === r.sku) || null;
      let msgHtml = (r.issues || []).map(i => renderResultIssueHtml(product, i, i.message || i)).join('');
      if (!msgHtml && r.message) {
        msgHtml = `<div class="result-issue-item"><div class="result-issue-primary">${escHtml(r.message)}</div></div>`;
      }
      if (!msgHtml && r.status === 'ACCEPTED') {
        msgHtml = `<div class="result-issue-item"><div class="result-issue-primary">亚马逊已接受请求，系统会继续追踪最终上架状态。</div></div>`;
      }
      if (!msgHtml) {
        msgHtml = '<div class="result-issue-item"><div class="result-issue-primary">-</div></div>';
      }
      if (r.discoverable) {
        msgHtml = `<div class="result-issue-item"><div class="result-issue-primary">已进入 DISCOVERABLE；库存 ${r.fulfillmentAvailability?.length || 0} 组；报价 ${r.offers?.length || 0} 组。</div></div>` + msgHtml;
      }
      html += `<tr style="border-bottom:1px solid #eee;">`;
      html += `<td style="padding:6px 8px;font-family:monospace;">${r.sku}</td>`;
      html += `<td style="padding:6px 8px;text-align:center;color:${color};">${icon} ${r.status}</td>`;
      html += `<td style="padding:6px 8px;">${route}</td>`;
      html += `<td style="padding:6px 8px;">${finalStatus}</td>`;
      html += `<td style="padding:6px 8px;font-family:monospace;">${asin}</td>`;
      html += `<td style="padding:6px 8px;font-size:12px;color:#666;">${msgHtml}${buildResultActionButtons(r, isPreview ? 'preview' : 'submit')}</td></tr>`;
    }
  }

  html += `</table></div>`;

  // 使用现有的modal或创建简单弹窗
  const overlay = document.createElement('div');
  overlay.className = 'result-center-overlay';
  overlay.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;top:0;left:0;right:0;bottom:0;background:rgba(0,0,0,0.5);z-index:9999;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;';
  overlay.onclick = (e) => { if (e.target === overlay) overlay.remove(); };

  const modal = document.createElement('div');
  modal.style.cssText = 'background:white;border-radius:12px;padding:24px;max-width:700px;width:90%;box-shadow:0 8px 32px rgba(0,0,0,0.3);';
  modal.innerHTML = `
    <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;margin-bottom:16px;">
      <h3 style="margin:0;">${isPreview ? '预览验证结果' : '提交结果'}</h3>
      <button onclick="this.closest('div[style*=fixed]').remove()" style="background:none;border:none;font-size:20px;cursor:pointer;">✕</button>
    </div>
    ${html}
  `;
  overlay.appendChild(modal);
  document.body.appendChild(overlay);
}

// ===== 23. Settings =====
function setAiConfigMode(mode) {
  aiConfigMode = mode === 'advanced' ? 'advanced' : 'simple';
  localStorage.setItem('amazon28_aiConfigMode', aiConfigMode);
  document.querySelectorAll('[data-ai-mode]').forEach(btn => {
    btn.classList.toggle('active', btn.dataset.aiMode === aiConfigMode);
  });
  document.querySelectorAll('.advanced-ai-field').forEach(el => {
    el.style.display = aiConfigMode === 'advanced' ? '' : 'none';
  });
  if (aiConfigMode === 'simple') fillRecommendedAiConfig({ silent: true });
  validateAiConfigFields();
}

function setFieldValidity(id, ok, message = '') {
  const el = document.getElementById(id);
  if (!el) return;
  el.classList.toggle('field-invalid', ok === false);
  el.classList.toggle('field-valid', ok === true);
  el.title = message || '';
}

function validateAiConfigFields() {
  const baseOk = value => String(value || '').trim().replace(/\/$/, '') === RECOMMENDED_AI_CONFIG.baseUrl;
  const endpointOk = value => /\{model\}/.test(String(value || '')) && /generateContent/i.test(String(value || ''));
  const provider = model => /gemini/i.test(String(model || '')) ? 'gemini' : (/^(gpt|o\d|dall-e|gpt-image)/i.test(String(model || '').trim()) ? 'openai' : '');
  const keyOk = id => {
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    return !!el?.value || String(el?.placeholder || '').startsWith('***');
  };
  const textProvider = provider(document.getElementById('cfgTextModel')?.value);
  const imageProvider = provider(document.getElementById('cfgImageModel')?.value);
  const textEndpoint = document.getElementById('cfgTextEndpoint')?.value || '';
  const imageEndpoint = document.getElementById('cfgImageEndpoint')?.value || '';
  setFieldValidity('cfgTextApiKey', keyOk('cfgTextApiKey'), '文字 Key 不能为空');
  setFieldValidity('cfgImageApiKey', keyOk('cfgImageApiKey'), '图片 Key 不能为空');
  setFieldValidity('cfgTextBaseUrl', baseOk(document.getElementById('cfgTextBaseUrl')?.value), 'Base URL 固定填 https://api.kk666.best');
  setFieldValidity('cfgImageBaseUrl', baseOk(document.getElementById('cfgImageBaseUrl')?.value), 'Base URL 固定填 https://api.kk666.best');
  setFieldValidity('cfgTextEndpoint', textProvider === 'openai' ? !/generateContent/i.test(textEndpoint) : endpointOk(textEndpoint), '接口格式必须和文字模型类型一致');
  setFieldValidity('cfgImageEndpoint', imageProvider === 'openai' ? !/generateContent/i.test(imageEndpoint) : endpointOk(imageEndpoint), '接口格式必须和图片模型类型一致');
  setFieldValidity('cfgTextModel', !(textProvider === 'openai' && /generateContent/i.test(textEndpoint)), 'GPT/OpenAI 模型不能配 Gemini 接口');
  setFieldValidity('cfgImageModel', !(imageProvider === 'openai' && /generateContent/i.test(imageEndpoint)), 'GPT/OpenAI 图片模型不能配 Gemini 接口');
}

function syncAiEndpointForModel(kind, options = {}) {
  const modelEl = document.getElementById(kind === 'image' ? 'cfgImageModel' : 'cfgTextModel');
  const endpointEl = document.getElementById(kind === 'image' ? 'cfgImageEndpoint' : 'cfgTextEndpoint');
  if (!modelEl || !endpointEl) return;
  const model = String(modelEl.value || '').trim();
  if (/gemini/i.test(model)) {
    endpointEl.value = RECOMMENDED_AI_CONFIG.endpoint;
  } else if (/^(gpt|o\d)/i.test(model)) {
    endpointEl.value = '/v1/chat/completions';
  } else if (/^(dall-e|gpt-image)/i.test(model)) {
    endpointEl.value = '/v1/images/edits';
  }
  validateAiConfigFields();
  if (!options.silent) showToast('info', '已根据模型类型同步接口格式；保存前可以点“测试连接”确认');
}

function fillRecommendedAiConfig() {
  const options = arguments[0] || {};
  const fields = {
    cfgTextBaseUrl: RECOMMENDED_AI_CONFIG.baseUrl,
    cfgImageBaseUrl: RECOMMENDED_AI_CONFIG.baseUrl,
    cfgTextEndpoint: RECOMMENDED_AI_CONFIG.endpoint,
    cfgImageEndpoint: RECOMMENDED_AI_CONFIG.endpoint,
    cfgTextModel: RECOMMENDED_AI_CONFIG.textModel,
    cfgImageModel: RECOMMENDED_AI_CONFIG.imageModel,
  };
  Object.entries(fields).forEach(([id, value]) => {
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (el) el.value = value;
  });
  validateAiConfigFields();
  if (!options.silent) showToast('success', '已按推荐填写 API 域名、接口格式和模型；请再粘贴 Key 并保存');
}

function resetRecommendedAiConfig() {
  showToast('info', '正在恢复推荐 AI 配置...');
  fetch('/api/config/recommended-ai', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({})
  }).then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
    if (d.error || d.success === false) {
      showToast('error', d.error || '恢复推荐配置失败');
      return;
    }
    fillRecommendedAiConfig({ silent: true });
    showToast('success', d.message || '已恢复推荐配置');
    refreshSetupStatus({ showFirstRun: false });
  }).catch(e => showToast('error', e.message));
}

function loadConfig(applyDefaultLang = false) {
  fetch('/api/config').then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
    if (d.text_api_key) document.getElementById('cfgTextApiKey').value = d.text_api_key;
    if (d.text_api_key_masked) document.getElementById('cfgTextApiKey').placeholder = d.text_api_key_masked;
    if (d.text_api_base) document.getElementById('cfgTextBaseUrl').value = d.text_api_base;
    if (d.text_endpoint_template) document.getElementById('cfgTextEndpoint').value = d.text_endpoint_template;
    if (d.text_model) document.getElementById('cfgTextModel').value = d.text_model;
    if (d.image_api_key) document.getElementById('cfgImageApiKey').value = d.image_api_key;
    if (d.image_api_key_masked) document.getElementById('cfgImageApiKey').placeholder = d.image_api_key_masked;
    if (d.image_api_base) document.getElementById('cfgImageBaseUrl').value = d.image_api_base;
    if (d.image_endpoint_template) document.getElementById('cfgImageEndpoint').value = d.image_endpoint_template;
    if (d.image_model) document.getElementById('cfgImageModel').value = d.image_model;
    document.getElementById('cfgOutputDir').value = d.output_dir || '';
    document.getElementById('cfgLang').value = d.default_lang || 'zh';
    document.getElementById('cfgBatchLimit').value = d.batch_limit || 500;
    document.getElementById('cfgConcurrency').value = d.ai_concurrency || d.concurrency || 3;
    document.getElementById('cfgImgConcurrency').value = d.image_concurrency || 2;
    document.getElementById('cfgMediaStoreEnabled').value = d.media_store_enabled ? 'true' : 'false';
    document.getElementById('cfgMediaStoreProvider').value = d.media_store_provider || 's3';
    document.getElementById('cfgMediaS3Bucket').value = d.media_s3_bucket || '';
    document.getElementById('cfgMediaS3Region').value = d.media_s3_region || 'us-east-1';
    document.getElementById('cfgMediaS3Prefix').value = d.media_s3_prefix || 'amazon28';
    document.getElementById('cfgMediaSubmitScheme').value = d.media_s3_submit_scheme || 's3';
    document.getElementById('cfgMediaPreviewBase').value = d.media_s3_preview_base || '';
    setAiConfigMode(aiConfigMode);
    validateAiConfigFields();
    if (applyDefaultLang && d.default_lang) setLanguage(d.default_lang);
  }).catch(() => {});
}

function saveConfig() {
  if (aiConfigMode === 'simple') fillRecommendedAiConfig({ silent: true });
  fetch('/api/config', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      text_api_key: document.getElementById('cfgTextApiKey').value,
      text_api_base: document.getElementById('cfgTextBaseUrl').value,
      text_endpoint_template: document.getElementById('cfgTextEndpoint').value,
      text_model: document.getElementById('cfgTextModel').value,
      image_api_key: document.getElementById('cfgImageApiKey').value,
      image_api_base: document.getElementById('cfgImageBaseUrl').value,
      image_endpoint_template: document.getElementById('cfgImageEndpoint').value,
      image_model: document.getElementById('cfgImageModel').value,
      mode: aiConfigMode,
    })
  }).then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
    showToast(d.error ? 'error' : 'success', d.error || '配置已保存');
    if (!d.error) refreshSetupStatus({ showFirstRun: false });
  }).catch(e => showToast('error', e.message));
}

function copyText(text, successMessage = '已复制') {
  const value = String(text || '');
  if (navigator.clipboard && navigator.clipboard.writeText) {
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(value)
      .then(() => showToast('success', successMessage))
      .catch(() => fallbackCopyText(value, successMessage));
    return;
  }
  fallbackCopyText(value, successMessage);
}

function fallbackCopyText(text, successMessage) {
  const textarea = document.createElement('textarea');
  textarea.value = text;
  textarea.setAttribute('readonly', 'readonly');
  textarea.style.position = 'fixed';
  textarea.style.left = '-9999px';
  document.body.appendChild(textarea);
  textarea.select();
  try {
    document.execCommand('copy');
    showToast('success', successMessage);
  } catch (e) {
    showToast('error', '复制失败，请手动复制');
  }
  textarea.remove();
}

function copySupportInfo() {
  fetch('/api/support-info').then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
    const text = JSON.stringify(d, null, 2);
    copyText(text, '已复制脱敏支持信息，可直接发给技术支持');
  }).catch(e => showToast('error', '复制支持信息失败: ' + e.message));
}

function downloadSupportBundle() {
  showToast('info', '正在生成支持包...');
  fetch('/api/support-bundle', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({})
  }).then(async response => {
    if (!response.ok) {
      let message = '生成支持包失败';
      try {
        const data = await response.json();
        message = data.error || message;
      } catch (e) {}
      throw new Error(message);
    }
    const blob = await response.blob();
    const disposition = response.headers.get('Content-Disposition') || '';
    const match = disposition.match(/filename="?([^"]+)"?/i);
    const filename = match ? match[1] : 'support-bundle.zip';
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const link = document.createElement('a');
    link.href = url;
    link.download = filename;
    document.body.appendChild(link);
    link.click();
    link.remove();
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
    showToast('success', '支持包已生成，下载后发给技术支持');
  }).catch(e => showToast('error', e.message));
}

function openRuntimeFolder(kind) {
  fetch('/api/open-folder', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({ kind })
  }).then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
    if (d.error) return showToast('error', d.error);
    showToast('success', '已打开：' + (d.path || kind));
  }).catch(e => showToast('error', '打开失败: ' + e.message));
}

function saveGeneralConfig() {
  const nextLang = document.getElementById('cfgLang').value || 'zh';
  fetch('/api/config', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      output_dir: document.getElementById('cfgOutputDir').value,
      default_lang: nextLang,
      batch_limit: parseInt(document.getElementById('cfgBatchLimit').value) || 500,
      ai_concurrency: parseInt(document.getElementById('cfgConcurrency').value) || 3,
      image_concurrency: parseInt(document.getElementById('cfgImgConcurrency').value) || 2,
      media_store_enabled: document.getElementById('cfgMediaStoreEnabled').value === 'true',
      media_store_provider: document.getElementById('cfgMediaStoreProvider').value || 's3',
      media_s3_bucket: document.getElementById('cfgMediaS3Bucket').value,
      media_s3_region: document.getElementById('cfgMediaS3Region').value || 'us-east-1',
      media_s3_prefix: document.getElementById('cfgMediaS3Prefix').value || 'amazon28',
      media_s3_submit_scheme: document.getElementById('cfgMediaSubmitScheme').value || 's3',
      media_s3_preview_base: document.getElementById('cfgMediaPreviewBase').value,
    })
  }).then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
    if (!d.error) setLanguage(nextLang);
    showToast(d.error ? 'error' : 'success', d.error || '设置已保存');
    if (!d.error) refreshSetupStatus({ showFirstRun: false });
  }).catch(e => showToast('error', e.message));
}

function testConnection(kind = 'text') {
  const label = kind === 'image' ? '图片 AI' : '文字 AI';
  showToast('info', `正在测试${label}...`);
  fetch('/api/config/test', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({ kind })
  }).then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
    showToast(d.success ? 'success' : 'error', d.message || (d.success ? '连接成功' : '连接失败'));
  }).catch(e => showToast('error', e.message));
}

function testAccountConnection(sellerId) {
  showToast('info', '正在测试 Amazon 账号连接...');
  fetch('/api/accounts/test', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({ seller_id: sellerId })
  }).then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
    if (d.success) {
      showToast('success', d.message || '账号连接成功');
    } else {
      showToast('error', d.message || '账号连接失败');
    }
    showAccountTestResult(d);
    loadAccounts();
    refreshSetupStatus({ showFirstRun: false });
  }).catch(e => showToast('error', '测试失败: ' + e.message));
}

function formatAccountCheckStatus(status) {
  const value = String(status || '').toLowerCase();
  if (value === 'pass') return ['通过', 'success'];
  if (value === 'warn') return ['提醒', 'warning'];
  return ['失败', 'danger'];
}

function getAccountTestTone(result) {
  if (!result?.success) return 'danger';
  return result?.readiness === 'basic_ok' ? 'warning' : 'success';
}

function getAccountTestTitle(result) {
  if (!result?.success) return 'Amazon 账号测试失败';
  return result?.readiness === 'basic_ok' ? 'Amazon 账号基础连接通过' : 'Amazon 账号测试通过';
}

function showAccountTestResult(result) {
  const checks = Array.isArray(result?.checks) ? result.checks : [];
  const tone = getAccountTestTone(result);
  const summaryText = result?.readiness === 'basic_ok'
    ? '系统已确认 LWA Token 和站点基础通信正常；Listings 上架能力会在导入真实商品后的预览/提交阶段继续校验。'
    : '系统会分别检查：LWA Token、站点映射、Listings API、账号权限。失败时按红色项处理。';
  const checkHtml = checks.length > 0
    ? checks.map(check => {
        const [label, tone] = formatAccountCheckStatus(check.status);
        const code = check.code ? ` · ${escHtml(check.code)}` : '';
        return `<div class="account-test-check ${tone}">
          <span class="account-test-dot"></span>
          <div>
            <strong>${escHtml(check.label || check.name || '检测项')}</strong>
            <p>${escHtml(check.message || '')}${code}</p>
          </div>
          <em>${label}</em>
        </div>`;
      }).join('')
    : '<div class="task-empty">当前版本没有返回分项结果，请把弹窗截图发给客服。</div>';
  showModal(getAccountTestTitle(result), `
    <div class="account-test-summary ${tone}">
      <strong>${escHtml(result?.message || (result?.success ? '连接成功' : '连接失败'))}</strong>
      <p>${escHtml(summaryText)}</p>
    </div>
    <div class="account-test-checks">${checkHtml}</div>
  `);
  document.getElementById('modalFooter').innerHTML = `
    ${result?.success ? '' : '<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="closeModal(); showAddAccount()">重新填写账号</button>'}
    <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="closeModal()">关闭</button>`;
}

// ===== 24. Account Management =====
function loadAccounts() {
  fetch('/api/accounts').then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
    if (d.error) return showToast('error', d.error);
    const accounts = d.accounts || [];
    amazonAccounts = accounts.filter(account => account.enabled !== false);
    if (amazonAccounts.length === 0) {
      setSelectedAmazonAccount('');
    } else if (!selectedAccountId || !amazonAccounts.some(account => account.seller_id === selectedAccountId)) {
      const defaultAccount = amazonAccounts.find(account => account.is_default) || amazonAccounts[0];
      setSelectedAmazonAccount(defaultAccount ? defaultAccount.seller_id : '');
    }
    const tbody = document.getElementById('accountBody');
    if (accounts.length === 0) {
      tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="5" style="text-align:center;color:var(--text-muted);padding:20px">暂无账号</td></tr>';
      return;
    }
    tbody.innerHTML = accounts.map(a => {
      const lastReadiness = String(a.last_test_readiness || '').trim();
      const lastTestBadgeClass = !a.last_test_success ? 'badge-danger' : (lastReadiness === 'basic_ok' ? 'badge-warning' : 'badge-success');
      const lastTestLabel = !a.last_test_success ? '失败' : (lastReadiness === 'basic_ok' ? '基础通过' : '通过');
      const lastTest = a.last_test_at
        ? `<span class="badge ${lastTestBadgeClass}" title="${escHtml(a.last_test_message || '')}">上次测试${lastTestLabel}</span>`
        : '<span class="badge badge-default">未测试</span>';
      return `<tr>
      <td>${escHtml(a.name)}</td>
      <td>${escHtml(a.seller_id)}</td>
      <td>${escHtml(a.marketplace_name || a.marketplace_id || '-')}</td>
      <td>${[
        a.is_default ? '<span class="badge badge-success">默认</span>' : '',
        a.enabled === false ? '<span class="badge badge-danger">停用</span>' : '<span class="badge badge-default">启用</span>',
        a.has_credentials === false ? '<span class="badge badge-warning">缺少凭证</span>' : '<span class="badge badge-success">凭证完整</span>',
        lastTest
      ].filter(Boolean).join(' ')}</td>
      <td>
        <button class="btn-link" onclick="testAccountConnection('${escHtml(a.seller_id)}')">测试</button> |
        ${!a.is_default && a.enabled !== false ? `<button class="btn-link" onclick="setDefaultAccount('${escHtml(a.seller_id)}')">设为默认</button> | ` : ''}
        <button class="btn-danger-link" onclick="deleteAccount('${escHtml(a.seller_id)}')">删除</button>
      </td>
    </tr>`;
    }).join('');
    updateWorkspaceContext();
  }).catch(() => {});
}

function showAddAccount() {
  document.getElementById('modalTitle').textContent = '添加亚马逊账号';
  document.getElementById('modalBody').innerHTML = `
    <div class="account-help-box" style="margin-bottom:12px;">
      <strong>客户照着填，不要猜</strong>
      <span>账号名称：随便起，例如“美国站主账号”。</span>
      <span>Seller ID：Seller Central 后台里的卖家 ID / Merchant Token。</span>
      <span>LWA Client ID / Secret：Developer Console 的 SP-API 应用凭证。</span>
      <span>Refresh Token：授权后得到的长 token，通常以 <code>Atzr|</code> 开头。</span>
    </div>
    <div class="settings-grid">
      <div class="form-group"><label>账号名称</label><input type="text" id="newAccName" placeholder="如: 主账号-美国站"><div class="field-help">给客户自己看的名字，不影响提交。</div></div>
      <div class="form-group"><label>Seller ID${tipFor('seller_id')}</label><input type="text" id="newAccSellerId" placeholder="A1B2C3D4E5F6G7"><div class="field-help">不要填店铺名，填 Seller ID / Merchant Token。</div></div>
      <div class="form-group"><label>站点${tipFor('marketplace_id')}</label><select id="newAccMarket">
        <option value="US">🇺🇸 US</option><option value="CA">🇨🇦 CA</option><option value="MX">🇲🇽 MX</option>
        <option value="UK">🇬🇧 UK</option><option value="DE">🇩🇪 DE</option><option value="FR">🇫🇷 FR</option>
        <option value="JP">🇯🇵 JP</option><option value="AU">🇦🇺 AU</option>
      </select><div class="field-help">美国站选 US；加拿大/墨西哥按实际店铺选。</div></div>
      <div class="form-group"><label>LWA Client ID${tipFor('lwa_client_id')}</label><input type="text" id="newAccClientId" placeholder="amzn1.application-oa2-client.xxx"><div class="field-help">一般以 amzn1.application-oa2-client 开头。</div></div>
      <div class="form-group"><label>LWA Client Secret${tipFor('lwa_client_secret')}</label><input type="password" id="newAccClientSecret" placeholder="Client Secret"><div class="field-help">和 Client ID 同一应用里的 Secret，注意不要多复制空格。</div></div>
      <div class="form-group"><label>Refresh Token${tipFor('refresh_token')}</label><input type="password" id="newAccRefreshToken" placeholder="Atzr|xxx"><div class="field-help">通常以 Atzr| 开头，是授权后得到的刷新令牌。</div></div>
    </div>
    <p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-top:8px;">
      以上凭证从 Amazon Seller Central 和 Developer Console 获取：
      <a href="https://sellercentral.amazon.com" target="_blank" style="color:var(--primary);">打开 Seller Central</a> ·
      <a href="https://developer.amazonservices.com/signin" target="_blank" style="color:var(--primary);">打开 Developer Console</a> ·
      <a href="https://developer-docs.amazon.com/sp-api/docs/connecting-to-the-selling-partner-api" target="_blank" style="color:var(--primary);">查看 SP-API 文档</a>
    </p>`;
  document.getElementById('modalFooter').innerHTML = `
    <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="closeModal()">取消</button>
    <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="addAccount()">添加</button>`;
  document.getElementById('modal').classList.add('show');
}

function addAccount() {
  const name = document.getElementById('newAccName').value;
  const seller_id = document.getElementById('newAccSellerId').value;
  const marketSelect = document.getElementById('newAccMarket');
  const marketplace = marketSelect.value;
  const marketplaceName = (marketSelect.options[marketSelect.selectedIndex] || {}).textContent || marketplace;
  const lwa_client_id = document.getElementById('newAccClientId').value;
  const lwa_client_secret = document.getElementById('newAccClientSecret').value;
  const refresh_token = document.getElementById('newAccRefreshToken').value;

  if (!name || !seller_id) return showToast('warning', '请填写账号名称和Seller ID');
  if (!lwa_client_id || !lwa_client_secret || !refresh_token) return showToast('warning', '请填写LWA凭证（Client ID、Client Secret、Refresh Token）');
  if (!/^amzn1\.application-oa2-client\./i.test(lwa_client_id.trim())) {
    return showToast('warning', 'LWA Client ID 通常以 amzn1.application-oa2-client. 开头，请检查是不是填错了');
  }
  if (!/^Atzr\|/i.test(refresh_token.trim())) {
    return showToast('warning', 'Refresh Token 通常以 Atzr| 开头，请检查是不是复制错了');
  }

  const mpIds = {US:'ATVPDKIKX0DER',CA:'A2EUQ1WTGCTBG2',MX:'A1AM78C64UM0Y8',UK:'A1F83G8C2ARO7P',DE:'A1PA6795UKMFR9',FR:'A13V1IB3VIYZZH',JP:'A1VC38T7YXB528',AU:'A39IBJ37TRP1C6'};

  fetch('/api/accounts', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      name,
      seller_id,
      marketplace_id: mpIds[marketplace] || 'ATVPDKIKX0DER',
      marketplace_name: marketplaceName.trim(),
      lwa_client_id,
      lwa_client_secret,
      refresh_token,
      enabled: true,
    })
  }).then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
    closeModal();
    loadAccounts();
    refreshSetupStatus({ showFirstRun: false });
    showToast(d.error ? 'error' : 'success', d.error || '账号已添加');
  }).catch(e => showToast('error', e.message));
}
function setDefaultAccount(sellerId) {
  fetch('/api/accounts/default', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({ seller_id: sellerId })
  }).then(r => r.json()).then(() => { loadAccounts(); refreshSetupStatus({ showFirstRun: false }); })
    .catch(e => showToast('error', e.message));
}

function deleteAccount(sellerId) {
  document.getElementById('modalTitle').textContent = t('delete_confirm');
  document.getElementById('modalBody').innerHTML = `<p>${t('delete_confirm')}</p>`;
  document.getElementById('modalFooter').innerHTML = `
    <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="closeModal()">${t('cancel')}</button>
    <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="doDeleteAccount('${escHtml(sellerId)}')">${t('delete')}</button>`;
  document.getElementById('modal').classList.add('show');
}
function doDeleteAccount(sellerId) {
  closeModal();
  fetch('/api/accounts', {
    method: 'DELETE',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({ seller_id: sellerId })
  }).then(() => { loadAccounts(); refreshSetupStatus({ showFirstRun: false }); })
    .catch(e => showToast('error', e.message));
}

// ===== 25. UI Helpers =====
function customerFriendlyMessage(msg) {
  const text = String(msg || '');
  if (!text) return '';
  if (text.includes('EXCEL_LOCKED') || /Permission denied|另一个程序|being used by another process|文件.*占用|Excel.*占用|WPS.*占用/i.test(text)) {
    return 'Excel 文件被打开/占用：请先关闭 Excel/WPS 里的这个表格，再重新点击。错误码：EXCEL_LOCKED';
  }
  if (text.includes('AI_BASE_BAD')) {
    return 'AI 接口域名不正确：请点“一键恢复推荐”，Base URL 固定用 https://api.kk666.best。错误码：AI_BASE_BAD';
  }
  if (text.includes('FILE_VERSION_CONFLICT')) {
    return '这个 Excel 已被另一个窗口或任务改动：请先刷新商品表，再重新保存，避免互相覆盖。错误码：FILE_VERSION_CONFLICT';
  }
  if (text.includes('AMAZON_ACCOUNT_BAD')) {
    return 'Amazon 账号信息格式不完整：请按示例重新填写 Seller ID、LWA 和 Refresh Token。错误码：AMAZON_ACCOUNT_BAD';
  }
  return text;
}

function showToast(type, msg) {
  const c = document.getElementById('toastContainer');
  const t = document.createElement('div');
  t.className = 'toast toast-' + type;
  t.textContent = type === 'error' ? customerFriendlyMessage(msg) : String(msg || '');
  c.appendChild(t);
  setTimeout(() => t.remove(), 4000);
}

function showSubmitSuccessToast(result) {
  const c = document.getElementById('toastContainer');
  const t = document.createElement('div');
  t.className = 'toast toast-submit-success';
  const submissionId = compactMiddle(result.submission_id || result.submissionId || '', 10, 8) || '未返回';
  const routeText = formatSubmissionRoute(result.submission_route || 'unknown');
  const accountMeta = result.account || result.marketplace_name
    ? { name: result.account || '', site: result.marketplace_name || '' }
    : getAccountMeta(selectedAccountId || '');
  const lines = [
    '提交流程已发送给 Amazon',
    `SKU：${result.sku || '-'}`,
    `状态：${formatSubmitStatusLabel(result.status || '')}`,
    accountMeta ? `账号 / 站点：${accountMeta.name || '-'} / ${accountMeta.site || '-'}` : '',
    `提交ID：${submissionId}`,
    `路线：${routeText}`,
  ].filter(Boolean);
  t.textContent = lines.join('\n');
  c.appendChild(t);
  setTimeout(() => t.remove(), 12000);
}

function showModal(title, body) {
  document.getElementById('modalTitle').textContent = title;
  document.getElementById('modalBody').innerHTML = body;
  document.getElementById('modalFooter').innerHTML = '<button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="closeModal()">关闭</button>';
  document.getElementById('modal').classList.add('show');
}

// Amazon SP-API 8 字段傻瓜级图文教程
// 教用户从零拿到 Seller ID / Marketplace / LWA Client ID/Secret / Refresh Token
function showAmazonCredsTutorial() {
  const body = `

      <div class="amz-tutorial-step" data-step="2">
        <label class="amz-step-check"><input type="checkbox" onchange="toggleAmzStep(this,2)"> <span class="amz-step-num">2</span> <strong>拿到 Seller ID</strong>（最简单的一个）</label>
        <div class="amz-step-body">

        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="amz-tutorial-step" data-step="3">
        <label class="amz-step-check"><input type="checkbox" onchange="toggleAmzStep(this,3)"> <span class="amz-step-num">3</span> <strong>注册"开发者应用"拿到 Client ID 和 Client Secret</strong></label>
        <div class="amz-step-body">
          后台顶部菜单 <strong>合作伙伴网络（Partner Network）→ 开发者中心（Develop apps for amazon）</strong>。<br>
          首次进入会让你<strong>注册成开发者</strong>（Become a Developer），按提示填公司信息+用途说明（用途填"自用上架工具"即可），1-2 个工作日内审批通过。<br>
          通过后回到开发者中心：
          <ol class="amz-step-ol">
            <li>点 <strong>Add new app client（添加应用）</strong></li>
            <li>App name 随便填，比如 <code>my-listing-tool</code></li>
            <li>API Type 选 <strong>SP API</strong>；Roles 勾上 <strong>Product Listing</strong>、<strong>Inventory and Order Tracking</strong> 这两个</li>
            <li>提交后会得到一对：</li>
          </ol>
          <div class="amz-step-find">
            <strong>LWA credentials</strong>：<br>
            • <code>Client identifier</code> → 后面填到 <strong>LWA Client ID</strong>（以 <code>amzn1.application-oa2-client.</code> 开头）<br>
            • <code>Client secret</code> → 后面填到 <strong>LWA Client Secret</strong>（点"View"才显示，<strong>只显示一次</strong>，立刻复制）
          </div>
          <div class="amz-step-tip">⚠️ Client Secret 一定要在创建后立刻复制保存，关掉就再也看不到了，要重新生成。</div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="amz-tutorial-step" data-step="4">
        <label class="amz-step-check"><input type="checkbox" onchange="toggleAmzStep(this,4)"> <span class="amz-step-num">4</span> <strong>给应用做"自我授权"拿到 Refresh Token</strong></label>
        <div class="amz-step-body">
          回到开发者中心，找到刚才创建的应用：
          <ol class="amz-step-ol">
            <li>点应用右边的 <strong>Edit App（编辑应用）→ 下方 OAuth 设置</strong>，把状态改成 <strong>Draft</strong>（草稿）即可（不需要发布）</li>
            <li>回到应用列表，点应用名旁边的 <strong>… 三个点 → Authorize（授权）</strong></li>
            <li>页面会提示"授权给自己的卖家账号"，点 <strong>Authorize App（授权）</strong></li>
            <li>跳转的浏览器地址栏里会出现一长串字符，找到 <code>spapi_oauth_code=ANXXxxxx...</code></li>
            <li>系统会显示一段 <strong>refresh_token</strong>（以 <code>Atzr|</code> 开头，几百个字符），<strong>立刻全选复制</strong></li>
          </ol>
          <div class="amz-step-tip">💡 这个长 Token 永久有效，但只在授权完成那一瞬间显示，关掉浏览器就丢了。</div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="amz-tutorial-step" data-step="5">
        <label class="amz-step-check"><input type="checkbox" onchange="toggleAmzStep(this,5)"> <span class="amz-step-num">5</span> <strong>把 4 个值填到下面"添加账号"弹窗</strong></label>
        <div class="amz-step-body">
          关掉这个教程，点 <strong>右上角「添加」按钮</strong>，按下面对照填：
          <div class="amz-step-find amz-step-table">
            <div><strong>账号名称</strong> → 自己起，比如"美国站主账号"</div>
            <div><strong>Seller ID</strong> → 第 2 步拿到的 Merchant Token</div>
            <div><strong>站点</strong> → 选 🇺🇸 US（美国站）</div>
            <div><strong>LWA Client ID</strong> → 第 3 步的 Client identifier</div>
            <div><strong>LWA Client Secret</strong> → 第 3 步的 Client secret</div>
            <div><strong>Refresh Token</strong> → 第 4 步的 refresh_token</div>
          </div>
          填完点 <strong>「测试连接」</strong>，每一项都显示绿色对勾就成了。<br>
          有红色 ❌ 的话，对照下面常见错误自查：
          <div class="amz-step-faq">
            <div>❌ <strong>"凭证不完整"</strong> → 4 个字段哪个还空着？或多复制了空格？</div>
            <div>❌ <strong>"LWA token 失效"</strong> → Refresh Token 可能复制错或已过期，回第 4 步重新授权一次</div>
            <div>❌ <strong>"Listings API 拒绝"</strong> → 应用 Roles 没勾对，回第 3 步重新编辑应用，把 Product Listing 加上</div>
            <div>❌ <strong>"无法连接 amazon.com"</strong> → 公司网防火墙拦了，去 <strong>设置 → API配置</strong> 顶部"还没有 Key？"卡片下方设置代理</div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="amz-tutorial-foot">
        <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="closeModal(); showAddAccount();">5 步都做完了，去填账号 →</button>
        <button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="showVendorQr()">卡住了，找客服</button>
        <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="closeModal()">关闭教程</button>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  document.getElementById('modalTitle').textContent = '亚马逊凭证 5 步获取教程';
  document.getElementById('modalBody').innerHTML = body;
  document.getElementById('modalFooter').innerHTML = '';
  document.getElementById('modal').classList.add('show');
}

function toggleAmzStep(checkbox, stepNum) {
  const step = checkbox.closest('.amz-tutorial-step');
  if (step) step.classList.toggle('done', checkbox.checked);
}

// 客服二维码弹窗（傻瓜买 Key 入口）
// ★★★ 售后请把 /static/img/vendor-qr.png 替换成你们自己的客服微信二维码图 ★★★
function showVendorQr() {
  const body = `
    <div style="text-align:center; padding:8px 0;">
      <p style="margin:0 0 12px; color:#374151; font-size:14px;">手机微信打开「扫一扫」，对准下面的二维码加客服好友</p>
      <img src="/static/img/vendor-qr.png" alt="客服微信二维码"
           style="width:240px; height:240px; border:1px solid #e5e7eb; border-radius:8px; object-fit:contain; background:#f9fafb;"
           onerror="this.style.display='none'; this.nextElementSibling.style.display='block';">
      <div style="display:none; padding:60px 20px; color:#6b7280; background:#f9fafb; border:1px dashed #d1d5db; border-radius:8px;">
        二维码图片还没配置。<br>请售后把客服二维码放到 <code>web/static/img/vendor-qr.png</code>。
      </div>
      <p style="margin:14px 0 0; color:#6b7280; font-size:12px;">扫码后告诉客服「我要买 AI Key 用于亚马逊上架工具」即可</p>
    </div>`;
  showModal('客服微信二维码', body);
}
function closeModal() {
  pendingSubmitPayload = null;
  document.getElementById('modal').classList.remove('show');
}

function showProgress(title, done, total) {
  const options = arguments[3] || {};
  document.getElementById('progressTitle').textContent = title;
  updateProgress(done, total, '');
  const cancelBtn = document.getElementById('progressCancelBtn');
  if (cancelBtn) {
    const cancelable = options.cancelable !== false;
    cancelBtn.style.display = cancelable ? '' : 'none';
    cancelBtn.textContent = options.buttonText || t('cancel_process');
  }
  document.getElementById('progressOverlay').classList.add('show');
}
function updateProgress(done, total, item) {
  const pct = total > 0 ? Math.round(done / total * 100) : 0;
  document.getElementById('progressFill').style.width = pct + '%';
  document.getElementById('progressText').textContent = done + ' / ' + total;
  document.getElementById('progressItem').textContent = item ? '当前: ' + item : '';
}
function hideProgress() { document.getElementById('progressOverlay').classList.remove('show'); }

function toggleDropdown(id) {
  const menu = document.getElementById(id);
  const wasOpen = menu.classList.contains('show');
  closeAllDropdowns();
  if (!wasOpen) menu.classList.add('show');
}
function closeAllDropdowns() {
  document.querySelectorAll('.dropdown-menu').forEach(m => m.classList.remove('show'));
  document.getElementById('colSettingsPanel').classList.remove('show');
}

async function loadTaskCenter() {
  try {
    const response = await fetch('/api/tasks');
    const data = await response.json();
    taskCenterData = data || { current: null, history: [] };
    renderTaskCenter();
    renderRecentSubmitBanner();
    loadSubmissionHistory();
  } catch (e) {}
}

async function loadSubmissionHistory() {
  const el = document.getElementById('submissionHistory');
  if (!el) return;
  try {
    const response = await fetch('/api/submission-history');
    const data = await response.json();
    const records = (data.records || []).slice(0, 8);
    if (records.length === 0) {
      el.innerHTML = '<div class="task-empty">暂无提交记录</div>';
      return;
    }
    el.innerHTML = records.map(rec => {
      const accepted = rec.accepted || rec.success || 0;
      const failed = rec.failed || 0;
      const total = rec.total || 0;
      const status = failed === 0 && accepted > 0 ? 'success' : (accepted === 0 ? 'danger' : 'warn');
      const time = (rec.timestamp || rec.time || '').replace('T', ' ').substring(0, 19);
      return `<div class="task-card">
        <div class="task-card-head">
          <strong>${escHtml(rec.account || '未知账号')}</strong>
          <span class="task-badge ${status}">${accepted}/${total}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="task-card-meta">${escHtml(time)}</div>
        <div class="task-card-progress">成功 ${accepted} · 失败 ${failed}${rec.file ? ` · ${escHtml(String(rec.file).split('/').pop())}` : ''}</div>
      </div>`;
    }).join('');
  } catch (e) {
    el.innerHTML = '<div class="task-empty">加载提交历史失败</div>';
  }
}

function formatTaskStatus(status) {
  const map = {
    running: ['运行中', 'processing'],
    completed: ['已完成', 'success'],
    failed: ['失败', 'danger'],
    cancelled: ['已取消', 'warn'],
    pass: ['通过', 'success'],
    warn: ['提示', 'warn'],
    fail: ['失败', 'danger'],
  };
  return map[status] || ['待处理', 'default'];
}

function buildTaskFactPills(task) {
  const result = task && typeof task.result === 'object' ? task.result : {};
  const first = Array.isArray(result.results) && result.results.length > 0 ? result.results[0] : null;
  const facts = [];
  const accountName = result.account || task.account || '';
  const siteName = first && first.marketplace_name ? first.marketplace_name : (task.marketplace || result.marketplace || '');
  const route = first && first.submission_route ? formatSubmissionRoute(first.submission_route) : '';
  const submissionId = first && (first.submission_id || first.submissionId) ? compactMiddle(first.submission_id || first.submissionId, 10, 8) : '';

  if (accountName) facts.push(`<span class="task-card-fact info">账号：<strong>${escHtml(accountName)}</strong></span>`);
  if (siteName) facts.push(`<span class="task-card-fact info">站点：<strong>${escHtml(siteName)}</strong></span>`);
  if (route) facts.push(`<span class="task-card-fact warn">路线：<strong>${escHtml(route)}</strong></span>`);
  if (submissionId) facts.push(`<span class="task-card-fact success">提交ID：<strong>${escHtml(submissionId)}</strong></span>`);

  return facts.length > 0 ? `<div class="task-card-facts">${facts.join('')}</div>` : '';
}

function getLatestCompletedSubmitTask() {
  const history = Array.isArray(taskCenterData.history) ? taskCenterData.history : [];
  return history.find(task => task && task.kind === 'submit' && task.status === 'completed') || null;
}

function resolveTaskAccountId(task) {
  const result = task && typeof task.result === 'object' ? task.result : {};
  const exactId = String(result.account_id || task.account_id || task.account || '').trim();
  if (!exactId) return '';
  const account = amazonAccounts.find(item => item && item.seller_id === exactId) || null;
  return account ? (account.seller_id || '') : '';
}

async function openTaskDetail(taskId) {
  if (!taskId) return;
  try {
    const response = await fetch('/api/tasks/' + encodeURIComponent(taskId));
    const task = await response.json();
    if (task.error) return showToast('error', task.error);
    const result = task && typeof task.result === 'object' ? task.result : {};
    const rows = Array.isArray(result.results) ? result.results : [];
    const issueRows = rows.map(row => {
      const issues = (row.issues || []).map(issue => {
        const message = typeof issue === 'string' ? issue : (issue.message || '');
        return `<div class="result-issue-item"><div class="result-issue-primary">${escHtml(message || '-')}</div></div>`;
      }).join('') || '<div class="result-issue-item"><div class="result-issue-primary">无</div></div>';
      return `<div style="padding:10px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--line);">
        <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;gap:12px;align-items:center;">
          <strong>${escHtml(row.sku || '-')}</strong>
          <span>${escHtml(formatSubmitStatusLabel(row.status || task.status || ''))}</span>
        </div>
        <div style="margin-top:6px;font-size:12px;color:var(--text-secondary);">
          路线：${escHtml(formatSubmissionRoute(row.submission_route || 'unknown'))}
          ${row.submission_id ? ` · 提交ID：${escHtml(compactMiddle(row.submission_id, 10, 8))}` : ''}
          ${row.asin ? ` · ASIN：${escHtml(row.asin)}` : ''}
        </div>
        <div style="margin-top:8px;">${issues}</div>
      </div>`;
    }).join('');

    showModal(task.title || '任务详情', `
      <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:12px;">
        <div class="preflight-tags">
          <span class="preflight-tag info">状态：${escHtml(formatTaskStatus(task.status || 'default')[0])}</span>
          <span class="preflight-tag info">文件：${escHtml(task.file_name || '-')}</span>
          ${result.account ? `<span class="preflight-tag info">账号：${escHtml(result.account)}</span>` : ''}
          ${result.marketplace ? `<span class="preflight-tag info">站点：${escHtml(result.marketplace)}</span>` : ''}
        </div>
        <div class="preflight-note">${escHtml(result.message || task.message || '暂无任务摘要')}</div>
        <div style="max-height:46vh;overflow:auto;">${issueRows || '<div class="preflight-empty">暂无明细结果</div>'}</div>
      </div>
    `);
  } catch (e) {
    showToast('error', '加载任务详情失败: ' + e.message);
  }
}

async function openRecentSubmitListingStatus() {
  const task = getLatestCompletedSubmitTask();
  if (!task) return showToast('warning', '最近没有可查看的提交记录');
  const result = task && typeof task.result === 'object' ? task.result : {};
  const first = Array.isArray(result.results) && result.results.length > 0 ? result.results[0] : null;
  if (!first || !first.sku) return showToast('warning', '最近一次提交缺少 SKU');

  const originalAccountId = selectedAccountId;
  const accountId = resolveTaskAccountId(task);
  if (!accountId) return showToast('warning', '这条历史提交没有保存明确账号，请重新选择账号后再查最终状态');
  selectedAccountId = accountId;
  try {
    const listing = await fetchListingStatusFor(task.input_file || currentFile, first.sku, accountId);
    showModal('Amazon 最终状态', `
      <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:12px;">
        <div class="preflight-tags">
          <span class="preflight-tag info">SKU：${escHtml(first.sku)}</span>
          <span class="preflight-tag info">状态：${escHtml(formatFinalListingStatus(listing.final_status || '') || '待判定')}</span>
          ${listing.asin ? `<span class="preflight-tag info">ASIN：${escHtml(listing.asin)}</span>` : ''}
          <span class="preflight-tag info">路线：${escHtml(formatSubmissionRoute(listing.route || first.submission_route || 'unknown'))}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="preflight-note">${escHtml(listing.discoverable ? '当前 listing 已进入 DISCOVERABLE。' : '当前还未进入可发现状态，继续观察 Amazon 后台状态。')}</div>
        <div style="font-size:12px;line-height:1.7;color:var(--text-secondary);">
          报价组：${escHtml(String(listing.offer_count || 0))} · 库存组：${escHtml(String(listing.fulfillment_count || 0))} · 后台问题：${escHtml(String(listing.issue_count || 0))}
        </div>
      </div>
    `);
  } catch (e) {
    showToast('error', '查询 Amazon 最终状态失败: ' + e.message);
  } finally {
    selectedAccountId = originalAccountId;
  }
}

function renderRecentSubmitBanner() {
  const banner = document.getElementById('submitResultBanner');
  if (!banner) return;
  const task = getLatestCompletedSubmitTask();
  if (!task) {
    banner.classList.add('hidden');
    banner.innerHTML = '';
    return;
  }

  const result = task && typeof task.result === 'object' ? task.result : {};
  const first = Array.isArray(result.results) && result.results.length > 0 ? result.results[0] : null;
  const route = first && first.submission_route ? formatSubmissionRoute(first.submission_route) : '待判定';
  const status = first ? formatSubmitStatusLabel(first.status || '') : '已完成';
  const submissionId = first && (first.submission_id || first.submissionId)
    ? compactMiddle(first.submission_id || first.submissionId, 10, 8)
    : '未返回';
  const account = result.account || task.account || '未记录';
  const marketplace = result.marketplace || task.marketplace || '未记录';
  const sku = first && first.sku ? first.sku : '-';
  const message = result.message || task.message || '最近一次提交流程已完成';

  banner.classList.remove('hidden');
  banner.innerHTML = `<div class="submit-result-main">
    <div class="submit-result-label">最近一次提交结果</div>
    <div class="submit-result-title">${escHtml(message)}</div>
    <div class="submit-result-summary">${escHtml(task.file_name || '')}${task.started_at ? ` · ${escHtml(task.started_at.replace('T', ' '))}` : ''}</div>
    <div class="submit-result-facts">
      <span class="submit-result-pill">SKU：${escHtml(sku)}</span>
      <span class="submit-result-pill">状态：${escHtml(status)}</span>
      <span class="submit-result-pill">账号：${escHtml(account)}</span>
      <span class="submit-result-pill">站点：${escHtml(marketplace)}</span>
      <span class="submit-result-pill">路线：${escHtml(route)}</span>
      <span class="submit-result-pill">提交ID：${escHtml(submissionId)}</span>
    </div>
  </div>
  <div class="submit-result-actions">
    <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="openRecentSubmitListingStatus()">查看 Amazon 最终状态</button>
    <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="openTaskDetail('${escHtml(task.id || '')}')">查看提交详情</button>
    <button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="document.getElementById('taskCenterGrid').classList.remove('collapsed'); window.scrollTo({ top: document.getElementById('taskCenterGrid').getBoundingClientRect().top + window.scrollY - 80, behavior: 'smooth' });">查看任务记录</button>
  </div>`;
}

function renderTaskCenter() {
  const currentEl = document.getElementById('taskCurrent');
  const historyEl = document.getElementById('taskHistory');
  if (!currentEl || !historyEl) return;

  const current = taskCenterData.current;
  if (current && current.status === 'running' && taskCenterCollapsed) {
    setTaskCenterCollapsed(false);
  }
  if (current && current.status === 'running') {
    const [label, tone] = formatTaskStatus(current.status);
    const progress = current.total > 0 ? `${current.progress || 0}/${current.total}` : '进行中';
    const stage = current.stage_name ? ` · ${current.stage_name}` : '';
    currentEl.innerHTML = `<div class="task-card active">
      <div class="task-card-head">
        <strong>${escHtml(current.title || '当前任务')}</strong>
        <span class="task-badge ${tone}">${label}</span>
      </div>
      <div class="task-card-meta">${escHtml(current.file_name || '')}</div>
      <div class="task-card-progress">${progress}${stage}${current.current_item ? ` · ${escHtml(current.current_item)}` : ''}</div>
      ${buildTaskFactPills(current)}
    </div>`;
  } else {
    currentEl.innerHTML = '<div class="task-empty">当前没有正在运行的批量任务</div>';
  }

  const history = (taskCenterData.history || []).slice(0, 8);
  if (history.length > 0) {
    rememberRecentSubmitResult(history[0], { toast: false });
  }
  if (history.length === 0) {
    historyEl.innerHTML = '<div class="task-empty">最近暂无任务记录</div>';
    return;
  }

  historyEl.innerHTML = history.map(task => {
    const [label, tone] = formatTaskStatus(task.status);
    const progress = task.total > 0 ? `${task.progress || task.success || 0}/${task.total}` : '';
    const detail = [task.stage_name || '', task.message || task.current_item || ''].filter(Boolean).join(' · ');
    return `<div class="task-card">
      <div class="task-card-head">
        <strong>${escHtml(task.title || task.kind || '任务')}</strong>
        <span class="task-badge ${tone}">${label}</span>
      </div>
      <div class="task-card-meta">${escHtml(task.file_name || '')}${task.started_at ? ` · ${escHtml(task.started_at.replace('T', ' '))}` : ''}</div>
      <div class="task-card-progress">${escHtml(progress)}${detail ? ` · ${escHtml(detail)}` : ''}</div>
      ${buildTaskFactPills(task)}
      <div class="task-card-actions">
        <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="openTaskDetail('${escHtml(task.id || '')}')">查看详情</button>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

async function runSelfCheck() {
  const container = document.getElementById('selfCheckResults');
  if (container) container.innerHTML = '<div class="task-empty">正在执行环境自检，请稍候...</div>';
  try {
    const response = await fetch('/api/self-check', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ account_id: selectedAccountId || '' }),
    });
    const data = await response.json();
    const checks = data.checks || [];
    if (!container) return;
    const actionForCheck = (check) => {
      const name = String(check.name || '');
      if (['ai_base_url', 'text_ai', 'image_ai'].includes(name)) {
        return `<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="showSettingsSection('ai'); setAiConfigMode('simple'); resetRecommendedAiConfig(); scrollToElementLater('#cfgTextApiKey')">修复 AI 配置</button>`;
      }
      if (name === 'amazon_account') {
        return '<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="showSettingsSection(\'amazon\'); showAddAccount()">添加/修复账号</button>';
      }
      if (name === 'output_dir') {
        return `<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="openRuntimeFolder('output')">打开输出目录</button>`;
      }
      if (name === 'media_store') {
        return `<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="showSettingsSection('advanced'); scrollToElementLater('#cfgMediaStoreEnabled')">检查媒体存储</button>`;
      }
      return '';
    };
    container.innerHTML = checks.map(check => {
      const [label, tone] = formatTaskStatus(check.status);
      const actionHtml = check.status === 'pass' ? '' : actionForCheck(check);
      return `<div class="task-card">
        <div class="task-card-head">
          <strong>${escHtml(check.name)}</strong>
          <span class="task-badge ${tone}">${label}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="task-card-meta">${escHtml(check.message || '')}</div>
        ${check.detail ? `<div class="task-card-progress">${escHtml(check.detail)}</div>` : ''}
        ${actionHtml ? `<div class="task-card-actions">${actionHtml}</div>` : ''}
      </div>`;
    }).join('');
    showToast(data.status === 'fail' ? 'warning' : 'success', data.status === 'fail' ? '自检存在失败项，请按结果逐项修复' : '自检完成');
  } catch (e) {
    if (container) container.innerHTML = '<div class="task-empty">自检失败，请稍后重试</div>';
    showToast('error', '自检失败: ' + e.message);
  }
}

// ===== 26. Initialization =====
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  applyLang();
  initializeColumnVisibility();
  refreshTemplateFlowUi();
  loadConfig(true);
  fetchAccounts(true).then(() => updateWorkspaceContext()).catch(() => updateWorkspaceContext());
  refreshSetupStatus({ showFirstRun: true });
  loadSelectedFields();
  loadTaskCenter();
  // Close dropdowns on outside click
  document.addEventListener('click', e => {
    if (!e.target.closest('.dropdown') && !e.target.closest('.col-settings-panel') && !e.target.closest('[onclick*="toggleColumnSettings"]')) {
      closeAllDropdowns();
    }
  });
  // Escape to close drawer
  document.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
    if (e.key === 'Escape') {
      closeDrawer();
      closeModal();
      closeAllDropdowns();
      closeMobileSidebar();
    }
  });
  window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
    if (!isMobileViewport()) closeMobileSidebar();
  });
  ['cfgTextApiKey','cfgImageApiKey','cfgTextBaseUrl','cfgImageBaseUrl','cfgTextEndpoint','cfgImageEndpoint','cfgTextModel','cfgImageModel'].forEach(id => {
    document.getElementById(id)?.addEventListener('input', validateAiConfigFields);
  });
  document.getElementById('cfgTextModel')?.addEventListener('change', () => syncAiEndpointForModel('text'));
  document.getElementById('cfgImageModel')?.addEventListener('change', () => syncAiEndpointForModel('image'));
  window.setInterval(loadTaskCenter, 5000);
  // Load existing files — restore from localStorage if available
  if (currentFile) {
    const baseName = currentFile.split('/').pop();
    templatePanelCollapsed = true;
    currentFileMeta = { type: baseName.toLowerCase().endsWith('.xls') ? 'xls' : 'xlsx', warning: '', xlsPreserveSupported: false };
    document.getElementById('fileInfo').dataset.baseName = baseName;
    document.getElementById('fileInfo').textContent = baseName;
    loadProducts();
  }
  fetch('/api/files').then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
    const files = d.input || [];
    if (!currentFile && files.length > 0) {
      templatePanelCollapsed = true;
      currentFile = files[0].path || files[0].name;
      localStorage.setItem('amazon28_currentFile', currentFile);
      currentFileMeta = { type: (files[0].name || '').toLowerCase().endsWith('.xls') ? 'xls' : 'xlsx', warning: '', xlsPreserveSupported: false };
      document.getElementById('fileInfo').dataset.baseName = files[0].name;
      document.getElementById('fileInfo').textContent = files[0].name;
      loadProducts();
    } else if (!currentFile) {
      refreshTemplateFlowUi();
    }
  }).catch(() => {});
});
